{{Gaza genocide sidebar}}

The '''Gaza genocide''' is the ongoing,<ref>{{cite web |date=27 November 2025 |title=Israel's genocide against Palestinians 'not over' despite ceasefire - new Amnesty briefing |url=https://www.amnesty.org.uk/press-releases/israels-genocide-against-palestinians-not-over-despite-ceasefire-new-amnesty |access-date=4 January 2026 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251128172416/https://www.amnesty.org.uk/press-releases/israels-genocide-against-palestinians-not-over-despite-ceasefire-new-amnesty |archive-date=28 November 2025 |publisher=[[Amnesty International]] |url-status=live}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |date=28 November 2025 |last1=Segal |first1=Raz |author1-link=Raz Segal |title=The genocide in Gaza is far from over |url=https://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2025/nov/28/the-genocide-in-gaza-is-far-from-over |access-date=4 January 2026 |work=[[The Guardian]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251128115413/https://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2025/nov/28/the-genocide-in-gaza-is-far-from-over |archive-date=28 November 2025 |url-status=live |ref=none}}</ref> [[Intent and incitement in the Gaza genocide|intentional]], and systematic destruction of the [[Palestinians|Palestinian people]] in the [[Gaza Strip]] carried out by [[Israel]] during the [[Gaza war]]. It encompasses [[Mass killing|mass killings]], deliberate [[Gaza Strip famine|starvation]], infliction of serious bodily and mental harm, and [[Attacks on health facilities during the Gaza war#Attacks in the Gaza Strip|prevention of births]]. Other acts include [[Blockade of the Gaza Strip|blockading]], [[Attacks on protected zones and civilians in Gaza|destroying civilian infrastructure]], destroying [[Attacks on health facilities during the Gaza war|healthcare facilities]], killing [[Killing of health workers in the Gaza war|healthcare workers]] and [[2025 Gaza Strip aid distribution killings|aid-seekers]], causing mass [[Gaza Strip evacuations|forced displacement]], committing [[Sexual and gender-based violence against Palestinians during the Gaza war|sexual violence]], and destroying [[Attacks on schools during the Gaza war|educational]], [[Attacks on religious sites during the Israeli invasion of Gaza|religious]], and [[Destruction of cultural heritage during the Israeli invasion of the Gaza Strip|cultural sites]].<ref name="UNCommissionGenocide">{{Cite web |date=16 September 2025 |title=Israel has committed genocide in the Gaza Strip, UN Commission finds |url=https://www.ohchr.org/en/press-releases/2025/09/israel-has-committed-genocide-gaza-strip-un-commission-finds |access-date=21 September 2025 |website=[[Office of the United Nations High Commissioner for Human Rights]] |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250925113927/https://www.ohchr.org/en/press-releases/2025/09/israel-has-committed-genocide-gaza-strip-un-commission-finds |archive-date=25 September 2025}}</ref> The genocide has been recognised by [[Special Committee to Investigate Israeli Practices Affecting the Human Rights of the Palestinian People|a United Nations special committee]]<ref name="UNCommitteeHeadGenocide">{{cite speech |last=Pieris |first=Mohan |author-link=Mohan Peiris |date=19 November 2024 |title=A genocide is unfolding before our eyes: History will not forgive our inaction, UN Special Committee warns General Assembly 4th Committee report |url=https://www.ohchr.org/en/statements-and-speeches/2024/11/genocide-unfolding-our-eyes-history-will-not-forgive-our-inaction |access-date=9 April 2025 |publisher=[[Office of the United Nations High Commissioner for Human Rights]] |language=en-US |quote=Our findings conclude that Israel’s methods of war align with the characteristics of genocide ... Our report leaves no room for ambiguity. A genocide is unfolding before our eyes. Failing to act now—failing to put an end to this atrocity crime—will tear apart the very foundation of the international rule of law we have collectively built to protect peace, security, and the well-being of all. Our inaction today is setting a perilous precedent for tomorrow. Think about it. |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250414205459/https://www.ohchr.org/en/statements-and-speeches/2024/11/genocide-unfolding-our-eyes-history-will-not-forgive-our-inaction |archive-date=14 April 2025 |url-status=live}}</ref> and [[2025 UNHRC Commission of Inquiry report on Gaza genocide|commission of inquiry]],<ref name="UNCommissionGenocide" /> the [[International Association of Genocide Scholars]],<ref name="IAGSReuters">{{cite news |last=van den Berg |first=Stephanie |date=1 September 2025 |title=Israel is committing genocide in Gaza, scholars' association says |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/israel-is-committing-genocide-gaza-scholars-association-says-2025-09-01/ |access-date=1 September 2025 |work=[[Reuters]] |archive-url=https://archive.today/20250917195128/https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/israel-is-committing-genocide-gaza-scholars-association-says-2025-09-01/ |archive-date=17 September |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250902042359/https://genocidescholars.org/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/IAGS-Resolution-on-Gaza-FINAL.pdf |archive-date=2 September 2025}}</ref> [[List of humanitarian and human rights groups accusing Israel of genocide in Gaza|multiple human rights groups]],{{#tag:ref| [[Amnesty International]],<ref name="Amnesty_International_Dec_2024">{{harvnb|Amnesty International report|2024|p=13}}: "This report focuses on the Israeli authorities' policies and actions in Gaza as part of the military offensive they launched in the wake of the Hamas-led attacks on 7 October 2023 while situating them within the broader context of Israel's unlawful occupation, and system of apartheid against Palestinians in Gaza, the West Bank, including East Jerusalem, and Israel. It assesses allegations of violations and crimes under international law by Israel in Gaza within the framework of genocide under international law, concluding that there is sufficient evidence to believe that Israel's conduct in Gaza following 7 October 2023 amounts to genocide."</ref> [[Médecins Sans Frontières]],<ref>{{harvnb|Médecins Sans Frontières|2025}}: "Our decision to describe what's happening in Gaza as a 'genocide' is based on nearly two years of extensive, firsthand information from our teams, who are witnessing massive levels of death and destruction by Israeli forces, a campaign of ethnic cleansing and the almost total dismantling of the health care system."</ref> [[B'Tselem]],<ref>{{harvnb|B'Tselem|2025|p=86}}: "The review presented in this report leaves no room for doubt: since October 2023, the Israeli regime has been responsible for carrying out genocide against the Palestinians in the Gaza Strip. Killing tens of thousands of people; causing bodily or mental harm to hundreds of thousands more; destroying homes and civilian infrastructure on a massive scale; starvation, displacement, and denying humanitarian aid—all this is being perpetrated systematically, as part of a coordinated attack aimed at annihilating all facets of life in the Gaza Strip."</ref> [[Physicians for Human Rights–Israel]],<ref name="Kottasová & Salman"/> [[International Federation for Human Rights]].<ref name="FIDH 2023" />|group=lower-alpha}} numerous [[genocide studies]] and [[international law]] scholars,<ref name="growing_agreement">{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
| {{harvnb|Sultany|2024|p=4}} : "Although legal scholars and commentators were slow to recognize the severity and urgency of the situation, this article sought to show that there is an emerging consensus that Israel's actions in Gaza are not another instance of armed conflict but instead amount to genocide"
| {{harvnb|Swart|2025|p=3}}: "South Africa's actions led to an ever-growing consensus in international legal circles that Israel is committing genocide"
| {{harvnb|Lederman|2025|p=1}}: "Roughly since mid-2024, there seems to have emerged a broad agreement among genocide scholars—at least those who have expressed their views on the matter—that this is indeed the case ... What followed seems to be a similar broad agreement emerging among legal scholars that this is indeed a genocide, and even those who are still hesitating find the genocide charges much more convincing."
| {{harvnb|Shaw|2025b|p=3}}: "By the end of 2024, when Amnesty International published a comprehensively evidenced and legally argued case,17 the consensus that Israel was committing genocide was becoming overwhelming"
| {{harvnb|Gessen|2024}}: "Trachtenberg testified to a consensus opinion among historians of genocide that what is happening in Gaza can indeed be called a genocide, largely because the intent to cause death on a massive scale has been so clear in the statements of Israeli officials"
| {{harvnb|Bouranova|2024}}: "The opposition is political, as there is consensus amongst the international human rights legal community, many other legal and political experts, including many Holocaust scholars, that Israel is committing genocide in Gaza."

By December 2025, the [[Gaza Health Ministry]] had reported that at least 70,117 people in Gaza [[Casualties of the Gaza war|had been killed]].<ref>{{cite web |date=3 December 2025 |title=Reported impact snapshot – Gaza Strip (3 December 2025) |url=https://www.ochaopt.org/content/reported-impact-snapshot-gaza-strip-3-december-2025 |work=[[United Nations Office for the Coordination of Humanitarian Affairs|Office for the Coordination of Humanitarian Affairs]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251204205622/https://www.ochaopt.org/content/reported-impact-snapshot-gaza-strip-3-december-2025 |archive-date=4 December 2025}}</ref> The vast majority of the victims were civilians,{{sfn|Schwarz|2024}}{{sfn|Tantesh|Graham-Harrison|2024}} and around 50% were women and children.<ref name="Spagat 2024a">{{cite web |last=Spagat |first=Mike |date=28 May 2024 |title=Gaza Ministry of Health releases detailed new casualty data amidst confusion of UN's death numbers in Gaza |url=https://aoav.org.uk/2024/gaza-ministry-of-health-releases-detailed-new-casualty-amidst-confusion-of-uns-death-numbers-in-gaza/ |access-date=10 July 2024 |website=[[Action On Armed Violence]] |language=en-US |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240710190121/https://aoav.org.uk/2024/gaza-ministry-of-health-releases-detailed-new-casualty-amidst-confusion-of-uns-death-numbers-in-gaza/ |archive-date=10 July 2024}}</ref>{{sfn|Graham-Harrison|2024a}} Compared to other recent global conflicts, the numbers of known [[Killing of journalists in the Gaza war|deaths of journalists]], humanitarian and [[Killing of health workers in the Gaza war|health workers]], and [[Effect of the Gaza war on children in the Gaza Strip|children]] are among the highest.<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
| {{harvnb|Amnesty International report|2024|p=16}}
| {{harvnb|Buschek|Christoph|Kalisch|Kollig|2024}}
| {{cite web |date=10 October 2024 |title=Gaza: At Least 3,100 Children Aged Under Five Killed With Others at Risk as Famine Looms |url=https://www.savethechildren.net/news/gaza-least-3100-children-aged-under-five-killed-others-risk-famine-looms |website=[[Save the Children]] |access-date=21 December 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20241104093600/https://www.savethechildren.net/news/gaza-least-3100-children-aged-under-five-killed-others-risk-famine-looms |archive-date=4 November 2024}}
| {{harvnb|Salzenstein|2024}}
| {{harvnb|Fayyad|2024}}
}}</ref> Thousands more uncounted bodies are thought to be under the rubble of destroyed buildings.{{sfn|Tantesh|Graham-Harrison|2024}}{{sfn|Massoud|Fick|2023}} A study in the medical journal ''The Lancet'' estimated that traumatic injury deaths were undercounted by June 2024, while noting an even larger potential death toll when "indirect" deaths are included.<ref>{{harvnb|Jamaluddine|Abukmail|Aly|Campbell|2025}}: "We estimated 64,260 deaths (95% CI 55 298–78 525) due to traumatic injury during the study period, suggesting the Palestinian MoH under-reported mortality by 41%. ... Our findings underestimate the full impact of the military operation in Gaza, as they do not account for non-trauma-related deaths resulting from health service disruption, food insecurity, and inadequate water and sanitation."</ref> The number of injured is greater than 171,000.<ref name="snapshot" /><ref name="Burke 2025">{{cite news |last1=Burke |first1=Jason |date=27 August 2025 |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2025/aug/27/children-make-up-third-of-outpatients-in-msf-hospitals-in-gaza-statistics-show |work=[[The Guardian]] |title=A third of outpatients treated for wounds at MSF's Gaza hospitals in 2024 were children, figures show |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250915182357/https://www.theguardian.com/world/2025/aug/27/children-make-up-third-of-outpatients-in-msf-hospitals-in-gaza-statistics-show |archive-date=15 September 2025}}</ref>{{sfn|Gómez-Ugarte|Chen|Acosta|Basellini|2025|p=13}} Gaza has the most child [[Amputation|amputees]] per capita in the world;<ref name="Amputee stats" /> the Gaza war caused more than 21,000 children to be [[Physical disability|disabled]].<ref name="Guardian_3_September_2025">{{cite news |date=3 September 2025 |title=Middle East crisis: at least 21,000 children disabled in Gaza during war, says UN committee – as it happened |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/live/2025/sep/03/gaza-graveyard-international-humanitarian-law-unrwa-israel-middle-east-crisis-latest-updates-news |work=[[The Guardian]] |access-date=7 September 2025 |archive-url= |archive-date=}}</ref>

An [[Israeli blockade of the Gaza Strip (2023–present)|Israeli blockade]] heavily contributed to [[Gaza Strip famine|starvation and confirmed famine]]. As of August 2025, projections show about 641,000 people experiencing [[Integrated Food Security Phase Classification|catastrophic levels]] and that "the number of people facing emergency levels will likely increase to 1.14 million".{{sfn|IPC Report August|2025|p=1}}<ref>{{cite news |date=23 August 2025 |first=Mary |last=Kekatos |title=Famine determined in parts of Gaza, 500,000 experiencing 'catastrophic' hunger: Report |url=https://abcnews.go.com/International/famine-determined-parts-gaza-500000-experiencing-catastrophic-hunger/story?id=124843218 |work=[[ABC News (United States)|ABC News]] |access-date=1 December 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251218051839/https://abcnews.go.com/International/famine-determined-parts-gaza-500000-experiencing-catastrophic-hunger/story?id=124843218 |archive-date=18 December 2025}}</ref> Early in the conflict, Israel cut off Gaza's water and electricity, but it later partially restored the water.<ref>{{cite web |first=Barak |last=Ravid |title=Israel resumes water supply to southern Gaza after U.S. pressure |url=https://www.axios.com/2023/10/15/israel-resumes-water-supply-to-southern-gaza-after-us-pressure |website=[[Axios (website)|Axios]] |access-date=18 September 2025 |date=15 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250915020309/https://www.axios.com/2023/10/15/israel-resumes-water-supply-to-southern-gaza-after-us-pressure |archive-date=15 September 2025}}</ref> As of May 2024, 84% of Gaza's health centres have been [[Attacks on health facilities during the Gaza war|destroyed or damaged]].{{sfn|Neuman|Baba|Wood|2024}} Israel also [[Destruction of cultural heritage during the Israeli invasion of the Gaza Strip|destroyed numerous cultural heritage sites]], including all 12 of Gaza's universities, and 80% of its schools.<ref name="scholasticide">{{cite web |date=18 April 2024 |title=UN experts deeply concerned over 'scholasticide' in Gaza }}</ref> Over 1.9 million Palestinians—85% of Gaza's population—were forcibly displaced.<ref>{{cite news |title=UN: Gaza 'catastrophe' threatens to raise record global displacement |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/12/13/un-refugee-chief-says-gaza-war-leading-to-catastrophic-displacement |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |date=13 December 2023 |access-date=10 November 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251110010942/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/12/13/un-refugee-chief-says-gaza-war-leading-to-catastrophic-displacement |archive-date=10 November 2025}}</ref>

In December 2023, the government of [[South Africa]] instituted proceedings, ''[[South Africa v. Israel]]'', against Israel at the [[International Court of Justice]] (ICJ), alleging a violation of the [[Genocide Convention]].<ref name="ICJ-2023-12-29"/> In January 2024, the court ordered Israel to take all measures within its power to prevent the commission of acts of genocide, to prevent and punish [[incitement to genocide]], and to allow basic humanitarian service, aid and supplies into Gaza.<ref name="ICJruling">[[#ICJ-order-2024-01-26|Order, ''S. Afr.'', No. 192 (ICJ 26 January 2024)]].</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Simon |first1=Scott |last2=Peralta |first2=Eyder |date=27 January 2024 |url-status=live |title=ICJ finds genocide case against Israel 'plausible', orders it to stop violations |url=https://www.npr.org/2024/01/27/1227397107/icj-finds-genocide-case-against-israel-plausible-orders-it-to-stop-violations#:~:text=Live%20Sessions-,ICJ%20finds%20genocide%20case%20against%20Israel%20%27plausible%27%2C%20orders%20it,Africa%20has%20brought%20against%20Israel. |work=[[NPR]] |access-date=28 January 2024 2024}}</ref>{{sfn|Casciani|2024a}} The court later ordered Israel to increase humanitarian aid into Gaza and to halt its [[Rafah offensive]].{{sfn|Casciani|2024b}}{{sfn|Marsi|Siddiqui|Motamedi|2024}} Israel did not fully comply with the court's orders.<ref name="Amnesty International Blockade">{{cite web |date=26 February 2024 |title=Israel defying ICJ ruling to prevent genocide by failing to |access-date=13 September 2025 |archive-date=2 October 2025}}</ref><ref name="Human Rights Watch Blockade">{{cite web |date=26 February 2024 |title=Israel Not Complying with World Court Order in Genocide Case Israel and its supporters maintain that its actions [[Gaza genocide denial|do not constitute genocide]].{{sfn|Casciani|2024a}}<ref>{{cite news |last1=Deutsch |first1=Anthony |last2=Sterling |first2=Toby |last3=Berg |first3=Stephanie van den |date=12 January 2024 |title=Israel rejects genocide charges, tells World Court it must defend itself |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/israel-counter-genocide-accusations-world-court-2024-01-12/ |archive-url=https://archive.today/20240810000046/https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/israel-counter-genocide-accusations-world-court-2024-01-12/ |archive-date=10 August 2024 |access-date=23 June 2025 |work=[[Reuters]] |language=en}}</ref> The Israeli government maintains that its military actions were a response to the [[Hamas]]-led [[October 7 attacks]] on Israel and that it sought to destroy Hamas and free [[Israeli hostages]].<ref name="UN Commission of Inquiry report 2025 64" />{{sfn|Casciani|2024a}}<ref name="TOI3-11-23">{{cite news |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/idf-soldiers-fend-off-nighttime-hamas-ambush-as-battalion-commander-killed-in-gaza/ |title=IDF soldiers fend off nighttime Hamas ambush, as battalion commander killed in Gaza |work=[[The Times of Israel]] |date=3 November 2023 |first1=Emanuel |last1=Fabian |first2=Michael |last2=Bachner |archive-date=2 November 2023 |access-date=3 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231102185204/https://www.timesofisrael.com/idf-soldiers-fend-off-nighttime-hamas-ambush-as-battalion-commander-killed-in-gaza/ |url-status=live}}</ref> There is increasing consensus among genocide and international legal scholars on the genocide assessment,<ref name="growing_agreement" /> though some academics challenge it.{{sfn|Moses|2025|pp=1; 10–13}}<ref name="Ayad 2025" />

== Background ==
{{Further|Background to the Gaza war|4=Israeli–Palestinian conflict}}[[File:OCHA OpT September 2023 map of the Gaza Strip.pdf|thumb|A September 2023 [[United Nations]] map of Gaza, showing its [[Gaza–Israel barrier|border barrier]] and checkpoints into Israel and Egypt and Israel's [[Maritime Exclusion Zone]], illustrating the geographic scope of the preexisting blockade and the physical constraints on movement and access.]]
Israel's [[Israeli occupation of the Gaza Strip|occupation of the Gaza Strip]] began in the [[1967 Arab–Israeli War]]. In 2005, Israel [[Israeli disengagement from the Gaza Strip|withdrew its ground forces]] in the context of the [[Oslo Accords]] and the [[Second Intifada]].<ref>{{Cite book |last=Stern-Weiner |first=Jamie |url=https://books.google.com/books?id=8U9V0AEACAAJ |title=Deluge: Gaza and Israel from Crisis to Cataclysm |date=2024 |publisher=OR Books |isbn=978-1-68219-619-9 |language=en}}</ref> The International Court of Justice subsequently issued an [[ICJ case on Israel's occupation of the Palestinian territories|advisory opinion]] that despite the withdrawal Israel is still illegally occupying the Gaza Strip.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Berg |first1=Raffi |date=19 July 2024 |title=UN top court says Israeli occupation of Palestinian territories is illegal |url=https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cjerjzxlpvdo |access-date=3 October 2025 |work=[[BBC News]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250922204607/https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cjerjzxlpvdo |archive-date=22 September 2025 |url-status=live}}</ref>

Since 2007, the [[Gaza Strip]] has been governed by [[Hamas]], an [[Islamism|Islamist]] militant group, while the [[West Bank]] remained under the control of the [[Palestinian Authority]]. After Hamas took over, Israel intensified its [[blockade of the Gaza Strip]], citing security concerns;<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
| {{harvnb|Perry|McDowall|2023}}
| {{harvnb|Kane|Cohen|Shamir|Scher|2023}}
| {{harvnb|Salam|2023a}}
}}</ref><ref name="Meakem">{{Cite news |last=Meakem |first=Allison |date=10 October 2023 |title=The Geopolitics of Palestine, Explained |work=[[Foreign Policy]] |url=https://foreignpolicy.com/2023/10/10/israel-palestine-conflict-gaza-hamas-war-geography-history/ |access-date=16 October 2023 |archive-date=15 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231015213033/https://foreignpolicy.com/2023/10/10/israel-palestine-conflict-gaza-hamas-war-geography-history/ |url-status=live}}</ref> international rights groups have called the blockade a form of [[collective punishment]].<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted|

| {{Cite magazine |date=9 October 2023 |title=Images of the Mass Kidnapping of Israelis by Hamas |url=https://www.theatlantic.com/international/archive/2023/10/kidnappings-israel-hamas-photographs/675593/ |access-date=10 October 2023 |magazine=[[The Atlantic]] |language=en |archive-date=10 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231010012057/https://www.theatlantic.com/international/archive/2023/10/kidnappings-israel-hamas-photographs/675593/ |url-status=live}}

}}</ref> [[Israeli government response to the October 7 attacks|Israel responded]] with a highly destructive<ref>{{cite news |last=Dyer |first=Evan |date=30 December 2023 |title=Israel's Gaza bombing campaign is the most destructive of this century, analysts say |url=https://www.cbc.ca/news/politics/israel-gaza-bombing-hamas-civilian-casualties-1.7068647 |work=[[CBC News]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240630222241/https://www.cbc.ca/news/politics/israel-gaza-bombing-hamas-civilian-casualties-1.7068647 |archive-date=30 June 2024}}</ref> [[Israeli bombing of the Gaza Strip|bombing campaign]] followed by an [[Israeli invasion of the Gaza Strip|invasion of the Gaza Strip]] on 27 October.{{sfn|Segal|Daniele|2024|p=6}}

Hamas officials said the attack was a response to the [[Israeli-occupied territories|Israeli occupation of the West Bank]], the [[blockade of the Gaza Strip|blockade of Gaza]], [[Israeli settler violence]] against Palestinians, [[Palestinian freedom of movement|restrictions on the movement of Palestinians]], and the [[Palestinians in Israeli custody|detainment of thousands of Palestinians, many without charges]], whom Hamas sought to release by taking Israeli hostages.<ref>{{cite news |date=7 October 2023 |title=Fears of a ground invasion of Gaza grow as Israel vows 'mighty vengeance' |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/10/7/world-is-watching-fears-grow-of-a-massive-gaza-invasion-by-israel |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=8 October 2023 |archive-date=8 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231008024318/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/10/7/world-is-watching-fears-grow-of-a-massive-gaza-invasion-by-israel |url-status=live}}</ref>{{sfn|McKernan|Michaelson|Graham-Harrison|Kierszenbaum|2023}}<ref>{{cite news |last=Pacchiani |first=Luca |date=7 October 2023 |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/hamas-deputy-chief-anticipates-hostages-will-be-swapped-for-palestinian-prisoners/ |title=Hamas deputy chief anticipates hostages will be swapped for Palestinian prisoners |work=[[The Times of Israel]] |access-date=25 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20241126123700/https://www.timesofisrael.com/hamas-deputy-chief-anticipates-hostages-will-be-swapped-for-palestinian-prisoners/ |archive-date=26 November 2024}}</ref> Numerous commentators have identified Israeli occupation as a cause of the war.<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
| {{harvnb|Matar|2023}}
| {{harvnb|Schenker|2023}}
| {{harvnb|Barghouti|2023}}
| {{harvnb|Federman|Adwan|2023}}
}}</ref> Several human rights organisations, including [[Amnesty International]],{{sfn|Amnesty International|2022|pp=266–267}} [[B'Tselem]],<ref>{{harvnb|B'Tselem|2021}}: "A regime that uses laws, practices and organized violence to cement the supremacy of one group over another is an apartheid regime. Israeli apartheid, which promotes the supremacy of Jews over Palestinians, was not born in one day or of a single speech. It is a process that has gradually grown more institutionalized and explicit, with mechanisms introduced over time in law and practice to promote Jewish supremacy. These accumulated measures, their pervasiveness in legislation and political practice, and the public and judicial support they receive—all form the basis for our conclusion that the bar for labeling the Israeli regime as apartheid has been met."</ref> and [[Human Rights Watch]],<ref>{{Cite news |last=Holmes |first=Oliver |date=27 April 2021 |title=Israel is committing the crime of apartheid, rights group says |work=[[The Guardian]] |url=http://www.theguardian.com/world/2021/apr/27/israel-committing-crime-apartheid-human-rights-watch |url-status=live |access-date=6 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20220202210105/https://www.theguardian.com/world/2021/apr/27/israel-committing-crime-apartheid-human-rights-watch |archive-date=2 February 2022}}</ref> have [[Israeli apartheid|likened the Israeli occupation to apartheid]]; Israel's supporters dispute this characterisation.<ref>{{cite news |date=4 May 2023 |title=Israël: l'Assemblée nationale rejette une |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20230614002231/https://www.lefigaro.fr/flash-actu/israel-l-assemblee-nationale-rejette-une-resolution-communiste-denoncant-un-regime-d-apartheid-20230504 |archive-date=14 June 2023}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Hutzler |first1=Alexandra |last2=Peller |first2=Lauren |date=19 July 2023 |title=House passes resolution saying Israel isn't a 'racist or apartheid state' |work=[[ABC News (United States)|ABC News]] |url=https://abcnews.go.com/Politics/house-vote-resolution-israel-racist-apartheid-state/story?id=101410569 |url-status=live |access-date=15 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231030033122/https://abcnews.go.com/Politics/house-vote-resolution-israel-racist-apartheid-state/story?id=101410569 |archive-date=30 October 2023}}</ref> A July 2024 [[advisory opinion]] by the [[International Court of Justice]] [[ICJ case on Israel's occupation of the Palestinian territories|affirmed the occupation as illegal]] and said it violated the [[International Convention on the Elimination of All Forms of Racial Discrimination]].<ref>{{cite news |last=Siddique |first=Haroon |date=19 July 2024 |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/article/2024/jul/19/israels-settlement-policies-break-international-law-court-finds |access-date=25 September 2024 |work=[[The Guardian]] |language=en-GB |archive-date=22 July 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240722174228/https://www.theguardian.com/world/article/2024/jul/19/israels-settlement-policies-break-international-law-court-finds |url-status=live}}</ref>

During the first 48 hours of Israel's retaliatory attack, IDF chief [[Herzi Halevi]] reported that the IDF attacked 1,000 targets. According to his wife, he told her that "Gaza will be destroyed". Reportedly, Prime Minister [[Benjamin Netanyahu]] subsequently said he wanted 5,000 targets to be attacked, even though the IDF had not confirmed 5,000 enemy targets. Artificial intelligence was used to generate a list of targets, in many cases based on unconfirmed or outdated intelligence. About 10,000 Palestinians were killed in a month, including entire families. [[Shmuel Lederman]] called this "as criminal as it gets".{{sfn|Lederman|2025|p=7}}

The Israeli government has said that the military actions it has undertaken are in response to the [[October 7 attacks]] and sought to destroy Hamas, overthrow its [[governance of the Gaza Strip]], and free Israeli hostages. It has denied that its military operations constitute genocide.<ref name="UN Commission of Inquiry report 2025 64" />{{sfn|Casciani|2024a}}<ref name="TOI3-11-23" /> Multiple commentators argue that part of the motive is retaliation for the 7 October attacks.<ref>{{harvnb|Fassin|2024|pp=1–2}}; {{harvnb|Semerdjian|2024a|pp=1, 3}}; {{harvnb|Levene|2024|pp=1–2}}</ref><ref name="Response">{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
| {{harvnb|Mackenzie|Lubell|2023}}: "Israel has tightened its blockade on and bombarded Gaza for three weeks after the Islamist group Hamas' Oct. 7 assault killed 1,400 Israelis ... Abbas ... said, 'Our people in the Gaza Strip are facing a war of genocide and massacres committed by the Israeli occupation forces in full view of the entire world.{{'"}}
| {{harvnb|Antonio|2023}}: "Israeli Ambassador to the Philippines Ilan Fluss rejected the notion that his country is committing genocide in Gaza City, where a two-week war has erupted ... their measures were targeting Hamas members, and they were 'taking all measures to avoid having civilians affected" by attacks. 'We are informing civilians even before attacks: keep away from Hamas' infrastructure and Hamas' facilities,' ... Hamas attacked Israel on Oct. 7, and killed at least 1,400 people, mostly civilians."
| {{harvnb|Chacar|2023}}
| {{harvnb|Smith|McCarthy|Londoño|Jordan|2023}}
| {{harvnb|Nichols|2023}}
| {{harvnb|Bishara|2023}}
}}</ref><ref>{{harvnb|Abraham|2024}}: {{'"}}There was a completely permissive policy regarding the casualties of [bombing] operations—so permissive that in my opinion it had an element of revenge," D., an intelligence source, claimed. ... A. also used the word "revenge" to describe the atmosphere inside the army after October 7.'</ref> [[Nimer Sultany]] argues that [[anti-Palestinianism]] is also a motive.{{sfn|Sultany|2024|pp=2–3}}

=== Definitions of genocide and legal challenges ===
{{main|Genocide definitions}}

The 1948 United Nations [[Genocide Convention]] defines genocide as acts committed "with intent to destroy, in whole or in part, a national, ethnic, racial, or religious group", and as such, "causing harm, preventing births, and forcibly transferring children".{{sfn|United Nations|2014}}<ref name="Genocide Prevention">{{cite web |title=United Nations Office on Genocide Prevention and the Responsibility to Protect |url=https://www.un.org/en/genocideprevention/genocide.shtml |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231201103920/https://www.un.org/en/genocideprevention/genocide.shtml |archive-date=1 December 2023 |access-date=3 January 2024 |website=[[United Nations]] |url-status=dead}}</ref> The [[International Court of Justice]] has never held a state liable for genocide.<ref>{{Cite news |last=Borger |first=Julian |date=2024-01-11 |title=ICJ case against Israel could finally empower the genocide convention |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2024/jan/11/icj-case-against-israel-could-finally-empower-the-genocide-convention |access-date=2026-01-22 |work=The Guardian |language=en-GB |issn=0261-3077 |quote=In 2007, the court [ICJ] ruled that Serbia had failed to prevent the 1995 genocide at Srebrenica in Bosnia and Herzegovina, a case of a victim taking an alleged perpetrator to court, but it has never yet held a state responsible for the commission of genocide.}}</ref><ref name="RSIL2024"/> The legal threshold for genocidal intent remains a major barrier to prosecution.<ref name="RSIL2024">{{cite web |last=Gehani |first=Brishna |date=16 February 2024 |title=Is the ICJ's standard of proof for genocide unattainable? |url=https://rsilpak.org/2024/is-the-icjs-standard-of-proof-for-genocide-unattainable/ |access-date=27 February 2025 |website=Research Society of International Law |language=en-US |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20241219161802/https://rsilpak.org/2024/is-the-icjs-standard-of-proof-for-genocide-unattainable/ |url-status=live |archive-date=19 December 2024}}</ref>

The original definition coined by [[Raphael Lemkin]] was broader than that used by the Genocide Convention and included [[Cultural genocide|cultural and social destruction]]. In contrast, orthodox scholarly definitions emphasise actions targeting a group's physical survival.{{sfn|Semerdjian|2024b|p=14}}{{sfn|McDoom|2024|p=3}} No minimum number of victims<ref>{{cite web|title=Legal concepts and questions |url=https://iimm.un.org/legal-concepts/|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240808100717/https://iimm.un.org/legal-concepts/ |url-status=live |archive-date=8 August 2024|website=Independent Investigative Mechanism for Myanmar}} "There is no minimum number of victims, but the part of the group targeted must be significant enough that its destruction would impact the group as a whole."</ref><ref>{{cite web|title=Large number of victims|website=ICTR/ICTY/IRMCT Case Law Database|url=https://cld.irmct.org/notions/show/508/large-number-of-victims# |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240825165026/https://cld.irmct.org/notions/show/508/large-number-of-victims|archive-date=25 August 2024|publisher=[[International Residual Mechanism for Criminal Tribunals]]}}</ref>{{sfn|UNHR|2024|pp=24–25}} or intended victims<ref>{{Cite web |last1=Stanton |first1=Gregory H |author-link=Gregory Stanton |date=25 May 2025 |title=Israel's Twelve Tactics of Denial |url=https://www.genocidewatch.com/single-post/israel-s-twelve-tactics-of-denial |access-date=23 September 2025 |website=Genocide Watch |language=en |quote=Many who have not read the Genocide Convention think genocide can only be proven if the intent is to destroy a whole people. But the Convention clearly states that intent to destroy part of a people is enough to prove genocide.}}</ref> is required to establish the crime, nor is complete destruction of the group.<ref>{{cite book |last1=Ohlin |first1=Jens |author-link=Jens David Ohlin |chapter=Attempt to Commit Genocide |date=15 October 2009 |title=The UN Genocide Convention |editor-last=Gaeta |editor-first=Paola |publisher=[[Oxford University Press]] |pages=193–206 |doi=10.1093/law/9780199570218.003.0009 |isbn=978-0-19-957021-8}}</ref> In the [[Rohingya genocide case]], several states contended that the ICJ should "adopt a balanced approach that recognizes the special gravity of the crime of genocide, without rendering the threshold for inferring [[genocidal intent]] so difficult to meet so as to make findings of genocide near-impossible."{{sfn|Jamshidi|2024a|p=13}}

== Genocidal intent and incitement ==
{{Main|Intent and incitement in the Gaza genocide}}

[[File:Palestinians under the rubble after Israeli airstrike of homes in the Gaza Strip.jpg|thumb|Palestinians under the rubble after [[Israeli bombing of the Gaza Strip]]]]
Experts affirm that statements by Israeli political and military leaders{{sfn|Segal|Daniele|2024|pp=1–2}}{{sfn|Lederman|2024|pp=1–2}}<ref name="Asem2025">{{cite news |last=Asem |first=Sondos |date=14 August 2025 |title=Israel's war on Gaza: Why do legal experts say it's genocide? |url=https://www.middleeasteye.net/news/israel-gaza-why-experts-say-genocide-international-law |url-status=live |work=[[Middle East Eye]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250819152628/https://www.middleeasteye.net/news/israel-gaza-why-experts-say-genocide-international-law |archive-date=19 August 2025}}</ref>—coupled with [[Eliminationism|eliminationist]] media rhetoric and Israel's conduct in Gaza—indicate [[genocidal intent]] and [[Incitement to genocide|incitement]] against the [[Palestinians|Palestinian people]] in Gaza.<ref name="Asem2025" /> Israeli officials and journalists{{sfn|Segal|Daniele|2024|pp=1–2}}{{sfn|Kulkarni|2023}}{{sfn|B'Tselem|2025|p=67}} have made verbal statements that [[Palestinians as animals in Israeli discourse|dehumanise Palestinians]] and [[Incitement to genocide|incite]], [[Genocide justification|justify]], or praise atrocities against them as a group.<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
| {{harvnb|UN Commission of Inquiry report|2025|p=54}}: "The Commission finds that many statements made by Israeli officials contain dehumanising sentiments that encourage hatred toward Palestinians and violence against Palestinians and are consistent with the pattern of conduct...that point to an intent to destroy Palestinians in Gaza as a group. The Commission considers that these statements by Israeli officials are reasonably interpreted as statements expressing an intent to destroy the Palestinian group in Gaza and they have been acted on as such by Israeli security forces in the Gaza Strip. They are direct evidence of dolus specialis."
| {{harvnb|Amnesty International report|2024|p=|pp=26–35}}: "Bearing in mind that...the othering and dehumanization of the protected group and that the use of derogatory language...can provide evidence of genocidal intent, Amnesty International examined Israeli officials' use of dehumanizing, racist and derogatory rhetoric against Palestinians.... It reviewed 102 statements made by Israeli government officials, high-ranking military officers and members of the Knesset made between 7 October 2023 and 30 June 2024 which dehumanized Palestinians, or called for, or justified, genocidal acts or other crimes under international law against them."
| {{harvnb|Kulkarni|2023}}: "Army's spokesperson Daniel Hagari, who bragged of dropping 'thousands of tons of munitions'...had no qualms admitting that 'we're focused on what causes maximum damage', rather than 'accuracy'. Referring to Palestinians as 'human animals', Defense Minister Yoav Gallant, who prided in having 'released all the restraints' on the military, had said in the early days of the war that 'we will eliminate everything' in Gaza...Legitimizing the mass killing of civilians in Gaza, Israeli President Isaac Herzog had declared that 'an entire nation out there is responsible' for the October 7 attack on Israel by Hamas, arguing that the 'rhetoric' about innocent civilians is 'absolutely not true.'... 'This practice of casting an entire population as enemies, as legitimate military targets, is a common genocidal mechanism,' Raz Segal, a prominent Jewish Israeli scholar of Holocaust and Genocide Studies, said in his remarks at the panel discussion."
}}</ref>{{sfn|Gessen|2024}} Genocidal intent is also evidenced by the [[Casualties of the Gaza war|scale]] and systematic nature of actions that exceed any legitimate military objective<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
| {{harvnb|Al-Waheidi|2025}}: "Fyfe, the Washington and Lee University legal scholar, said, 'Genocide can occur within or outside of war. But it is never permissible, even if the war itself is. So war is not a defense...If a military leader intends to gain land and removing a group is the only way to do it, that's not necessarily genocide. But if the only reasonable inference from a siege or campaign is that the group itself is being destroyed as such, then that is genocidal intent...I do not think it is reasonable to claim that the siege is a military objective, given that Hamas is already crippled."{{px2}}"
| {{harvnb|Gurmendi Dunkelberg|2025|p=21}}
| {{harvnb|Jamshidi|2024b}}
}}</ref><ref name="Asem2025" />—including the extensive targeting of children,<ref name="UN Commission of Inquiry report 2025 64">{{harvnb|UN Commission of Inquiry report|2025|p=64}}: "The extensive and deliberate targeting of Palestinian children shows that the military operations were not conducted solely to defeat Hamas and other Palestinian armed groups, nor can they legitimately contribute to the other stated goals of defending the state of Israel and securing the release of Israeli hostages."</ref><ref name="Asem2025" /><ref name="IAGSResolution"/> widespread sexual violence,<ref>{{harvnb|UN Commission of Inquiry report|2025|p=25}}: "Whether targeting women, men, boys or girls, sexual violence was conducted not just to degrade and humiliate profoundly the direct victims but to punish the Palestinian group as a whole."</ref> [[Destruction of cultural heritage during the Israeli invasion of the Gaza Strip|destruction of cultural heritage]],<ref>{{harvnb|Amnesty International report|2024|p=32}}:</ref><ref name="whywecall" /><ref>{{Cite web |date=30 January 2024 |title=Widescale destruction of cultural heritage in Gaza |url=https://www.museumsassociation.org/museums-journal/news/2024/01/widescale-destruction-of-cultural-heritage-in-gaza/ |access-date=29 September 2025 |website=[[Museums Association]] |language=en-US |quote=The destruction of cultural heritage, which Palestinians have accused Israel of targeting deliberately, was cited as evidence in South Africa's case to the UN International Court of Justice that the state is committing acts of genocide in Gaza. |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250818185206/https://www.museumsassociation.org/museums-journal/news/2024/01/widescale-destruction-of-cultural-heritage-in-gaza/ |archive-date=18 August 2025}}</ref> and imposition of [[Gaza humanitarian crisis|life-destroying conditions]]<ref>{{harvnb|Amnesty International report|2024|p=213}}: "The nature of the conditions of life that Israel imposed on Palestinians in Gaza following 7 October 2023 indicates that the destruction of the group, as such, was their intended outcome. The Israeli authorities decided to impose a total siege on Gaza on 9 October 2023...fully aware that this would necessarily cause and exacerbate malnutrition, hunger, the outbreak of multiple diseases and, ultimately, bring Gaza to the brink of famine. Indeed, Israel must have been aware of the 'objective probability' that these conditions of life would lead to the physical destruction of Palestinians in Gaza, a factor identified as probative of intent."</ref>{{sfn|Quigley|2024a}}—together with the persistence of these practices despite awareness of their catastrophic effects.<ref>{{harvnb|UN Commission of Inquiry report|2025|p=62}}: "The Commission finds that the Israeli authorities were aware that, by destroying the healthcare system throughout Gaza, their actions would lead to the destruction of Palestinians as a group... the systematic and complete destruction of the healthcare system in Gaza, the siege-induced deprivation of medical necessities... were part of the intent to destroy Palestinians in Gaza by preventing their capacity and possibility to heal, recover and live"</ref><ref>{{harvnb|Lederman|2025|p=2}}: "The case of Gaza...shows us again why the meaning of intent in the Genocide Convention should be reinterpreted...to include the foreseeable consequences of a given policy when its meaning is the genocidal destruction of a group or a severe harm to it as a group—a knowledge-based rather than purpose-based concept of genocide. Such a concept points to...moving away from the focus on obscure mental states of individual perpetrators to the collective process that leads to genocide."</ref>

{{Quote box|"I have ordered a complete siege on the Gaza Strip. There will be no electricity, no food, no fuel, everything is closed. We are fighting human animals, and we are acting accordingly."{{#tag:ref|[[Modern Hebrew|Hebrew]]: {{lang|he|״הוריתי להטיל מצור מוחלט על רצועת עזה. לא יהיה חשמל, לא יהיה מזון, לא יהיה דלק הכל סגור. אנחנו נלחמים בחיות אדם ואנחנו נוהגים בהתאם״|rtl=y}}|group=lower-alpha}}
| author = – [[Yoav Gallant]], Minister of Defense of Israel, on 9 October 2023<ref>{{Cite web |date=10 October 2023 |script-title=he:מדיניות נקמה יצאה לדרך; ישראל מבצעת פשעי מלחמה בעזה |title=mediniot nikma yetza'a lidrach; yisral mivtza'at pashe'i milchama be'eza |trans-title=A policy of revenge is underway; Israel is committing war crimes in Gaza |url=https://www.btselem.org/hebrew/press_releases/20231010_revenge_policy_in_motion_israel_committing_war_crimes_in_gaza |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250119111743/https://www.btselem.org/hebrew/press_releases/20231010_revenge_policy_in_motion_israel_committing_war_crimes_in_gaza |archive-date=19 January 2025 |access-date=30 September 2025 |website=[[B'Tselem]] |language=he}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=2023 |title=Gaza/Palestine: States have a Duty to Prevent Genocide |url=https://www.icj.org/resource/gaza-occupied-palestinian-territory-states-have-a-duty-to-prevent-genocide/ |access-date=30 September 2025 |website=[[International Commission of Jurists]] |language=en-US |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250924011619/https://www.icj.org/resource/gaza-occupied-palestinian-territory-states-have-a-duty-to-prevent-genocide/ |archive-date=24 September 2025}}</ref><ref>{{Cite AV media |url=https://www.facebook.com/reel/2475688039283347/ |script-title=he:הוריתי להטיל מצור מוחלט על עזה. ‏אנחנו נלחמים בחיות אדם, ונוהגים בהתאם. |title=horiti lehatil metzur muchlat al aza. anachanu nilchmim bechayot adam, venohagim behitam |trans-title=I have ordered a complete blockade of Gaza. We are fighting human beings, and we are acting accordingly. |date=9 October 2023 |first=Yoav |last=Gallant |author-link=Yoav Gallant |language=he |access-date=30 September 2025 |via=www.facebook.com |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251123173104/https://www.facebook.com/reel/2475688039283347/ |archive-date=23 November 2025}}</ref>

}}

Both a [[Independent International Commission of Inquiry on the Occupied Palestinian Territory|United Nations commission of inquiry]] and [[Amnesty International]] documented a "pattern of conduct" by Israeli authorities, concluding that genocidal intent is the "only reasonable inference" that can be drawn from the evidence.<ref>{{harvnb|Amnesty International report|2024|p=35}}: "The evidence presented in the report clearly shows that the destruction of Palestinians in Gaza, as such, was Israel's intent—either in addition to or as a means to achieve its military aims. There is only one reasonable inference that can be drawn from the evidence presented: genocidal intent has been part and parcel of Israel's conduct in Gaza since 7 October 2023, including its military campaign."</ref><ref>{{harvnb|UN Commission of Inquiry report|2025|p=64}}: "On the basis of fully conclusive evidence, the Commission finds that statements made by Israeli authorities are direct evidence of genocidal intent. Additionally, on the basis of circumstantial evidence, the Commission finds that genocidal intent was the only reasonable inference that could be drawn, based on the pattern of conduct of the Israeli authorities. Thus, the Commission concludes that the Israeli authorities and Israeli security forces have the genocidal intent to destroy, in whole or in part, the Palestinians in the Gaza Strip."</ref> Other organisations that have attributed genocidal intent to the actions or statements of Israeli officials include a [[Committee on the Exercise of the Inalienable Rights of the Palestinian People|United Nations panel]]{{sfn|Kulkarni|2023}}{{sfn|Condon|Condon|2024}} and [[Genocide Watch]].<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
| {{harvnb|Stanton|2025b}}
| {{harvnb|Condon|Condon|2024}}
| {{harvnb|Kulkarni|2023}}
}}</ref><ref name="twailr">{{harvnb|"Public Statement: Scholars Warn"|2023}}</ref> As part of ''[[Defense for Children International – Palestine v. Biden]]'', the historian [[Barry Trachtenberg]] said that the rhetoric used by Israeli officials underlies the consensus among genocide historians that the situation in Gaza constitutes genocide.{{sfn|Gessen|2024}} [[Navi Pillay]], the chair of the UN commission of inquiry, compared the statements of Israeli politicians to the genocidal incitement during the [[Rwandan genocide]].<ref>{{Cite news |last1=Doherty |first1=Ben |date=3 November 2025 |title=World must fight Israel's genocide in Gaza like it did apartheid, pioneering South African judge says |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2025/nov/04/world-must-fight-israel-genocide-gaza-like-aparthied-navi-pillay |access-date=3 November 2025 |work=[[The Guardian]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251105173449/https://www.theguardian.com/world/2025/nov/04/world-must-fight-israel-genocide-gaza-like-aparthied-navi-pillay |archive-date=5 November 2025}}</ref>

In September 2025, Israeli prime minister Benjamin Netanyahu, president [[Isaac Herzog]], and former defence minister [[Yoav Gallant]] were found by a United Nations commission of inquiry to have engaged in "direct and public [[incitement to commit genocide]]".{{sfn|UN Commission of Inquiry report|2025|pp=64–67}} Israeli leaders' [[Intent and incitement in the Gaza genocide#Amalek|repeated references]] to [[Amalek]]—the biblical enemy of Israelites whose annihilation is commanded by God—have been considered evidence of genocidal intent by many critics,<ref>{{harvnb|Bartov|2023}}; {{harvnb|Jones|2024}}; {{harvnb|Levene|2024|pp=4–5}}; {{harvnb|Coghill|2024}}</ref><ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted||{{harvnb|Marin|West|2024}}|{{harvnb|Bybelezer|2023}}|{{harvnb|Jones|2024}}|{{harvnb|Netanyahu|2023}}}}</ref> including South Africa.<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
| {{harvnb|Goldenberg|2024}}
| {{harvnb|Schmitz|2024}}
| {{harvnb|Coghill|2024}}
| {{harvnb|Bartov|2023}}
}}</ref><ref name="McGreal 2023">{{cite news |last=McGreal |first=Chris |author-link=Chris McGreal |date=13 November 2023 |title=US rights group sues Biden for alleged 'failure to prevent genocide' in Gaza |language=en-GB |work=[[The Guardian]] |url=https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/2023/nov/13/biden-lawsuit-alleged-failure-prevent-genocide-israel-palestine |access-date=14 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231121091027/https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/2023/nov/13/biden-lawsuit-alleged-failure-prevent-genocide-israel-palestine |archive-date=21 November 2023}}</ref>

== Onset ==
[[B'Tselem]], the South African case against Israel, and some scholars who argue Israel is committing genocide argument give 7 October as its start date.<ref>{{harvnb|Jamshidi|2024a|pp=1–4}}: "In its application to the ICJ, South Africa describes Israel's entire campaign inside Gaza since 7 October as genocidal."</ref>{{sfn|Semerdjian|2024a|pp=3–4}}{{sfn|B'Tselem|2025|p=82}} According to B'Tselem, "The genocidal assault on the residents of Gaza, and on all Palestinians as a group, cannot be understood without acknowledging the impact of the 7 October attack on Israeli society. The shock, fear and humiliation elicited by the attack, and the societal upheaval it triggered, served as a driving force for a shift in government policy toward the Palestinians—from oppression and control to destruction and annihilation."{{sfn|B'Tselem|2025|p=5}} [[Martin Shaw (sociologist)|Martin Shaw]] and [[A. Dirk Moses]] argue that this "front-loaded violence" makes it harder to argue that the genocide began after the initial Israeli attack on Gaza.{{sfn|Shaw|2025b|p=3}}{{sfn|Moses|2025|p=12}}

On 13 October 2023, the historian [[Raz Segal]] said Israel was committing a "textbook case of genocide". He was one of the first scholars to do so.{{sfn|Klein|2025}} Others argue that the war was initially legitimate and the genocide started later, in 2024 or 2025.{{sfn|Shaw|2025b|p=3}}{{sfn|Moses|2025|p=12}} In September 2024, a UN [[Special Committee to Investigate Israeli Practices Affecting the Human Rights of the Palestinian People|Special Committee]] concluded, "the policies and practices of Israel during the reporting period [i.e. October 2023 to July 2024] are consistent with the characteristics of genocide."{{sfn|OHCHR|2024d|pp=1, 25–26}}

=== Direct killings ===
{{see also|War crimes in the Gaza war#By Israel|Gaza humanitarian crisis|Casualties of the Gaza war}}
UN experts and human rights organisations have characterised Israel's actions in Gaza as [[Extermination (crime)|extermination]],<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
| {{harvnb|Murphy|2025}}: "U.N. experts said in a report on Tuesday that Israel committed the crime against humanity of 'extermination' by killing civilians sheltering in schools and religious sites in Gaza, part of a 'concerted campaign to obliterate Palestinian life.{{'"}}
| {{Cite web |date=19 December 2024 |title=Israel's Crime of Extermination, Acts of Genocide in Gaza |url=https://www.hrw.org/news/2024/12/19/israels-crime-extermination-acts-genocide-gaza |access-date=16 September 2025 |website=[[Human Rights Watch]] |language=en |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250918070734/https://www.hrw.org/news/2024/12/19/israels-crime-extermination-acts-genocide-gaza |archive-date=18 September 2025}}
| {{harvnb|Condon|Condon|2024}}
| {{harvnb|Bayoumi|2025}}: "...today it is Israel's acts of extermination and genocide of Palestinians in Gaza, funded and enabled at every turn by a complicit west..."
| {{harvnb|Nashed|2025}}: {{"'}}The fact that the claims made by the RSF in Sudan resemble the claims Israel is making in Gaza … reveals the emergence of a template to commit mass extermination and even genocide,' said Luigi Daniele, a senior lecturer on IHL at Nottingham Law School."
}}</ref> a [[Crimes against humanity|crime against humanity]] that involves "the act of killing on a large scale". During the [[Israeli bombing of the Gaza Strip|first two months of bombing]], Israel dropped 25,000 tonnes of explosives on the Gaza Strip. Many of these were unguided bombs dropped in densely populated areas, obliterating entire neighbourhoods.{{sfn|Albanese|2024a|pp=6–7}} Since 7 October 2023, the IDF has been accused of extrajudicial killing of unarmed Palestinians<ref>{{cite news |last1=Debre |first1=Isabel |last2=Shurafa |first2=Wafaa |date=14 December 2023 |title=Hungry, thirsty and humiliated: Israel's mass arrest campaign sows fear in northern Gaza |url=https://apnews.com/article/palestinians-detained-israel-hamas-gaza-war-0ecbc338e4024add059b87b38022086d |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240118123911/https://apnews.com/article/palestinians-detained-israel-hamas-gaza-war-0ecbc338e4024add059b87b38022086d |archive-date=18 January 2024 |access-date=2 February 2024 |work=[[Associated Press]] |url-status=live |language=en}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last=Frankel |first=Julia |date=15 December 2023 |title=Israeli military opens probe after videos show Israeli forces killing 2 Palestinians at close range |url=https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-west-bank-gaza-war-east-jerusalem-shooting-army-23338c903c08bdd3e5fade3e2a048ab1 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240124200810/https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-west-bank-gaza-war-east-jerusalem-shooting-army-23338c903c08bdd3e5fade3e2a048ab1 |archive-date=24 |archive-date=5 February 2024 |access-date=2 February 2024 |work=[[CNN]] |language=en}}</ref> Israeli soldiers have killed Palestinian civilians, with a December 2023 UN report stating that they allegedly shot them in front of their families.{{sfn|UNHR|2024|pp=37–38}} In January 2024, Israeli soldiers shot at civilians waving [[white flag]]s, killing one.{{sfn|UNHR|2024|pp=37–38}}<ref>{{Cite news |date=24 January 2024 |title=Video shows Gaza civilian shot and killed in group waving white flag In April 2024, [[Gaza Strip mass graves|mass graves]] were found containing over 300 corpses,{{sfn|UNHR|2024|p=40}}<ref name="un-1148876">{{Cite news |date=23 April 2024 |title=Mass graves in Gaza show victims' hands were tied, says UN rights office |url=https://news.un.org/en/story/2024/04/1148876 |access-date=21 November 2025 |work=UN News |publisher=[[United Nations]] |quote=A total of 283 bodies were recovered at Nasser Hospital ... There are reports that the hands of some of these bodies were also tied' |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240503081228/https://news.un.org/en/story/2024/04/1148876 |archive-date=3 May 2024}}</ref> allegedly including older people, women and wounded,<ref name="un-1148876"/> and others with their hands tied.<ref name="un-1148876"/> The IDF said accusations that it caused the killings were "baseless and unfounded",<ref name="toi-mass-graves">{{Cite news |last=Fabian |first=Emanuel |date=23 April 2024 |title=IDF rejects 'baseless' claim it dug mass graves at Gaza hospital; At least 14,000 Palestinians had been killed in Gaza by December 2023.<ref>{{cite news |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/israeli-authorities-identify-gaza-hostages-dead-captivity-2023-12-01/ |title=Israeli authorities identify Gaza hostages dead captivity |work=[[Reuters]] |date=1 December 2023 |access-date=10 November 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251110121934/https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/israeli-authorities-identify-gaza-hostages-dead-captivity-2023-12-01/ |archive-date=10 November 2025}}</ref> In late 2024, a study limited only to those fatalities confirmed by at least three independent sources, and only from November 2023 to April 2024 (about 8,100 people), corroborated previous reports by the UN and news outlets that 70% of fatalities were women and children.<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
| {{harvnb|Faddoul|Shannon|Asghar|Boukari|2024|pp=25–26}}
| {{harvnb|Saric|2024}}
| {{harvnb|Thomas|2023}}
| {{harvnb|Associated Press|2023a}}
| {{harvnb|Sawafta|Fick|2023}}
| {{cite web |title=Nearly 25,000 Palestinians killed during 70-day Israeli genocide in Gaza |date=15 December 2023 |url=https://euromedmonitor.org/en/article/6035/Nearly-25,000-Palestinians-killed-during-70-day-Israeli-genocide-in-Gaza |publisher=[[Euro-Mediterranean Human Rights Monitor]] |access-date=25 December 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231220142411/https://euromedmonitor.org/en/article/6035/Nearly-25,000-Palestinians-killed-during-70-day-Israeli-genocide-in-Gaza |url-status=live |archive-date=20 December 2023}}
| {{harvnb|Burga|2023}}
}}</ref>{{#tag:ref|Per the [[Gaza Health Ministry]] and Government Information Office by 3 January 2024, over 22,300 people had been confirmed dead.<ref name="cas1tmp4">{{cite magazine |title=Health Ministry In Hamas-run Gaza Says War Death Toll Hits 22,313 |url=https://www.barrons.com/news/health-ministry-in-hamas-run-gaza-says-war-death-toll-hits-22-313-584e999b?refsec=topics_afp-news |access-date=3 January 2024 |magazine=[[Barron's]] |date=3 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240103101715/https://www.barrons.com/news/health-ministry-in-hamas-run-gaza-says-war-death-toll-hits-22-313-584e999b?refsec=topics_afp-news |url-status=live |archive-date=3 January 2024}}</ref>|group=lower-alpha}} As of 31 August 2024, data from the Ministry of Health (only for those of the dead who were fully identified, about 34,000 people at the time) showed that 60% of those killed were women, children, and the elderly.{{sfn|Graham-Harrison|2024b}} Eleven months later (31 July 2025) the number of those of the dead who were fully identified reached 60,199, 52.6% of whom were women, children, and the elderly.<ref>{{cite web |url=https://data.techforpalestine.org/ar/updates/killed-in-gaza-update-2025-08-17/ |title=Killed in Gaza |website=[[Tech for Palestine]] |date=17 August 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251224002852/https://data.techforpalestine.org/ar/updates/killed-in-gaza-update-2025-08-17/ |archive-date=24 December 2025}}</ref><ref>{{cite web |url=https://www.un.org/unispal/document/unrwa-sitrep-184-15aug25/ |title=UNRWA Situation Report #184 |website=[[United Nations]] |date=15 August 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250817183430/https://www.un.org/unispal/document/unrwa-sitrep-184-15aug25/ |archive-date=17 August 2025}}</ref>{{#tag:ref|47.4% were non-elderly men, 30.7% were children, 17.1% were non-elderly women, 3.0% were elderly men and 1.9% were elderly women.|group=lower-alpha}}

By 14 January 2024, over 23,900 Gazans had been confirmed killed.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Nashed |first1=Mat |last2=Cordall |first2=Simon Speakman |date=14 January 2024 |title=Israel's 100 days of relentless war on Gaza |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/features/longform/2024/1/14/israels-100-days-of-relentless-war-on-gaza |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240229143219/https://www.aljazeera.com/features/longform/2024/1/14/israels-100-days-of-relentless-war-on-gaza |archive-date=29 February 2024}}</ref> By 10 May, deaths had topped 35,000, a third of them unidentified, with over 10,000 more estimated to be buried under the rubble.<ref name="KhatibMcKeeYusuf"/> Within the first three weeks, the Israeli assault killed more children in Gaza than were killed worldwide across all conflict zones in any year since 2019.<ref>{{cite web |date=29 October 2023 |title=Gaza: 3,195 Children Killed in Three Weeks Surpasses Annual Number of Children Killed in Conflict Zones Since 2019 |archive-date=3 November 2023}}</ref>{{sfn|Qutami|2023|p=531}} Over 52,000 people had been wounded by December 2023,{{sfn|Thomas|2023}}{{sfn|Associated Press|2023a}} and by May 2024 this number had risen to over 77,700.{{sfn|United Nations in Palestine|2024}}<ref>{{cite news |last1=Adler |first1=Nils |last2=Uras |first2=Umut |date=5 May 2024 |title=Israel's war on Gaza live: Netanyahu accused of 'sabotaging' truce talks – Gaza death toll reaches 34,683 as Israeli offensive continues |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/5/5/israels-war-on-gaza-live-neither-side-willing-to-budge-in-truce-talks?update=2880155 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240505130049/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/5/5/israels-war-on-gaza-live-neither-side-willing-to-budge-in-truce-talks?update=2880155 |archive-date=5 May 2024}}</ref>

As of 10 October 2025, the Gaza Health Ministry reports that at least 67,194 Gazans were killed, which is between 3% and 4% of Gaza's total population.<ref>{{cite news |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/3/18/gaza-tracker |title=Gaza tracker |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |date=18 March 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251009155809/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/3/18/gaza-tracker |archive-date=9 October 2025}}</ref>

''[[+972 Magazine]]'' and ''Local Call'' reported that the IDF decided early in the war to authorise killing up to 15 to 20 civilians per low-ranking militant, while for a senior militant killing more than 100 civilians was authorised. An intelligence officer said that Israel was not interested in killing Palestinian operatives in a military context only, but preferred to bomb them in their family homes, saying "It's much easier to bomb a family's home" where they are easier to target.<ref>{{harvnb|Abraham|2024}}: "{{px2}}'It was very surprising for me that we were asked to bomb a house to kill a ground soldier, whose importance in the fighting was so low' said one source."</ref> Another intelligence officer said that in targeting junior militants, Israel used only [[dumb bomb]]s, which can destroy entire buildings, to not "waste expensive bombs on unimportant people".{{sfn|Abraham|2024}}

In March 2024, ''[[Haaretz]]'' reported that some Israeli commanders had set up "kill zones" in which soldiers were [[Rules of engagement|commanded to kill]] anyone on sight, even if they were unarmed.{{sfn|Kubovich|2024a}}{{sfn|Sultany|2024|p=11}} According to an Israeli officer, "in practice, a terrorist is anyone the IDF has killed in the areas in which its forces operate."{{sfn|Kubovich|2024a}}{{#tag:ref|In the original Hebrew article the Haaretz reporter used the term "Extermination Zones" ({{lang|he|שטחי ההשמדה}}, {{lang|he-latn|Shtachei Hashmada}}){{sfn|Kubovich|2024b}} instead of the English version term "Kill Zone".|group=lower-alpha}}

In June, the [[Associated Press]] found that Israel's campaign in Gaza was killing entire bloodlines of Palestinians to a "degree never seen before".<ref>{{cite news |last1=El Deeb |first1=Sara |date=17 June 2024 |title=Investigation identifies entire Palestinian families killed by Israeli strikes in Gaza |url=https://www.pbs.org/newshour/world/investigation-identifies-entire-palestinian-families-killed-by-israeli-strikes-in-gaza |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240619102152/https://www.pbs.org/newshour/world/investigation-identifies-entire-palestinian-families-killed-by-israeli-strikes-in-gaza |archive-date=19 June 2024 |access-date=25 June 2024 |work=[[PBS News Hour]] |agency=[[Associated Press]]}}</ref> According to testimony given to the Israeli [[Knesset]], Israeli soldiers driving [[IDF Caterpillar D9|armoured bulldozers]] had been ordered to "run over terrorists, dead and alive, in the hundreds".<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
| {{cite news |date=24 October 2024 |title=Israeli soldiers returning from war struggle with trauma and suicide |url=https://www.jpost.com/israel-news/article-825955 |access-date=28 October 2024 |work=[[The Jerusalem Post]] |language=en |archive-url=https://archive.today/20241024174515/https://www.jpost.com/israel-news/article-825955 |archive-date=24 October 2024}}
| {{harvnb|Cook|2024}}
| {{harvnb|Ebrahim|2024}}
| {{Cite news |date=24 October 2024 |title=Not the Onion: CNN highlights 'suffering' of Israeli army bulldozer driver who ran over so many people in Gaza it made him turn vegetarian |url=https://www.newarab.com/news/israeli-soldier-can-no-longer-eat-meat-after-killing-gaza |access-date=28 October 2024 |work=[[The New Arab]] |archive-url=https://archive.today/20241102160153/https://www.newarab.com/news/israeli-soldier-can-no-longer-eat-meat-after-killing-gaza |archive-date=2 November 2024}}
}}</ref>
[[File:Al-Tabieen school massacre 05.jpg|thumb|Bags of burned, dismembered limbs from the 10 August 2024 [[Al-Tabaeen school attack|Israeli airstrike on the Al-Tabaeen School]], which was hosting [[Internally displaced person|displaced]] sheltering Palestinians.|286x286px]]
The proportion of women and children among the dead is disputed,<ref name="Horton et al.">{{Cite news |last1=Horton |first1=Jake |last2=Sardarizadeh |first2=Shayan |last3=Durbin |first3=Adam |date=16 May 2024 |title=Gaza war: Why is the UN citing lower death toll for women and children? |url=https://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-69014893
