|language=en-GB}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |last=Ioanes |first=Ellen |date=17 May 2024 |title=The controversy over Gaza's death toll, explained |url=https://www.vox.com/world-politics/2024/5/17/24159263/gaza-deaths-israel-hamas-hospital-ministry-health |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240625225820/https://www.vox.com/world-politics/2024/5/17/24159263/gaza-deaths-israel-hamas-hospital-ministry-health |archive-date=25 June 2024 |access-date=12 July 2024 |website=[[Vox (website)|Vox]]}}</ref> but the names, gender, and age of 60,000+ of the victims are known and published.<ref name="techforpalestine-kills">{{cite web |url=https://data.techforpalestine.org/docs/killed-in-gaza/ |title=Killed in Gaza |website=[[Tech for Palestine]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251231024151/https://data.techforpalestine.org/docs/killed-in-gaza/ |archive-date=31 December 2025}}</ref> On 7 May 2024, total deaths quoted by the UN were 34,735, of which 24,686 are fully identified: 52% women and children, 8% elderly of all genders, and 40% men.<ref name="Horton et al." /> In November 2024, the UN published an analysis covering 8,119 fatalities that were verified by at least three independent sources, between November 2023 and April 2024, with 70% of them women and children.{{sfn|Saric|2024}} As of 31 August 2024, per the Gaza Ministry of Health, the number of fatalities had risen to 40,691, 34,344 identified by name: 17,652 (51%) women and children, 2,955 (9%) elderly of all genders (defined as those aged 60 or older), and 13,737 (40%) men.<ref>{{cite news |last=Zerrouky |first=Madjid |date=21 September 2024 |title=Gaza's Health Ministry reveals names of several thousand dead, over 11,355 of them are minors |url=https://www.lemonde.fr/en/international/article/2024/09/21/gaza-s-health-ministry-reveals-names-of-several-thousand-dead-over-11-355-of-them-are-minors_6726814_4.html |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240926222850/https://www.lemonde.fr/en/international/article/2024/09/21/gaza-s-health-ministry-reveals-names-of-several-thousand-dead-over-11-355-of-them-are-minors_6726814_4.html |archive-date=26 September 2024 |access-date=23 September 2024 |work=[[Le Monde]]}}</ref>{{sfn|Graham-Harrison|2024b}}<ref>{{Cite news |date=31 August 2024 |title=Health official says polio vaccine campaign begins in war-torn Gaza |url=https://www.france24.com/en/live-news/20240831-health-official-says-polio-vaccine-campaign-begins-in-war-torn-gaza |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240923003419/https://www.france24.com/en/live-news/20240831-health-official-says-polio-vaccine-campaign-begins-in-war-torn-gaza |archive-date=23 September 2024 |access-date=23 September 2024 |work=[[France 24]] |agency=[[Agence France-Presse]]}}</ref> A year later (31 July 2025), per the Gaza Ministry of Health, the number of fatalities identified by name reached 60,199: 28,728 (48%) were women and children, 2,928 (5%) were elderly of all genders (defined as those aged 65 or older), and 28,543 (47%) were men. A minimum of 18,457 children had been killed since October 2023.<ref name="techforpalestine-kills" /> In November 2024, the Gaza Health Ministry reported that 1,410 Gazan families had been completely erased from the civil registry as a result of Israeli bombings.<ref>{{Cite news |last=Saab |first=Sheren Falah |title=Entire Families Were Crushed in Gaza by Israeli Airstrikes. Not Even Memories Remain |work=[[Haaretz]] |date=5 December 2024 |url=https://www.haaretz.com/middle-east-news/palestinians/2024-12-05/ty-article-magazine/.premium/entire-families-crushed-in-gaza-by-israeli-airstrikes-not-even-memories-remain/00000193-92bf-dfe8-a5db-fbff98170000 |access-date=12 December 2024 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20241206080712/https://www.haaretz.com/middle-east-news/palestinians/2024-12-05/ty-article-magazine/.premium/entire-families-crushed-in-gaza-by-israeli-airstrikes-not-even-memories-remain/00000193-92bf-dfe8-a5db-fbff98170000 |archive-date=6 December 2024}}</ref> Data collection has become increasingly difficult for the Gaza Health Ministry due to the destruction of infrastructure.<ref name="KhatibMcKeeYusuf" /> The ministry has had to supplement its usual reporting based on hospital dead with other sources of information,<ref name="KhatibMcKeeYusuf" /> including reports by the media and first responders as well as families and widows, who must formally register their husbands' deaths to qualify for government assistance.<ref>{{Cite news |last=van der Merwe |first=Ben |date=4 April 2024 |title=Israel-Hamas war: Gaza's morgue network has effectively collapsed – how are they recording their dead? |url=https://news.sky.com/story/israel-hamas-war-health-system-collapse-in-gaza-leaves-authorities-struggling-to-count-the-dead-13107279 |access-date=26 July 2024 |work=[[Sky News]] |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240424190142/https://news.sky.com/story/israel-hamas-war-health-system-collapse-in-gaza-leaves-authorities-struggling-to-count-the-dead-13107279 |archive-date=24 April 2024}}</ref> Professor Mike Spagat found an urgent need for a transparent methodology to reconcile its top-line death numbers—34,535 as of 30 April 2024—with its detailed breakdowns, including only those of the dead who were fully identified, summing to 24,653 on the same date.<ref name="Spagat 2024a" /> By August 2025, this gap between the number of victims and the number of fully identified vicitms became smaller (about 62,000 vs. about 60,000), as more victims were identified.<ref>{{cite web | url=https://english.wafa.ps/Pages/Details/160545 | title=Gaza death toll surges to 62,192 as Israel continues the genocide | website=Wafa | date=21 August 2025 }}</ref> The ministry's figures for the total number killed have been contested by Israeli authorities but accepted as accurate by Israeli intelligence services, the UN, and the [[World Health Organization]].<ref name="KhatibMcKeeYusuf" /> More recently, ''The Guardian'' has reported that a classified IDF database registered 8,900 killed militants. This and GHM's data imply a civilian death rate of 83%, which exceeds that of any conflict since 1989 except the [[Rwandan genocide]], the [[Siege of Mariupol]], and the [[Siege of Srebrenica]].<ref>{{cite news |last1=Graham-Harrison |first1=Emma |last2=Abraham |first2=Yuval |date=21 August 2025 |title=Revealed: Israeli military's own data indicates civilian death rate of 83% in Gaza war |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/ng-interactive/2025/aug/21/revealed-israeli-militarys-own-data-indicates-civilian-death-rate-of-83-in-gaza-war |access-date=22 August 2025 |work=[[The Guardian]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250821135825/https://www.theguardian.com/world/ng-interactive/2025/aug/21/revealed-israeli-militarys-own-data-indicates-civilian-death-rate-of-83-in-gaza-war |archive-date=21 August 2025}}</ref> The IDF denied this, saying the figures were inaccurate and inconsistent with its data.<ref>{{cite news |title=IDF denies report claiming that its own database found that vast majority of Gaza dead were civilians |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/idf-denies-report-claiming-that-its-own-database-found-that-vast-majority-of-gaza-dead-were-civilians/ |access-date=6 November 2025 |work=[[The Times of Israel]] |date=21 August 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251008091647/https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/idf-denies-report-claiming-that-its-own-database-found-that-vast-majority-of-gaza-dead-were-civilians/ |archive-date=8 October 2025}}</ref>
A 2025 paper on the Gaza war estimated 64,260 deaths from traumatic injury between October 2023 and 30 June 2024, and likely exceeding 70,000 by October 2024, with 59.1% being women, children and the elderly. It concluded that the GHM undercounted trauma-related deaths by 41% in its report, and also noted that its findings "underestimate the full impact of the military operation in Gaza, as they do not account for non-trauma-related deaths resulting from health service disruption, food insecurity, and inadequate water and sanitation."{{sfn|Jamaluddine|Abukmail|Aly|Campbell|2025}} A comparable estimate for traumatic injury deaths was around 80,000 for January 2025.{{sfn|Bloxham|2025|p=23}} A February study in ''[[The Lancet]]'' estimated that life expectancy in the Gaza Strip between October 2023 and September 2024 decreased by 34.9 years, excluding indirect deaths. The study also used census and registration data to assess the reliability of the Gaza Health Ministry's death count, and found no substantial errors.{{sfn|Guillot|Draidi|Cetorelli|Monteiro Da Silva|2025|pp=478–485}}

In May 2025, finance minister [[Bezalel Smotrich]] claimed that Israel was targeting Hamas's civilian workers, saying, "We're eliminating ministers, bureaucrats, money handlers—everyone who holds up Hamas's civilian rule."{{sfn|Shpigel|2025}} Killing civilian members of Hamas is in itself illegal.{{sfn|Jamshidi|2024b|p=}}{{page needed|date=October 2025}}

Starting in June 2025, IDF soldiers said they were ordered to [[2025 Gaza Strip aid distribution killings|shoot at]] crowds of Palestinians near [[Gaza Humanitarian Foundation]] aid sites,<ref>{{cite news|last1=Hasson |first1=Nir |last2=Kubovich |first2=Yaniv |last3=Peleg |first3=Bar |date=27 June 2025 |title='It's a Killing Field': IDF Soldiers Ordered to Shoot Deliberately at Unarmed Gazans Waiting for Humanitarian Aid |url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2025-06-27/ty-article-magazine/.premium/idf-soldiers-ordered-to-shoot-deliberately-at-unarmed-gazans-waiting-for-humanitarian-aid/00000197-ad8e-de01-a39f-ffbe33780000 |work=[[Haaretz]] |access-date=14 July 2025 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20250714035002/https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2025-06-27/ty-article-magazine/.premium/idf-soldiers-ordered-to-shoot-deliberately-at-unarmed-gazans-waiting-for-humanitarian-aid/00000197-ad8e-de01-a39f-ffbe33780000 |archive-date=14 July 2025}}</ref> killing over 1,000 people.<ref>{{cite news |date=23 July 2025 |title=Israeli forces have killed over 1,000 aid-seekers in Gaza since May, the U.N. says |url=https://www.npr.org/2025/07/23/nx-s1-5477365/israel-gaza-aid-casualties |work=[[NPR]] |agency=[[Associated Press]] |access-date=30 July 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250729010824/https://www.npr.org/2025/07/23/nx-s1-5477365/israel-gaza-aid-casualties |archive-date=29 July 2025}}</ref> Amnesty International alleged Israel was trying to restrict aid to starve and inflict genocide upon the Palestinians.<ref>{{cite web |date=3 July 2025 |title=Gaza: Evidence points to Israel's continued use of starvation to inflict genocide against Palestinians |url=https://www.amnesty.org/en/latest/news/2025/07/gaza-evidence-points-to-israels-continued-use-of-starvation-to-inflict-genocide-against-palestinians/ |website=[[Amnesty International]] |access-date=14 July 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250704213128/https://www.amnesty.org/en/latest/news/2025/07/gaza-evidence-points-to-israels-continued-use-of-starvation-to-inflict-genocide-against-palestinians/ |archive-date=4 July 2025}}</ref>

In November 2025, a study by the [[Max Planck Institute for Demographic Research]] estimated that the total number of violent deaths in Gaza was between 100,000 and 126,000, of which 27% were children under 15 years old, and 24% women.<ref>{{Cite web |date=25 November 2025 |title=Gaza: study reveals unprecedented losses of life and life expectancy |url=https://www.mpg.de/25778228/1125-defo-gaza-study-reveals-unprecedented-losses-of-life-and-life-expectancy-154642-x |access-date=2 December 2025 |website=[[Max-Planck-Gesellschaft]] |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251222030059/https://www.mpg.de/25778228/1125-defo-gaza-study-reveals-unprecedented-losses-of-life-and-life-expectancy-154642-x |archive-date=22 December 2025}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |last=Endt |first=Christian |date=24 November 2025 |title=Kriegstote im Gazastreifen: Mehr als 100.000 Tote im Gazakrieg |trans-title=War deaths in the Gaza Strip: More than 100,000 dead in the Gaza war |url=https://www.zeit.de/politik/ausland/2025-11/kriegstote-gazastreifen-opferzahlen-schaetzung |access-date=21 December 2025 |work=[[Die Zeit]] |language=de-DE |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251212153644/https://www.zeit.de/politik/ausland/2025-11/kriegstote-gazastreifen-opferzahlen-schaetzung |archive-date=12 December 2025}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |last=Hauenstein |first=Hanno |date=1 December 2025 |title=Max-Planck-Institut zählt 126.000 Gaza-Tote: Was heißt das für den Genozid? |trans-title=Max Planck Institute counts 126,000 Gaza dead: What does that mean for the genocide? |url=https://www.freitag.de/autoren/hanno-hauenstein/max-planck-institut-zaehlt-126-000-gaza-tote-was-heisst-das-fuer-den-genozid |access-date=2 December 2025 |work=[[Der Freitag]] |language=de |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251210014016/https://www.freitag.de/autoren/hanno-hauenstein/max-planck-institut-zaehlt-126-000-gaza-tote-was-heisst-das-fuer-den-genozid |archive-date=10 December 2025}}</ref>

=== Indirect deaths ===
[[File:Mother cries for her 4-year-old daughter, who lost her life due to malnutrition and lack of treatment due to the war on Gaza, Gaza Strip.jpg|thumb|Mother cries for her 4-year-old daughter, who died due to [[malnutrition]] and lack of treatment]]
Rasha Khatib, [[Martin McKee]], and [[Salim Yusuf]] published an estimate of the number of deaths, directly or indirectly caused by the conflict, that as of July 2024 had already occurred or would occur in the coming months and years. Indirect Palestinian deaths from disease are expected to be much higher due to the intensity of the conflict, destruction of healthcare infrastructure, lack of food, water, shelter, and safe places for civilians to flee, and reduction in [[UNRWA]] funding. They estimated that the total conflict-related deaths in Gaza will likely be four to 16 times higher than the reported death toll. By multiplying the reported deaths by five, they argued that "186,000 or even more deaths could be attributable to the current conflict in Gaza".<ref name="KhatibMcKeeYusuf">{{harvnb|Khatib|McKee|Yusuf|2024}}: "Armed conflicts have indirect health implications beyond the direct harm from violence. Even if the conflict ends immediately, there will continue to be many indirect deaths in the coming months and years from causes such as reproductive, communicable, and non-communicable diseases. The total death toll is expected to be large given the intensity of this conflict; destroyed health-care infrastructure; severe shortages of food, water, and shelter; the population's inability to flee to safe places; and the loss of funding to UNRWA, one of the very few humanitarian organisations still active in the Gaza Strip. In recent conflicts, such indirect deaths range from three to 15 times the number of direct deaths. Applying a conservative estimate of four indirect deaths per one direct death to the 37,396 deaths reported, it is not implausible to estimate that up to 186,000 or even more deaths could be attributable to the current conflict in Gaza. Using the 2022 Gaza Strip population estimate of 2,375,259, this would translate to 7.9% of the total population in the Gaza Strip."</ref> Spagat wrote that their estimate "lacks a solid foundation and is implausible",<ref>{{cite web |last=Spagat |first=Mike |date=10 July 2024 |title=A critical analysis of The Lancet's letter "Counting the Dead in Gaza: Difficult but Essential". Professor Mike Spagat reviews the claim the total Gaza death toll may reach upwards of 186,000 |url=https://aoav.org.uk/2024/a-critical-analysis-of-the-lancets-letter-counting-the-dead-in-gaza-difficult-but-essential-professor-mike-spagat-reviews-the-claim-the-total-gaza-death-toll-may-reach-upwards-of-186000/ |access-date=10 July 2024 |website=Action On Armed Violence |language=en-US |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240710190128/https://aoav.org.uk/2024/a-critical-analysis-of-the-lancets-letter-counting-the-dead-in-gaza-difficult-but-essential-professor-mike-spagat-reviews-the-claim-the-total-gaza-death-toll-may-reach-upwards-of-186000/ |archive-date=10 July 2024}}</ref><ref name="Bigg 2024">{{cite news |last=Bigg |first=Matthew Mpoke |date=11 July 2024 |title=Fighting Isn't the Only Killer of Gazans Amid the War, Researchers Say |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2024/07/11/world/middleeast/gaza-war-death-toll-lancet.html |url-status=live |url-access=subscription |access-date=11 July 2024 |work=[[The New York Times]] |language=en-US |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240712123712/https://www.nytimes.com/2024/07/11/world/middleeast/gaza-war-death-toll-lancet.html%20 |archive-date=12 July 2024}}</ref> but it was "fair to call attention to the fact that not all of the deaths are going to be direct violent ones", and has called the death toll in Gaza "staggeringly high".<ref name="Horton et al."/><ref name="Bigg 2024"/> [[Donald Bloxham]] also notes that most deaths have been "indirect deaths" in various wars and that the "systematic obstruction of supplies into Gaza" is an Israeli policy, which makes calling these deaths "indirect" incorrect.<ref name="Bloxham_2025">{{harvnb|Bloxham|2025|pp=23–24}}: "When considering the total 'excess mortality,' we need to add the Palestinians who have died because of the blockade in combination with the IDF's destruction of health and sanitation and food infrastructure. As public health experts noted, in many wars, 'most deaths' are 'due to the indirect [sic] impacts of war: malnutrition, communicable disease, exacerbations of noncommunicable disease, [and] maternal and infant disorders.'117 'Indirect' would be the wrong word for this conflict given the nature of Israeli policies, including the systematic obstruction of supplies into Gaza."</ref>

An October 2024 letter by US healthcare workers who had served in Gaza since 7 October 2023 tried to estimate the number of Gazans who had died of starvation based on publicly available IPC reports.<ref>{{cite web |title=USA Letter |date=2 October 2024 |url=https://www.gazahealthcareletters.org/usa-letter-oct-2-2024 |access-date=21 October 2024 |website=Gaza Healthcare Letters |language=en-US |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20241009234500/https://www.gazahealthcareletters.org/usa-letter-oct-2-2024 |archive-date=9 October 2024}}</ref> It said the most conservative estimate was that at least 62,413 people in Gaza had died from starvation, most of them young children; this estimate was based on the assumption that catastrophic (level 5) food insecurity results in a death rate of at least 2 deaths per 10,000 people per day.{{#tag:ref|Per the IPC manual, the starvation death rate does not necessarily have to be that high (does not have to be at least 2 deaths per 10,000 people per day) to declare catastrophic (level 5) food insecurity. However, it does need to be that high to declare famine.|group=lower-alpha}} The physicians also estimated that at least 5,000 people had died from lack of access to care for chronic diseases.<ref>{{cite news |last=Hurwitz |first=Sophie |date=8 October 2024 |url=https://www.motherjones.com/politics/2024/10/us-israel-funding-gaza-palestine-deaths-october-100000-17-billion/ |title=Report: In One Year, More Than 100,000 Deaths in Gaza—Aided by $17.9 Billion From the US |work=[[Mother Jones (magazine)|Mother Jones]] |access-date=17 October 2024 |quote=Brown University's Costs of War Project calculated "the money that's spent on war, and the toll on human lives" after a year of war in Gaza. The numbers are staggering. |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20241010053644/https://www.motherjones.com/politics/2024/10/us-israel-funding-gaza-palestine-deaths-october-100000-17-billion/ |archive-date=10 October 2024}}</ref><ref name="WatsonInstituteEstimatedDeaths">{{harvnb|Stamatopoulou-Robbins|2024}}: "In addition to killing people directly through traumatic injuries, wars cause "indirect deaths" by destroying, damaging, or causing deterioration of economic, social, psychological and health conditions. Most expansively, this report describes the causal pathways that can be expected to lead to far larger numbers of indirect deaths. These deaths result from diseases and other population-level health effects that stem from war's destruction of public infrastructure and livelihood sources, reduced access to water and sanitation, environmental damage, and other such factors. This report builds on a foundation of previous Costs of War research for its framework and methodology in covering the most significant chains of impact, or causal pathways, to indirect war deaths in Gaza and the West Bank. Unlike in combat, these deaths do not necessarily occur immediately or in the close aftermath of the battles which many observers focus on. While it will take years to assess the full extent of these population-level health effects, they will inevitably lead to far higher numbers of deaths than direct violence."</ref><ref name="GazaHealthcareLettersEstimatedDeaths">{{cite web |url=https://static1.squarespace.com/static/66e083452b3cbf4bbd719aa2/t/66fcd754b472610b6335d66f/1727846228615/Appendix+20241002.pdf |title=Appendix to letter of October 2, 2024 re: American physicians observations from the Gaza Strip since October 7, 2023 |author=<!--Not stated--> |date=2 October 2024 |website=Gaza Healthcare Letters |access-date=17 October 2024 |quote=These are the most conservative estimates of the death toll that can be made with the given available data as of September 30, 2024. It is highly likely that the real number of deaths in Gaza from this conflict is far higher than this most conservative estimate. Without an immediate ceasefire the death toll will only continue to mount, especially among young children. |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20241007173405/https://static1.squarespace.com/static/66e083452b3cbf4bbd719aa2/t/66fcd754b472610b6335d66f/1727846228615/Appendix+20241002.pdf |archive-date=7 October 2024}}</ref> The indirect death estimates in two studies reviewed by ''The Economist'' implied that the life expectancy in Gaza has fallen by 35 years, rivalling the [[Rwandan genocide]] in absolute terms.<ref>{{cite news |date=6 August 2025 |title=How much of Gaza is left standing? |url=https://www.economist.com/interactive/graphic-detail/2025/08/06/how-much-of-gaza-is-left-standing |access-date=8 August 2025 |newspaper=[[The Economist]] |archive-url=https://archive.today/20250807165501/https://www.economist.com/interactive/graphic-detail/2025/08/06/how-much-of-gaza-is-left-standing |archive-date=7 August 2025}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |date=8 August 2025 |title=How much of Gaza is left standing? True toll may be even greater than official reports suggest |url=https://www.smh.com.au/world/middle-east/how-much-of-gaza-is-left-standing-true-toll-may-be-even-greater-than-official-reports-suggest-20250808-p5mlhn.html |access-date=8 August 2025 |work=[[The Sydney Morning Herald]] |language=en |archive-url=https://archive.today/20250808060545/https://www.smh.com.au/world/middle-east/how-much-of-gaza-is-left-standing-true-toll-may-be-even-greater-than-official-reports-suggest-20250808-p5mlhn.html |archive-date=8 August 2025}}</ref>

=== Starvation and blockade ===
{{main|Gaza Strip famine|Blockade of the Gaza Strip}}

{{#invoke:Multiple image|

In February 2024, [[Human Rights Watch]] and [[Amnesty International]] both released statements declaring Israel had failed to comply with the ICJ's 26 January ruling to prevent genocide by [[Israeli blockade of the Gaza Strip (2023–present)|blocking aid]] from entering Gaza.<ref name="Human Rights Watch Blockade" /><ref name="Amnesty International Blockade" /><ref>{{cite news |date=26 February 2024 |title=Has Israel complied with ICJ order in Gaza genocide case? |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2024/2/26/has-israel-complied-with-icj-order-in-gaza-genocide-case |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240305002212/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2024/2/26/has-israel-complied-with-icj-order-in-gaza-genocide-case |archive-date=5 March 2024 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]]}}</ref> A Refugees International report found that Israel had "consistently and groundlessly impeded aid operations within Gaza".{{sfn|Johnson|2024b}} The historian Melanie Tanielian argues that starvation and blockade should be foregrounded as methods of genocide alongside mass bombing.{{sfn|Tanielian|2024|pp=3–4}} In an April report, [[B'Tselem]] called the unfolding famine "the product of a deliberate and conscious Israeli policy".{{sfn|Sultany|2024|p=7}}<ref>{{cite report |url=https://www.btselem.org/publications/202404_manufacturing_famine |title=Manufacturing Famine: Israel is Committing the War Crime of Starvation in the Gaza Strip |date=April 2024 |publisher=[[B'Tselem]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240719222458/https://www.btselem.org/publications/202404_manufacturing_famine |archive-date=19 July 2024}}</ref>

In October 2023, the [[World Food Program]] warned of Gaza's dwindling food supply,{{sfn|Tanielian|2024|pp=6–7}} and in December, alongside the UN, it reported that more than half of Gaza's population was "starving", fewer than one in ten were eating every day, and 48% were suffering "extreme hunger".<ref>{{cite news |last=Singh |first=Namita |date=10 December 2023 |title=UN says half of Gaza's population is now starving |url=https://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/middle-east/israel-gaza-war-palestinians-starving-un-wfp-b2461488.html |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240119132024/https://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/middle-east/israel-gaza-war-palestinians-starving-un-wfp-b2461488.html |archive-date=19 January 2024 |access-date=13 December 2023 |work=[[The Independent]]}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Siddiqui |first1=Usaid |last2=Pietromarchi |first2=Virginia |last3=Quillen |first3=Stephen |date=10 December 2023 |title=Israel-Hamas war updates: Fierce battles rage in southern and northern Gaza |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2023/12/10/israel-hamas-war-live-no-safe-place-in-gaza-as-severe-hunger-spreads |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240226131329/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2023/12/10/israel-hamas-war-live-no-safe-place-in-gaza-as-severe-hunger-spreads |archive-date=26 February 2024 |access-date=13 December 2023 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]]}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last=Ebrahim |first=Nadeen |date=5 December 2023 |title='It's chaos': Starving Gazans dig for food, supplies under the rubble |url=https://www.cnn.com/2023/12/05/middleeast/gaza-bakery-hunger-israel-hamas-war-intl/index.html |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240116152114/https://www.cnn.com/2023/12/05/middleeast/gaza-bakery-hunger-israel-hamas-war-intl/index.html |archive-date=16 January 2024 |access-date=13 December 2023 |work=[[CNN]]}}</ref> Palestinian Foreign Minister [[Riyad al-Maliki]] referred to "Israel's deliberate use of starvation as a weapon of war against the people it occupied"; an Israeli official called the charge "blood-libellous" and "delusional".<ref>{{cite news |last=Tétrault-Farber |first=Gabrielle |date=13 December 2023 |title=Palestinian minister accuses Israel of starving Gazans; Israel says charge 'obscene' |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/palestinian-foreign-minister-accuses-israel-deliberately-starving-gazans-2023-12-12/ |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240228113139/https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/palestinian-foreign-minister-accuses-israel-deliberately-starving-gazans-2023-12-12/ |archive-date=28 February 2024 |access-date=13 December 2023 |work=[[Reuters]]}}</ref> In December 2023, Human Rights Watch found that Israel was using starvation as a weapon of war by deliberately denying access to food and water.<ref>{{cite web |date=18 December 2023 |title=Israel: Starvation Used as Weapon of War in Gaza |url=https://www.hrw.org/news/2023/12/18/israel-starvation-used-weapon-war-gaza |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240307221127/https://www.hrw.org/news/2023/12/18/israel-starvation-used-weapon-war-gaza |archive-date=7 March 2024 |access-date=1 January 2024 |publisher=[[Human Rights Watch]]}}</ref> In January 2024, UN experts accused Israel of "destroying Gaza's food system and using food as a weapon against the Palestinian people".<ref>{{cite web |date=16 January 2024 |title=Over one hundred days into the war, Israel destroying Gaza's food system and weaponising food, say UN human rights experts |url=https://www.ohchr.org/en/press-releases/2024/01/over-one-hundred-days-war-israel-destroying-gazas-food-system-and |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240226103315/https://www.ohchr.org/en/press-releases/2024/01/over-one-hundred-days-war-israel-destroying-gazas-food-system-and |archive-date=26 February 2024 |access-date=26 January 2024 |website=[[Office of the United Nations High Commissioner for Human Rights]] |publisher=[[United Nations]]}}</ref> In February 2024, finance minister Bezalel Smotrich personally blocked US-funded shipments of flour from entering Gaza, in violation of promises Israel had made to the US government.<ref>{{cite news |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/finance-minister-blocks-flour-shipments-from-reaching-gaza/ |title=Smotrich blocks flour shipments from reaching Gaza, in breach of Israeli pledge to US |newspaper=[[The Times of Israel]] |date=14 February 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240319130727/https://www.timesofisrael.com/finance-minister-blocks-flour-shipments-from-reaching-gaza/ |archive-date=19 March 2024}}</ref>

In early 2024, the [[United Nations special rapporteur]] on the right to food [[Michael Fakhri]] said that Israel is "culpable" of genocide because "Israel has announced its intention to destroy the Palestinian people, in whole or in part, simply for being Palestinian" and because Israel was denying food to Palestinians by halting humanitarian aid and "intentionally" destroying <blockquote>small-scale fishing vessels, greenhouses and orchards in Gaza ... We have never seen a civilian population made to go so hungry so quickly and so completely, that is the consensus among starvation experts. Israel is not just targeting civilians, it is trying to damn the future of the Palestinian people by harming their children.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Lakhani |first1=Nina |date=27 February 2024 |title=Israel is deliberately starving Palestinians, UN rights expert says |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2024/feb/27/un-israel-food-starvation-palestinians-war-crime-genocide |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240228041844/https://www.theguardian.com/world/2024/feb/27/un-israel-food-starvation-palestinians-war-crime-genocide |archive-date=28 February 2024 |newspaper=[[The Guardian]]}}</ref></blockquote> After the ICJ ruling, the number of aid trucks Israel allowed into Gaza dropped by 40%.<ref>{{cite news |last=Marsi |first=Federica |date=27 February 2024 |title=How much aid has entered Gaza? |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/2/27/israels-war-on-gaza-live-biden-comments-turn-focus-back-to-gaza-ceasefire?update=2735412 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240227143519/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/2/27/israels-war-on-gaza-live-biden-comments-turn-focus-back-to-gaza-ceasefire?update=2735412 |archive-date=27 February 2024 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]]}}</ref> In the ICJ's March reaffirmation of provisional measures, the court highlighted the "unprecedented levels of food insecurity experienced by Palestinians in the Gaza Strip over recent weeks, as well as the increasing risks of epidemics",{{sfn|Sultany|2024|p=5}} acknowledging that since the Court's January order there had been a "lack of Israeli compliance" resulting in "the catastrophic living conditions" deteriorating further.{{sfn|Sultany|2024|p=6}}

In March 2024, 12 Israeli human rights organisations signed an open letter accusing Israel of failing to abide by the ICJ ruling to prevent genocide by facilitating the delivery of humanitarian aid.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Beaumont |first1=Peter |last2=Burke |first2=Jason |date=11 March 2024 |title=Israeli human rights groups accuse country of failing to abide by ICJ's Gaza aid ruling |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2024/mar/11/israeli-human-rights-groups-icj-gaza-aid-ruling |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240311204045/https://www.theguardian.com/world/2024/mar/11/israeli-human-rights-groups-icj-gaza-aid-ruling |archive-date=11 March 2024 |work=[[The Guardian]]}}</ref>{{sfn|Johnson|2024a}} In April the UN special rapporteur on the right to health [[Tlaleng Mofokeng]] said Israel was "killing and causing irreparable harm against Palestinian civilians with its bombardments", adding, "They are also knowingly and intentionally imposing [[Gaza Strip famine|famine]]" and accusing Israel of "genocide".<ref name="Al-Monitor-2024-04-22">{{cite web |date=22 April 2024 |title=Gaza health system 'completely obliterated': UN expert |url=https://www.al-monitor.com/originals/2024/04/gaza-health-system-completely-obliterated-un-expert |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240518013104/https://www.al-monitor.com/originals/2024/04/gaza-health-system-completely-obliterated-un-expert |archive-date=18 May 2024 |access-date=4 May 2024 |website=Al-Monitor |language=en |agency=[[Agence France-Presse]]}}</ref>

In October 2024, Israel had reportedly adopted a modified version of the [[Israeli Generals' Plan|Generals' Plan]].<ref>{{cite news |last=Krever |first=Mike |date=12 October 2024 |title=After mulling siege plan, Israel ramps up military push in northern Gaza |url=https://edition.cnn.com/2024/10/12/middleeast/israel-military-push-northern-gaza-intl/index.html |access-date=13 October 2024 |work=[[CNN]] |url-status=live |archive-url=https://archive.today/20241013142409/https://edition.cnn.com/2024/10/12/middleeast/israel-military-push-northern-gaza-intl/index.html |archive-date=13 October 2024}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last=Bowen |first=Jeremy |date=12 October 2024 |title=Israeli attack on northern Gaza hints at retired general's 'surrender or starve' plan for war |url-status=live |url=https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/c1e82yy0wxno |access-date=12 October 2024 |work=[[BBC News]] |archive-url=https://archive.today/20241012161158/https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/c1e82yy0wxno |archive-date=12 October 2024}}</ref>{{#tag:ref|Some Israeli officials denied the plan had been adopted; however, an official familiar with the situation stated that some aspects of the plan were already in progress.<ref>{{cite news |date=13 October 2024 |title=Netanyahu mulls plan to empty northern Gaza of civilians |url=https://www.politico.com/news/2024/10/13/netanyahu-mulls-plan-to-empty-northern-gaza-of-civilians-00183574 |work=[[Politico]] |agency=[[Associated Press]] |url-status=live |access-date=14 October 2024 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20241014042030/https://www.politico.com/news/2024/10/13/netanyahu-mulls-plan-to-empty-northern-gaza-of-civilians-00183574 |archive-date=14 October 2024}}</ref>|group=lower-alpha}} The proposed plan included orders for all residents of northern Gaza to leave within a week; a full siege on water, food, and fuel; and then the arrest or killing of all who remained.<ref>{{Cite magazine|last1=Rapoport |first1=Meron |date=17 September 2024 |title=A plan to liquidate northern Gaza is gaining steam |url=https://www.972mag.com/northern-gaza-liquidation-scenario-eiland-rabi/ |magazine=[[+972 Magazine]] |access-date=14 October 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20241010022043/https://www.972mag.com/northern-gaza-liquidation-scenario-eiland-rabi/ |archive-date=10 October 2024}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title=North Gaza siege: Netanyahu considers plan to starve out Hamas fighters |url=https://www.jpost.com/israel-hamas-war/article-821301 |work=[[The Jerusalem Post]] |date=23 September 2024 |url-status=live |access-date=14 October 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20241002192315/https://www.jpost.com/israel-hamas-war/article-821301 |archive-date=2 October 2024}}</ref> By mid-October 2024, Israel had ordered the evacuation of northern Gaza and prevented the entry of humanitarian aid for almost two weeks.<ref>{{Cite news|last1=Rémy |first1=Jean-Philippe |date=9 October 2024 |title=Israel orders new evacuations in northern Gaza |url=https://www.lemonde.fr/en/international/article/2024/10/09/israel-orders-new-evacuations-in-northern-gaza_6728770_4.html |work=[[Le Monde]] |access-date=14 October 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20241009142142/https://www.lemonde.fr/en/international/article/2024/10/09/israel-orders-new-evacuations-in-northern-gaza_6728770_4.html |archive-date=9 October 2024}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Khadder |first1=Kareem |last2=Salman |first2=Abeer |last3=Kourdi |first3=Eyad |last4=Lockwood |first4=Pauline |date=11 October 2024 |title=UN says no food has entered northern Gaza since start of October, putting 1 million people at risk of starvation |url=https://www.cnn.com/2024/10/11/middleeast/food-northern-gaza-starvation-un-intl |work=[[CNN]] |access-date=14 October 2024 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20241102164249/https://www.cnn.com/2024/10/11/middleeast/food-northern-gaza-starvation-un-intl |archive-date=2 November 2024}}</ref> According to Stephen Devereux, avoidable deaths due to starvation as a result of Israeli policies "almost certainly constitutes a war crime and a crime against humanity".<ref>{{Cite web|last1=Devereux |first1=Stephen |date=5 November 2024 |doi=10.19088/IDS.2024.042 |title=Was There a Famine in Gaza in 2024? |publisher=[[Institute of Development Studies]] |url=https://www.ids.ac.uk/publications/was-there-a-famine-in-gaza-in-2024/ |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20241113004044/https://www.ids.ac.uk/publications/was-there-a-famine-in-gaza-in-2024/ |archive-date=13 November 2024}}</ref>

On 21 November 2024, the International Criminal Court [[International Criminal Court arrest warrants for Israeli leaders|issued arrest warrants]] for Israeli Prime Minister Benjamin Netanyahu and the former defence minister Yoav Gallant, asserting that the two "bear criminal responsibility for the war crime of starvation as a method of warfare".<ref>{{cite news |last1=Borger |first1=Julian |author1-link=Julian Borger |last2=Roth |first2=Andrew |date=21 November 2024 |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2024/nov/21/icc-issues-arrest-warrant-for-benjamin-netanyahu-israel |title=ICC issues arrest warrant for Benjamin Netanyahu for alleged Gaza war crimes |work=[[The Guardian]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20241205002406/https://www.theguardian.com/world/2024/nov/21/icc-issues-arrest-warrant-for-benjamin-netanyahu-israel |url-status=live |archive-date=5 December 2024}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Shotter |first1=James |last2=Ralph |first2=Oliver |date=21 November 2024 |url=https://www.ft.com/content/0b62f17a-97db-4817-90f8-f98adead79f0 |title=ICC issues arrest warrant for Israeli PM Benjamin Netanyahu |work=[[Financial Times]] |url-access=subscription |url-status=live |archive-url=https://archive.today/20241121233145/https://www.ft.com/content/0b62f17a-97db-4817-90f8-f98adead79f0 |archive-date=21 November 2024}}</ref><ref name="El Abdallah 2024">{{cite press release |last=El Abdallah |first=Fadi |date=21 November 2024 |url=https://www.icc-cpi.int/news/situation-state-palestine-icc-pre-trial-chamber-i-rejects-state-israels-challenges |title=Situation in the State of Palestine: ICC Pre-Trial Chamber I rejects the State of Israel's challenges to jurisdiction and issues warrants of arrest for Benjamin Netanyahu and Yoav Gallant |publisher=[[International Criminal Court]] |access-date=21 November 2024 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20241121130247/https://www.icc-cpi.int/news/situation-state-palestine-icc-pre-trial-chamber-i-rejects-state-israels-challenges |archive-date=21 November 2024 |url-status=live}}</ref>

Israel lifted restrictions on aid into Gaza in January–February 2025 during the first stage of [[January 2025 Gaza war ceasefire|the January ceasefire]]. But on 2 March, Israel announced that all humanitarian aid would be blocked indefinitely unless Hamas agreed to alter the terms of the ceasefire deal, which Hamas refused to do.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Rowlands |first1=Lyndal |last2=Adler |first2=Nils |last3=Quillem |first3=Stephen |last4=Motamedi |first4=Maziar |date=2 March 2025 |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2025/3/2/live-israel-us-propose-terms-to-extend-gaza-ceasefire-hamas-yet-to-reply?update=3549776 |title=Updates: Israel blocks all aid into Gaza after first phase of truce ends |newspaper=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250305214841/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2025/3/2/live-israel-us-propose-terms-to-extend-gaza-ceasefire-hamas-yet-to-reply?update=3549776 |archive-date=5 March 2025}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last=Doucet |first=Lyse |date=3 March 2025 |title=Gaza ceasefire in peril as Israel and Hamas hit impasse |url=https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/articles/ckgz7p85mdgo |newspaper=[[BBC News]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250305215154/https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/ckgz7p85mdgo |url-status=live |archive-date=5 March 2025}}</ref> Within four days, food supplies in Gaza had rapidly depleted while the price of food had more than doubled. Aid agencies such as [[Oxfam]] and [[UNICEF]] warned of mass starvation if the aid freeze continued. Oxfam policy lead Bushra Khalidi predicted "the total collapse of systems that sustain life".<ref>{{cite news |last1=Frankel |first1=Julia |last2=Magdy |first2=Samy |date=5 March 2025 |title=Israel's cutoff of supplies to Gaza sends prices soaring as aid stockpiles dwindle |url=https://apnews.com/article/israel-gaza-aid-cutoff-netanyahu-hunger-war-940ceea2c2b754d197a4f07c0cad86de |url-status=live |work=[[Associated Press]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250305215422/https://apnews.com/article/israel-gaza-aid-cutoff-netanyahu-hunger-war-940ceea2c2b754d197a4f07c0cad86de |archive-date=5 March 2025}}</ref> Lawyer Salah Abdel-Ati said Israel's actions were illegal under the [[Geneva Conventions]], which prohibits the destruction or withholding of essentials such as food in combat zones.<ref>{{cite news |last=Jalal |first=Rasha |date=5 March 2025 |title=Palestinians in Gaza fear threat of famine over Israel's Ramadan aid blockade |url=https://www.newarab.com/news/gazas-palestinians-fear-famine-over-israels-ramadan-aid-block |url-status=live |work=[[The New Arab]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250305215633/https://www.newarab.com/news/gazas-palestinians-fear-famine-over-israels-ramadan-aid-block |archive-date=5 March 2025}}</ref>

In May 2025, after blocking the import of all food, medicine, and fuel for two and a half months,<ref>{{cite news |date=25 May 2025 |title=Aid trucks going into Gaza are a "drop in the bucket as to what's needed," WFP director says |url=https://www.cbsnews.com/news/aid-trucks-gaza-world-food-program-israel-hamas/ |access-date=28 May 2025 |work=[[CBS News]] |language=en-US |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250528212442/https://www.cbsnews.com/news/aid-trucks-gaza-world-food-program-israel-hamas/ |archive-date=28 May 2025}}</ref> Netanyahu announced that Israel would allow "minimal humanitarian aid" into Gaza due to international pressure.{{sfn|Shpigel|2025}} Israel has proposed using private companies to distribute aid to the south of Gaza only. The plan is backed by the US, which has created the [[Gaza Humanitarian Foundation]] (GHF) to deliver aid without "Hamas stealing, looting or leveraging this assistance for its own ends". The United Nations aid chief [[Thomas Fletcher (diplomat)|Tom Fletcher]] criticised the plan, saying it "forces further displacement" and "makes aid conditional on political and military aims".{{sfn|Nichols|2025a}} Numerous Palestinians have been [[Rafah aid distribution killings|killed by Israeli forces]] while approaching GHF aid distribution points.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Tondo |first1=Lorenzo |last2=Tantesh |first2=Malak |date=3 June 2025 |title=At least 27 Palestinians killed by Israeli fire at food point, Gaza officials say |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2025/jun/03/palestinians-killed-israeli-fire-aid-point-gaza-officials-say |work=[[The Guardian]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250603172833/https://www.theguardian.com/world/2025/jun/03/palestinians-killed-israeli-fire-aid-point-gaza-officials-say |archive-date=3 June 2025}}</ref>

In August 2025, it was reported that Israel planned to surge aid to other parts of Gaza while cutting off all aid to Gaza City to force residents to evacuate while Israel takes over the city.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Nicholls |first1=Catherine |last2=Edwards |first2=Christian |last3=Vales |first3=Leinz |last4=Vogt |first4=Adrienne |date=8 August 2025 |title=Israel's security cabinet approves plan to take over Gaza City |url=https://www.cnn.com/world/live-news/israel-gaza-war-netanyahu-08-08-25#cme2gkxi000183b6tmv28m1yi |work=[[CNN]] |access-date=8 August 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250808143736/https://www.cnn.com/world/live-news/israel-gaza-war-netanyahu-08-08-25#cme2gkxi000183b6tmv28m1yi |archive-date=8 August 2025}}</ref> As of August 2025, projections show the entire population is experiencing "high levels of acute food insecurity", with about 641,000 people experiencing [[Integrated Food Security Phase Classification|catastrophic levels]].{{sfn|IPC Report August|2025|p=1}} The IPC confirmed famine is taking place in the [[Gaza Governorate]].{{sfn|IPC Report August|2025|p=1}}<ref>{{Cite news |last=Nichols |first=Michelle |date=22 August 2025 |title=Famine has struck Gaza, says global hunger monitor |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/famine-has-struck-gaza-says-global-hunger-monitor-2025-08-22/ |access-date=22 August 2025 |work=[[Reuters]] |language=en |archive-url=https://archive.today/20250822091426/https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/famine-has-struck-gaza-says-global-hunger-monitor-2025-08-22/ |archive-date=22 August 2025}}</ref>

Two weeks after the [[Gaza peace plan|October 2025 ceasefire]] came into effect, dozens of NGOs, including the [[Norwegian Refugee Council]] and [[Médecins Sans Frontières|Doctors Without Borders]], announced that Israel was arbitrarily blocking their shipments of aid to Gaza. World Health Organisation head Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus said, "the situation still remains catastrophic because what's entering is not enough" and "there is no dent in hunger because there is not enough food".<ref>{{cite web |title=Mounting alarm as Israeli authorities reject NGO applications to transport life saving aid into Gaza |website=[[Norwegian Refugee Council]] |date=23 October 2025 |url=https://www.nrc.no/news/2025/october/mounting-alarm-as-israeli-authorities-reject-ngo-applications-to-transport-life-saving-aid-into-gaza |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251108180034/https://www.nrc.no/news/2025/october/mounting-alarm-as-israeli-authorities-reject-ngo-applications-to-transport-life-saving-aid-into-gaza |archive-date=8 November 2025}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |first=Abby |last=Rogers |agency=[[Agence France-Presse]] and [[Reuters]] |title=Hunger crisis in Gaza is catastrophic despite ceasefire, WHO chief says |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |date=23 October 2025 |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/10/23/hunger-crisis-in-gaza-is-catastrophic-despite-ceasefire-who-chief-says |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251108180323/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/10/23/hunger-crisis-in-gaza-is-catastrophic-despite-ceasefire-who-chief-says |archive-date=8 November 2025}}</ref>

By December 2025, the food situation improved, with famine and catastrophic food insecurity (level 5) no longer happening; but 27% of the population still experienced emergency-level food insecurity (level 4) and another 50% of the population experienced crisis-level food insecurity (level 3).<ref>{{cite web |title=Humanitarian Situation Update #351 {{!}} Gaza Strip |website=occupied Palestinian territory {{!}} [[ReliefWeb]] |date=31 December 2025 |url=https://reliefweb.int/report/occupied-palestinian-territory/humanitarian-situation-update-351-gaza-strip |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251231080950/https://reliefweb.int/report/occupied-palestinian-territory/humanitarian-situation-update-351-gaza-strip |archive-date=31 December 2025}}</ref><ref>{{cite web |title=Gaza Strip: Acute Food Insecurity Situation for 16 October - 30 November 2025 and Projection for 1 December 2025 - 15 April 2026 |website=IPC - Integrated Food Security Phase Classification |date=19 December 2025 |url=https://www.ipcinfo.org/ipc-country-analysis/details-map/en/c/1159820/?iso3=PSE |archive-url= |archive-date=}}</ref> At the turn of the year, Israel's expulsion of Doctors Without Borders and several other humanitarian organizations from Gaza raised fears that the effects of malnutrition on the population would not be adequately treated or monitored; these organizations helped alleviate effects of famine/malnutrition by treating children with severe acute malnutrition.<ref>{{cite web |title=Inter-Agency Standing Committee (IASC) Statement: Revoke planned international NGO ban, humanitarian leaders urge Israeli authorities |website=occupied Palestinian territory {{!}} [[ReliefWeb]] |date=1 January 2026 |url=https://reliefweb.int/report/occupied-palestinian-territory/inter-agency-standing-committee-iasc-statement-revoke-planned-international-ngo-ban-humanitarian-leaders-urge-israeli-authorities |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20260102141932/https://reliefweb.int/report/occupied-palestinian-territory/inter-agency-standing-committee-iasc-statement-revoke-planned-international-ngo-ban-humanitarian-leaders-urge-israeli-authorities |archive-date=2 January 2026}}</ref><ref>{{cite web |title=53 International NGOs warn Israel's recent registration measures will impede critical humanitarian action |website=Médecins du Monde |date=2 January 2026 |url=https://www.medecinsdumonde.org/en/news/53-international-ngos-warn-israels-recent-registration-measures-will-impede-critical-humanitarian-action/ |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20260105221712/https://www.medecinsdumonde.org/en/news/53-international-ngos-warn-israels-recent-registration-measures-will-impede-critical-humanitarian-action/ |archive-date=5 January 2026}}</ref>

[[Mark Levene]] and Elyse Semerdjian locate the mass destruction of infrastructure within Israel's [[Dahiya doctrine]], implemented against Gaza since 2006, with Levene calling it [[urbicide]] and a tool of genocide.{{sfn|Levene|2024|pp=6–7}}{{sfn|Semerdjian|2024a|p=2}} In October 2024, [[Forensic Architecture]] concluded, "Israel's military campaign in Gaza is organised, systematic, and intended to destroy conditions of life and life-sustaining infrastructure".<ref>{{cite web |title=A Cartography of Genocide: Israel's Conduct in Gaza Since October 2023 |date=7 October 2024 |url=https://forensic-architecture.org/investigation/a-cartography-of-genocide |access-date=27 October 2024 |website=[[Forensic Architecture]] |archive-url=https://archive.today/20241028155707/https://forensic-architecture.org/investigation/a-cartography-of-genocide |archive-date=28 October 2024}}</ref>

In July 2025, ''[[The Guardian]]'' reported that "about 70% of the structures in Gaza are either completely destroyed or severely damaged". Israel was reportedly paying contractors up to 5,000 shekels per building demolished.<ref>{{Cite news |last=Mahdawi |first=Arwa |date=9 July 2025 |url=https://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2025/jul/09/bulldzoer-gaza-genocide-idf-meta |title=Seeking bulldozer drivers to demolish Gaza: how a genocide is being outsourced |newspaper=[[The Guardian]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250711034859/https://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2025/jul/09/bulldzoer-gaza-genocide-idf-meta |archive-date=11 July 2025}}</ref> In February 2025 it was reported that at least 15 children had died of [[hypothermia]] over the winter due to Israel's destruction of housing and power facilities.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Shurafa |first1=Wafaa |last2=Magdy |first2=Samy |date=26 February 2025 |url=https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-hamas-war-children-cold-death-3085913b482dc5e45edd221ceccb17b3 |title=Medics say 6 babies have died from the cold in Gaza as displaced people shelter in tents and rubble |work=[[Associated Press]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250226190710/https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-hamas-war-children-cold-death-3085913b482dc5e45edd221ceccb17b3 |archive-date=26 February 2025}}</ref> In May 2025, Netanyahu said, "we are destroying more and more homes, and Gazans have nowhere to return to. The only inevitable outcome will be the wish of Gazans to emigrate outside of the Gaza Strip."{{sfn|B'Tselem|2025|p=47}}

In a December 2024 report, Human Rights Watch accused Israel of committing acts of genocide in Gaza by targeting water and sanitation infrastructure and depriving Palestinians of adequate access to water. The report alleges that Israel intentionally damaged solar panels powering treatment plants, a reservoir, and warehouses, while blocking repair materials and fuel for generators, cutting electricity supplies, and attacking workers.<ref name="hrw-report">{{cite report |url=https://www.hrw.org/report/2024/12/19/extermination-and-acts-genocide/israel-deliberately-depriving-palestinians-gaza |title=Extermination and Acts of Genocide: Israel Deliberately Depriving Palestinians in Gaza of Water |url-status=live |date=19 December 2024 |publisher=[[Human Rights Watch]] |quote=Israeli authorities' and forces' actions to deprive the population of Gaza of access to water amount to acts of genocide under the Genocide Convention and the Rome Statute of the International Criminal Court. Specifically, their actions amount to deliberately inflicting conditions of life calculated to bring about the physical destruction of the Palestinian population in Gaza. Genocidal intent may also be inferred from Israeli authorities' and forces' continued actions to deprive Palestinians in Gaza of water, despite clear data and warnings from the United Nations since October and orders from the International Court of Justice calling for the provision of water since January, alongside Israeli authorities' statements, and therefore these acts may amount to the crime of genocide. |access-date=20 January 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250209092600/https://www.hrw.org/report/2024/12/19/extermination-and-acts-genocide/israel-deliberately-depriving-palestinians-gaza |archive-date=9 February 2025}}</ref><ref name="Berg2024">{{cite news |last=Berg |first=Raffi |date=19 December 2024 |title=HRW accuses Israel of acts of genocide over Gaza water access |url=https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/c75wqr0k3dyo |access-date=21 December 2024 |work=[[BBC News]] |language=en-GB |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20241220111016/https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/c75wqr0k3dyo |archive-date=20 December 2024 |url-status=live}}</ref> According to B'Tselem, Israel has destroyed 84% of Gaza's water facilities,{{sfn|B'Tselem|2025|p=35}} while in a report authored and published by the [[World Bank]], [[European Union]], and United Nations it was reported that 89% of Gaza's water, sanitation, and hygiene facilities had been destroyed or damaged.<ref>{{cite report |date=February 2025 |title=Gaza and West Bank Interim Rapid Damage and Needs Assessment |url=https://thedocs.worldbank.org/en/doc/133c3304e29086819c1119fe8e85366b-0280012025/original/Gaza-RDNA-final-med.pdf |publisher=[[World Bank]], [[European Union]], [[United Nations]] |page=37 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251218220355/https://thedocs.worldbank.org/en/doc/133c3304e29086819c1119fe8e85366b-0280012025/original/Gaza-RDNA-final-med.pdf |archive-date=18 December 2025}}</ref> UN Special Rapporteur [[Pedro Arrojo-Agudo]] called these attacks "an important part of a genocidal strategy."<ref>{{cite news |last=Lakhani |first=Nina |date=11 November 2025 |title=Israelis attacked Palestinian water sources over 250 times in five years, data reveals |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2025/nov/11/israel-attacks-palestine-water |work=[[The Guardian]] |access-date=11 November 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251231210533/https://www.theguardian.com/world/2025/nov/11/israel-attacks-palestine-water |archive-date=31 December 2025}}</ref>

Rafah, a city in the southern Gaza Strip, has been razed;<ref>{{cite news |last1=Hasson |first1=Nir |last2=Michaeli |first2=Yarden |last3=Scharf |first3=Avi |date=12 June 2025 |title=Rafah Is Gone. Razed to the Ground. And It's Not the Only City Wiped Out by the Israeli Army |url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2025-06-12/ty-article-magazine/.premium/rafah-is-gone-razed-to-the-ground-its-not-the-only-city-decimated-by-the-israeli-army/00000197-6506-db73-aff7-7d4ee6bb0000 |work=[[Haaretz]] |access-date=13 September 2025 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20250612195429/https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2025-06-12/ty-article-magazine/.premium/rafah-is-gone-razed-to-the-ground-its-not-the-only-city-decimated-by-the-israeli-army/00000197-6506-db73-aff7-7d4ee6bb0000 |archive-date=12 June 2025}}</ref> this has been mostly carried out by bulldozing and controlled demolitions of buildings, rather than by aerial bombardment.<ref name="nytrafah">{{cite news |last1=Granados |first1=Samuel |last2=Toler |first2=Aric |last3=Boxerman |first3=Aaron |title=Gazans Once Escaped to Rafah. Now Israel is Razing It |work=[[The New York Times]] |date=15 May 2025 |url=https://www.nytimes.com/interactive/2025/05/15/world/middleeast/rafah-gaza-israel-damage.html |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250516081153/https://www.nytimes.com/interactive/2025/05/15/world/middleeast/rafah-gaza-israel-damage.html |archive-date=16 May 2025}}</ref> In July 2025, the BBC reported that Israel had engaged in controlled demolitions of civilian infrastructure, potentially in violation of the Geneva Convention.<ref name="BBCVerifyDemolitions">{{cite news |last1=Garman |first1=Benedict |last2=Murphy |first2=Matt |date=18 July 2025 |title=Israel levelling thousands of Gaza civilian buildings in controlled demolitions |url=https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/resources/idt-33fccfbe-abcc-4af1-bdd2-632b2787cf59 |work=[[BBC News]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250724002043/https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/resources/idt-33fccfbe-abcc-4af1-bdd2-632b2787cf59 |archive-date=24 July 2025}}</ref> The BBC reported an IDF spokesperson saying, "Hamas and other terrorist organizations conceal military assets in densely populated civilian areas. The IDF identifies and destroys terrorist infrastructure located, among other places, within buildings in these areas."<ref name="BBCVerifyDemolitions" /> In November 2025, the BBC reported that Israel had demolished over 1,500 more buildings in Gaza since the ceasefire with Hamas.<ref name="BBCCeasfireDemolitions">{{cite news |last1=Garman |first1=Benedict |last2=Metzler |first2=Barbara |date=12 November 2025 |title=Israel has destroyed more than 1,500 more buildings in Gaza since ceasefire |url=https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/c0mxylxw48yo |work=[[BBC News]] |archive-url=https://archive.today/20251112014950/https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/c0mxylxw48yo |archive-date=12 November 2025}}</ref> A spokesperson for the IDF said it was acting "in accordance with the ceasefire framework" as the demolitions occurred behind the [[Yellow Line (Gaza)|Yellow Line]], in the portion of Gaza under Israeli military control, which comprises 53% of Gaza.<ref name="BBCCeasfireDemolitions"/>

=== Forced displacement ===
{{See also|Gaza Strip evacuations}}{{#invoke:Multiple image|
| perrow            = 1/2/2
| total_width       = 300
| image1            = Return of displaced people via Al-Rasheed Street after ceasefire, January 2025, Gaza Strip.jpg
| image2            = An aerial view of Al-Mawasi area where displaced Palestinians live in tents, Gaza Strip.jpg
| image3            = An aerial photo of displaced Palestinians waiting in northern Nuseirat to return to their homes in Gaza.jpg
| footer_align      = center
| footer            = '''Clockwise from top''': {{startflatlist}}
* Return of displaced people via Al-Rasheed Street after ceasefire, January 2025, Gaza Strip
* An aerial photo of displaced Palestinians waiting in northern Nuseirat to return to their homes in Gaza
* An aerial view of Al-Mawasi area where displaced Palestinians live in tents, Gaza Strip
{{endflatlist}}
}}

Since October 2023, Israel's evacuation orders have displaced 1.9 million people—nearly Gaza's entire population—through unclear, inconsistent directives, often issued amid bombings, leaving civilians with no safe routes or destinations. Humanitarian zones were repeatedly attacked, while Israel blocked aid, leading to starvation, destroyed infrastructure, and uninhabitable conditions. Senior Israeli officials openly declared intentions to reduce Gaza's territory and push Palestinians out, reinforcing policies of [[ethnic cleansing]] and permanent displacement. Human Rights Watch reported that Israel's systematic forced displacement of Palestinians in Gaza amounts to [[war crime]]s and [[crimes against humanity]].<ref>{{cite web |last=Hardman |first=Nadia |date=14 November 2024 |title="Hopeless, Starving, and Besieged" |url=https://www.hrw.org/report/2024/11/14/hopeless-starving-and-besieged/israels-forced-displacement-palestinians-gaza |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250328094008/https://www.hrw.org/report/2024/11/14/hopeless-starving-and-besieged/israels-forced-displacement-palestinians-gaza |archive-date=28 March 2025 |website=[[Human Rights Watch]] |language=en}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last=Gritten |first=David |date=15 November 2024 |title=Gaza: HRW accuses Israel of war crime with displacements |url=https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/ce8ygyem84jo |url-status=live |access-date=25 March 2025 |work=[[BBC News]] |language=en-GB |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250323051248/https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/ce8ygyem84jo |archive-date=23 March 2025}}</ref>{{sfn|Gómez-Ugarte|Chen|Acosta|Basellini|2025|p=13}} South Africa and others criticised the [[Gaza Strip evacuations]] as a key component of the genocide.{{sfn|Jamshidi|2024a|pp=14–16}} B'Tselem mentions statements by Israeli high-ranking officials that a "central objective of the war" was ethnic cleansing.{{sfn|B'Tselem|2025|p=47}}

On 6 October 2024, Israel designated northern Gaza as a combat zone and ordered the civilian population to evacuate.<ref>{{cite news |last=Rasgon |first=Adam |date=6 October 2024 |url=https://www.nytimes.com/live/2024/10/06/world/israel-iran-hezbollah-lebanon |url-status=live |url-access=subscription |title=A new Israeli map labels nearly all of northern Gaza 'new evacuation zones |newspaper=[[The New York Times]]|archive-url=https://archive.today/20241006192404/https://www.nytimes.com/live/2024/10/06/world/israel-iran-hezbollah-lebanon |archive-date=6 October 2024}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last=Keller-Lynn |first=Carrie |date=6 October 2024 |url=https://www.wsj.com/world/middle-east/israel-launches-new-offensive-in-northern-gaza-orders-mass-evacuation-786f2fff |title=Israel Launches New Offensive in Northern Gaza, Orders Mass Evacuation |newspaper=[[The Wall Street Journal]] |archive-url=https://archive.today/20241006181906/https://www.wsj.com/world/middle-east/israel-launches-new-offensive-in-northern-gaza-orders-mass-evacuation-786f2fff |archive-date=6 October 2024 |url-status=live |url-access=subscription}}</ref> Both Israeli military analysts and the [[Al Mezan Center for Human Rights]] alleged that this was the first stage of the "[[Israeli generals' plan|Generals' Plan]]", a policy proposed by the former Israeli general [[Giora Eiland]] to force Palestinians out of Gaza.<ref>{{cite news |last=Monks |first=Kieron |date=6 October 2024 |url=https://inews.co.uk/news/world/evacuate-die-israel-generals-plan-north-gaza-3310922 |url-status=live |title='Evacuate or die': Israel moves towards 'general's plan' for north Gaza |newspaper=[[The i Paper|iNews]] |archive-url=https://archive.today/20241006134926/https://inews.co.uk/news/world/evacuate-die-israel-generals-plan-north-gaza-3310922 |archive-date=6 October 2024}}</ref> The [[UN Human Rights Office]] said that Israel may have caused the "destruction of the Palestinian population in Gaza's northernmost governorate through death and displacement."<ref>{{cite web |date=20 October 2024 |title=UN Human Rights Office is concerned over the potential destruction of the Palestinian population in north Gaza |url=https://reliefweb.int/report/occupied-palestinian-territory/un-human-rights-office-concerned-over-potential-destruction-palestinian-population-north-gaza |url-status=live |archive-url=https://archive.today/20241021081250/https://reliefweb.int/report/occupied-palestinian-territory/un-human-rights-office-concerned-over-potential-destruction-palestinian-population-north-gaza |archive-date=21 October 2024 |access-date=23 October 2024 |website=[[ReliefWeb]] |publisher=[[United Nations Human Rights Council]]}}</ref>

During the [[January 2025 Gaza war ceasefire|January 2025 ceasefire]], displaced persons were able to return to their homes in northern Gaza. After Israel [[March 2025 Israeli attacks on the Gaza Strip|broke the ceasefire]] in March 2025, displacement orders resumed. The [[2025 Gaza City offensive]] led to further evacuation orders for 1.2 million people.<ref>{{cite web |title='No Place Under Heaven': Forced displacement in the Gaza Strip, 2023-2025 |url=https://www.btselem.org/gaza_strip/202512_no_place_under_heaven_forced_displacement_in_the_gaza_strip_2023_2025 |publisher=[[B'Tselem]] |access-date=4 January 2026 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251220061844/https://www.btselem.org/gaza_strip/202512_no_place_under_heaven_forced_displacement_in_the_gaza_strip_2023_2025 |archive-date=20 December 2025 |date=19 December 2025 |url-status=live}}</ref>

=== Attacks on healthcare ===
{{main|Attacks on health facilities during the Gaza war}}

{{#invoke:Multiple image|
| perrow            = 1/1

}}

In November 2023 in ''[[The Lancet]]'' and in February 2024 in ''[[BMJ Global Health]]'', multiple doctors detailed how the targeting of Gazan health infrastructure and medical personnel, coupled with rhetoric used by Israeli politicians, amounts to genocide.<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted|

| {{harvnb|Hanbali|Kwong|Neilson|Smith|2024|p=e014942}}
| {{harvnb|Sathar|2023|pp=82–83}}
| {{harvnb|Sankar|2024}}
}}</ref> Legal scholars have supported this assessment.{{sfn|Mahomed|2023|pp=77–79}}{{sfn|Sultany|2024|p=11}} [[Healthcare in the State of Palestine|Gaza's healthcare system]] faced humanitarian crises as a result of Israel's assault: hospitals began shutting down by 23 October as they ran out of fuel.<ref>{{cite news |date=24 October 2023 |title=Gaza hospital generators to run out of fuel in 48 hours: Health Ministry |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/10/24/gaza-hospital-generators-to-run-out-of-fuel-in-48-hours-health-ministry |url-status=live unit|NICUs]] died.<ref>{{cite news |date=13 November 2023 |title=3 premature babies die at Al-Shifa Hospital: Doctor staffers, and ambulances and health institutions have been destroyed.<ref name="Healthcare destroyed">{{#invoke:list|bulleted|

}}</ref> {{lang|fr|[[Médecins Sans Frontières]]}} reported that scores of ambulances and medical facilities were damaged or destroyed,<ref>{{cite news |title=Gaza war inflicts catastrophic damage on infrastructure and economy |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/gaza-war-inflicts-catastrophic-damage-infrastructure-economy-2023-11-17/#:~:text=HOSPITALS%20AND%20SCHOOLS&text=OCHA%20said%2055%20ambulances%20in,of%20drugs%20and%20blood%20products. |url-status=live |archive-url=https://ghostarchive.org/archive/20240303120357/https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/gaza-war-inflicts-catastrophic-damage-infrastructure-economy-2023-11-17/#:~:text=HOSPITALS%20AND%20SCHOOLS&text=OCHA%20said%2055%20ambulances%20in,of%20drugs%20and%20blood%20products. |archive-date=3 March 2024 |access-date=18 November 2023 |work=[[Reuters]] |date=17 November 2023}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Riash |first1=Abed Abu |last2=Marsi |first2=Federica |date=12 October 2023 |title=Gaza medics say Israel targeting ambulances, health facilities |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/10/12/war-crime-gaza-medics-say-israel-targeting-ambulances-health-facilities |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231022010523/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/10/12/war-crime-gaza-medics-say-israel-targeting-ambulances-health-facilities |archive-date=22 October 2023 |access-date=12 October 2023 |publisher=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]]}}</ref> and that its own staff were killed.<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
