As of February 2025, at least 160 healthcare workers from Gaza are believed to be detained by Israel, with another 24 missing after being taken from Gaza hospitals. Al-Shifa hospital director [[Mohammed Abu Salmiya]], detained for seven months and released without charges, detailed the abuses he faced and said that in Israeli prisons "no day passes without torture".<ref>{{cite news |last1=Kelly |first1=Annie |last2=Osman |first2=Hoda |last3=Jallad |first3=Farah |date=25 February 2025 |title=More than 160 Gazan medics held in Israeli prisons amid reports of torture |url=https://www.theguardian.com/global-development/2025/feb/25/more-than-160-gazan-medics-held-in-israeli-prisons-amid-reports-of-torture |access-date=28 February 2025 |work=[[The Guardian]] |language=en-GB |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250225182144/https://www.theguardian.com/global-development/2025/feb/25/more-than-160-gazan-medics-held-in-israeli-prisons-amid-reports-of-torture |archive-date=25 February 2025}}</ref>

=== Preventing births ===
In March 2025, a UN investigation concluded that Israel had committed genocidal acts in Gaza by systematically destroying its reproductive healthcare facilities while imposing a siege preventing necessary medications for deliveries, pregnancies, and [[Neonatal nursing|neonatal care]], causing "irreversible" harm to Palestinians' reproductive prospects in Gaza. The commission also found that Israeli forces intentionally destroyed Gaza's main [[IVF|in-vitro]] [[fertility clinic]], Al-Basma IVF Centre, which served 2,000 to 3,000 patients a month. Israel destroyed about 4,000 [[embryo]]s and 1,000 specimens of [[sperm]] and unfertilised [[Egg cell|eggs]] in the attack.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Shubailat |first1=Nadine |last2=Alcini |first2=Camilla |date=24 April 2024 |title=Over 4,000 IVF embryos destroyed in 1 shelling at Gaza's largest fertility center, director says |url=https://abcnews.go.com/International/4000-ivf-embryos-destroyed-1-shelling-gazas-largest/story?id=109350404 |work=[[ABC News (United States)|ABC News]] |access-date=11 May 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240506030400/https://abcnews.go.com/International/4000-ivf-embryos-destroyed-1-shelling-gazas-largest/story%3Fid%3D109350404 |archive-date=6 May 2024}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Salem |first1=Saleh |last2=Creidi |first2=Imad |last3=Mills |first3=Andrew |date=17 April 2024 |title=Gaza's IVF embryos destroyed by Israeli strike |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/5000-lives-one-shell-gazas-ivf-embryos-destroyed-by-israeli-strike-2024-04-17/ |work=[[Reuters]] |access-date=11 May 2025 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20240417122745/https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/5000-lives-one-shell-gazas-ivf-embryos-destroyed-by-israeli-strike-2024-04-17/ |archive-date=17 April 2024}}</ref> No evidence that the building was used for military purposes was found. The commission concluded that the destruction of the clinic "was a measure intended to prevent births among Palestinians in Gaza, which is a genocidal act".<ref name=Independent_International_Commission_Inquiry_2025_births>{{harvnb|Independent International Commission of Inquiry|2025|p=39}}: "175. The Commission finds that the ISF intentionally attacked and destroyed the Basma IVF clinic which was the main fertility centre in Gaza. The ISF destroyed all of the reproductive material that was stored for the future conception of Palestinians. The Commission did not find any evidence that this IVF clinic was a legitimate military target at the time that it was attacked by the ISF. The Commission concludes that the destruction of the Basma IVF clinic was a measure intended to prevent births among Palestinians in Gaza, which is a genocidal act under the Rome Statute and Genocide Convention. The Commission also concludes that this was done with the intent to destroy the Palestinians in Gaza as a group, in whole or in part, and that this is the only inference that could reasonably be drawn from the acts in question"</ref><ref name="NDTV-March 13">{{cite news |date=13 March 2025 |title="Genocidal Acts": UN Slams Israel's Attacks On Gaza Reproductive Centres |url=https://www.ndtv.com/world-news/genocidal-acts-un-slams-israels-attacks-on-gaza-reproductive-centres-7915048 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250314093302/https://www.ndtv.com/world-news/genocidal-acts-un-slams-israels-attacks-on-gaza-reproductive-centres-7915048 |archive-date=14 March 2025 |access-date=13 March 2025 |work=[[NDTV]] |language=en |agency=[[Agence France-Presse]]}}</ref><ref name="Le Poidevin 2025a">{{cite news |last=Le Poidevin |first=Olivia |date=13 March 2025 |title=UN experts accuse Israel of genocidal acts and sexual violence in Gaza |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/un-experts-accuse-israel-genocidal-acts-sexual-violence-gaza-2025-03-13/ |access-date=13 March 2025 |work=[[Reuters]] |archive-url=https://archive.today/20250313082455/https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/un-experts-accuse-israel-genocidal-acts-sexual-violence-gaza-2025-03-13/ |archive-date=13 March 2025}}</ref> UN experts reported that they had found that Israel had systematically destroyed women's health care facilities and used sexual violence as a war strategy, thereby carrying out genocidal acts against Palestinians.<ref name="NDTV-March 13"/><ref name="Le Poidevin 2025a"/>

According to statistics from the [[Gaza Ministry of Health]] reported by [[Physicians for Human Rights]], the birth rate in Gaza in May and June 2025 had fallen 41% from the same months in 2022. The ministry also reported an increase in infant mortality, miscarriages, and premature births in Gaza during this time.<ref>{{cite web |date=14 January 2026 |url=https://phr.org/our-work/resources/destroying-hope-for-the-future-reproductive-violence-in-gaza/ |title=Destroying Hope for the Future: Reproductive Violence in Gaza |access-date=14 January 2026 |website=[[Physicians for Human Rights]]}}</ref>

=== Destruction of cultural, religious and educational sites ===
{{main|Destruction of cultural heritage during the Israeli invasion of the Gaza Strip}}

{{see also|Attacks on schools during the Gaza war|Israeli razing of cemeteries and necroviolence against Palestinians|Attacks on religious sites during the Israeli invasion of Gaza}}{{#invoke:Multiple image|
| perrow            = 1/2/2
| total_width       = 300
| image1            = A mosque destroyed in the Jabalia area of the Gaza Strip.jpg
| image2            = Damage in Gaza Strip during the October 2023 - 16.jpg
| image3            = غزة، مركز رشاد الشوا (1) غزة بعد الحرب 23-25.jpg
| footer_align      = center
| footer            = '''Clockwise from top''': {{startflatlist}}
* A mosque in Gaza destroyed in an Israeli airstrike, 20 February 2025.
* The wreckage of the [[Rashad Shawa Cultural Center]]
* A mosque in Khan Younis, 8 October 2023
{{endflatlist}}
}}
[[Amnesty International]] notes that "while the destruction of historical, cultural and religious property or heritage is not considered a prohibited act under the Genocide Convention, the ICJ has established that such destruction can provide evidence of intent to physically destroy the group when carried out deliberately."{{sfn|Amnesty International report|2024|p=32}} The [[Lemkin Institute for Genocide Prevention]] has said that Israel's deliberate destruction of cemeteries in Gaza indicates genocidal intent because it enacts the "[[Historical negationism|erasure of a people's...historical presence]]".<ref name="whywecall">{{cite web |date=29 December 2023 |title=Statement on Why We Call the Israeli Attack on Gaza Genocide |url=https://www.lemkininstitute.com/statements-new-page/statement-on-why-we-call-the-israeli-attack-on-gaza-genocide |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231230154434/https://www.lemkininstitute.com/statements-new-page/statement-on-why-we-call-the-israeli-attack-on-gaza-genocide |archive-date=30 December 2023 |access-date=23 September 2025 |website=[[Lemkin Institute for Genocide Prevention]] |language=en}}</ref>

Since 7 October 2023, the IDF has been accused of using excessive force against dozens of schools;<ref>{{cite news |date=24 January 2024 |title=How Israel has destroyed Gaza's schools and universities |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2024/1/24/how-israel-has-destroyed-gazas-schools-and-universities |access-date=2 February 2024 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240206045355/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2024/1/24/how-israel-has-destroyed-gazas-schools-and-universities |archive-date=6 February 2024}}</ref><ref>{{cite web |date=19 October 2023 |title=Gaza: UN experts decry bombing of hospitals and schools as crimes against humanity, call for prevention of genocide |url=https://www.ohchr.org/en/press-releases/2023/10/gaza-un-experts-decry-bombing-hospitals-and-schools-crimes-against-humanity |website=[[Office of the United Nations High Commissioner for Human Rights]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240131100935/https://www.ohchr.org/en/press-releases/2023/10/gaza-un-experts-decry-bombing-hospitals-and-schools-crimes-against-humanity |archive-date=31 January 2024}}</ref> theft;{{sfn|Kottasová|Salman|Alkhaldi|Bashir|2023}} desecration and mutilation of deceased Palestinians;<ref name="Salman & Khadder 2023"/> and making no, or an inadequate, distinction between Hamas forces and civilians.<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
| {{cite web |date=20 October 2023 |title=Damning evidence of war crimes as Israeli attacks wipe out entire families in Gaza |url=https://www.amnesty.org/en/latest/news/2023/10/damning-evidence-of-war-crimes-as-israeli-attacks-wipe-out-entire-families-in-gaza/ |publisher=[[Amnesty International]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231105011959/https://www.amnesty.org/en/latest/news/2023/10/damning-evidence-of-war-crimes-as-israeli-attacks-wipe-out-entire-families-in-gaza/ |archive-date=5 November 2023}}
| {{harvnb|B'Tselem|2023}}
| {{harvnb|Gvaryahu|2024}}
| {{harvnb|Marsi|Mohamed|2024b}}
| {{harvnb|Bateman|2024}}
| {{harvnb|Sultany|2024|pp=11–12}}
| {{Cite news|date=19 June 2024 |title=Laws of war likely 'consistently violated' in Israeli strikes on Gaza: UN rights office |url=https://news.un.org/en/story/2024/06/1151196 |work=UN News |publisher=[[United Nations]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240703075536/https://news.un.org/en/story/2024/06/1151196 |archive-date=3 July 2024}}
}}</ref> The targeting of cultural and educational sites have also been cited as genocidal acts, as has the use of [[white phosphorus]].{{#tag:ref|The use of white phosphorus against military targets located among civilians is contrary to [[Protocol on Incendiary Weapons|Protocol III]] of the [[Convention on Certain Conventional Weapons]], of which Israel is not a signatory.<ref>{{cite news |date=13 October 2023 |title=Human Rights Watch says Israel used white phosphorus in Gaza, Lebanon |language=en |work=[[Reuters]] |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/human-rights-watch-says-israel-used-white-phosphorous-gaza-lebanon-2023-10-12/ |access-date=17 October 2023 |archive-date=13 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231013003409/https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/human-rights-watch-says-israel-used-white-phosphorous-gaza-lebanon-2023-10-12/ |url-status=live}}</ref>|group=lower-alpha}}{{sfn|Üngör|2024|p=8}}

On 18 April 2024, UN experts in [[Geneva]] condemned Israel for its "[[scholasticide]]" in Gaza, finding that it had destroyed more than 80% of schools and killed 5,000 students, 261 teachers, and dozens of professors.<ref name="scholasticide" />

Amnesty International identified at least four instances in which there was "no imperative military necessity" for the deliberate destruction of Gazan cultural and religious sites:{{sfn|Amnesty International report|2024|p=216}} the destruction of the Al-Mughraqa campus of [[Al-Azhar University – Gaza|Al-Azhar University]], the Al-Zahra campus of [[Israa University (Palestine)|Israa University]], the Al-Dhilal mosque and Bani Suheila cemetery in Khan Younis, and the Al-Istiqlal mosque in Khan Younis.{{sfn|Amnesty International report|2024|pp=222–233}} Amnesty International pointed to the attitudes and behaviour of Israeli soldiers involved in the demolitions of these sites in videos posted on social media as evidence that these actions demonstrated genocidal intent. Amnesty International also noted the overall volume of destruction of Gazan cultural, historical and religious sites, including Gaza's central archives.{{sfn|Amnesty International report|2024|pp=216–219}}

As of January 2025, Israel had destroyed 815 mosques and 19 cemeteries during the Gaza war.<ref>{{cite news |date=5 January 2025 |author=The New Arab Staff |title=Nearly 1,000 mosques in Gaza damaged, destroyed by Israel |url=https://www.newarab.com/news/nearly-1000-mosques-gaza-damaged-destroyed-israel |work=[[The New Arab]] |access-date=27 February 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250109003458/https://www.newarab.com/news/nearly-1000-mosques-gaza-damaged-destroyed-israel |archive-date=9 January 2025 |url-status=live |language=en-EN}}</ref>

In June 2025, UN experts published a report saying Israel had committed the crime against humanity of [[Extermination (crime)|extermination]] for "killing civilians sheltering in schools and religious sites". According to the report, Israel has destroyed over 90% of educational buildings in Gaza.{{sfn|Murphy|2025}}

=== Serious bodily and mental harm, and sexual violence ===
{{main|Sexual and gender-based violence against Palestinians during the Gaza war|Torture during the Gaza war|Effect of the Gaza war on children in the Gaza Strip|Women in the Gaza war}}

The number of injured since 7 October 2023 due to Israeli military actions is greater than 170,000,<ref name="snapshot"/><ref name="Burke 2025"/> and Gaza has the most child amputees per capita worldwide.<ref name="Amputee stats">{{#invoke:list|bulleted|

|newspaper=[[The Washington Post]] |language=en-US |url-access=subscription |url-status=live}}</ref> death, arson, and rape,<ref>{{cite news |last=Shawer |first=Mosab |date=10 January 2024 In August 2024, the UN OHCHR reported receiving testimony from Palestinians imprisoned at [[Sde Teiman detention camp]] about rape and sexual assault perpetrated on detainees.<ref name="ohchr-2024-08" /> The Lemkin Institute considers this and similar reports to be indicative of "Sexualized Violence During Genocide", or sexual violence being used to destroy a group.<ref name="lemkin">{{cite web |date=11 September 2024 |title=The Genocidal Dimensions of Israel's Use of Sexual and Gender-Based Violence (SGBV) against Palestinians |url=https://www.lemkininstitute.com/statements-new-page/the-genocidal-dimensions-of-israel%E2%80%99s-use-of-sexual-and-gender-based-violence-(sgbv)-against-palestinians |access-date=17 December 2024 |website=[[Lemkin Institute for Genocide Prevention]] |language=en |archive-date=30 September 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240930203114/https://www.lemkininstitute.com/statements-new-page/the-genocidal-dimensions-of-israel%E2%80%99s-use-of-sexual-and-gender-based-violence-(sgbv)-against-palestinians |url-status=live}}</ref>

As of 25 August 2024, the UN estimates that most of Gaza's 2.2&nbsp;million people are confined to roughly {{convert|15|sqmi}}, causing a critical lack of basic services, like clean water, and diseases spreading widely, such as [[Hepatitis C]].<ref>{{cite news |last=Clayton |first=Freddie |date=25 August 2024 |title=Gaza's 2.2 million people are confined to a humanitarian area smaller than Manhattan |url=https://www.nbcnews.com/news/world/gaza-humanitarian-zones-smaller-than-manhattan-rcna167056 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240911101752/https://www.nbcnews.com/news/world/gaza-humanitarian-zones-smaller-than-manhattan-rcna167056 |archive-date=11 September 2024 |access-date=30 August 2024 |work=[[NBC News]]}}</ref>

Amnesty International reported that the pattern of abuses inside Israeli prisons "underscores the systematic dehumanization and mental and physical abuse of Palestinians in Gaza and may also be taken into account with a view to inferring genocidal intent from pattern of conduct."{{sfn|Amnesty International report|2024|p=296}} According to the [[Independent International Commission of Inquiry on the Occupied Palestinian Territory|Independent International Commission of Inquiry]], gender-based and sexual violence were committed "to dominate, oppress and destroy the Palestinian people in whole or in part."<ref name=Independent_International_Commission_Inquiry_2025_sex_vio>{{harvnb|Independent International Commission of Inquiry|2025|p=1}}: "The Commission also examines the sharp increase in sexual and gender-based violence perpetrated by members of the Israeli Security Forces and settlers online and in person across the Occupied Palestinian Territory, including rape and other forms of sexual violence. It also examines how sexual and gender-based violence has taken different forms when committed against male and female members of the Palestinian community in order to dominate, oppress and destroy the Palestinian people in whole or in part."</ref> According to a UN committee, the Gaza war has resulted in disabilities for more than 21,000 children as of September 2025.<ref name="Guardian_3_September_2025"/>

=== Ecocide ===
{{main|Environmental impact of the Gaza war}}

[[File:Tones of waste have accumulated near populated areas across Gaza posing catastrophic environmental and health risks. Children rummage through trash daily 7.jpg|thumb|Waste has accumulated near populated areas across Gaza, posing environmental and health risks.]]
Israel's bombing in Gaza caused [[Environmental impact of the Gaza war|severe environmental devastation]], destroying vegetation, water, sanitation, and waste infrastructure and contaminating air, soil, and water. The UN and environmental groups report damage consistent with "[[ecocide]]", citing massive debris, untreated sewage, and toxic pollution. These conditions have triggered disease outbreaks, respiratory illnesses, and long-term health risks.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Joseph |first=Lesley |date=27 February 2025 |title=Israel's bombing of Gaza caused untold environmental damage − recovery will take effort and time |url=http://theconversation.com/israels-bombing-of-gaza-caused-untold-environmental-damage-recovery-will-take-effort-and-time-245311 |access-date=11 October 2025 |website=[[The Conversation (website)|The Conversation]] |language=en-US |archive-date=14 November 2025}}</ref><ref name="Ahmed et al.">{{Cite news |last1=Ahmed |first1=Kaamil |last2=Gayle |first2=Damien |last3=Mousa |first3=Aseel |date=29 March 2024 |title='Ecocide in Gaza': does scale of environmental destruction amount to a war crime? |url=https://www.theguardian.com/environment/2024/mar/29/gaza-israel-palestinian-war-ecocide-environmental-destruction-pollution-rome-statute-war-crimes-aoe |access-date=11 October 2025 |work=[[The Guardian]] |language=en-GB |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20260101104242/https://www.theguardian.com/environment/2024/mar/29/gaza-israel-palestinian-war-ecocide-environmental-destruction-pollution-rome-statute-war-crimes-aoe |first5=Mohammed |last6=Al-Najar |first6=Husam |last7=Butmeh |first7=Abeer |last8=Abu Dayyeh |first8=Rasha |last9=Al-Shewy |first9=Mohamed |last10=Aker |first10=Amira |date=4 November 2024 |title=From Ecocide to Genocide: A Call to Action for Scientists Globally to Address the Destruction in Gaza |ssrn=5021472}}</ref> Multiple commentators have argued that deliberate ecocide is a central component of Israel's genocide in Gaza.<ref>{{Cite news |last=Monbiot |first=George |author-link=George Monbiot |date=27 September 2025 |title=Israel's gecocide in Gaza sends this message: even if we stopped October 2024 |title=Ecocide: Israel's Deliberate and Systematic Environmental Destruction in Gaza – occupied Palestinian territory water, land, and food systems constitutes a genocidal act, as it inflicts conditions of life calculated to destroy the group, in whole or in part.{{Genocide Convention Article 2}}<ref>{{cite journal === Targeting of specific professions ===

==== Educationalists ====
The killing of educationalists, and destruction of educational infrastructure such as schools and  universities, has been recognised by scholars as a component part of the Gaza Genocide. <ref>{{Cite journal |last=Alarabeed |first=Wadee |date=2025-11-11 |title=The banality of scholasticide: the role of universities and academia in an age of genocide |url=https://www.tandfonline.com/doi/full/10.1080/14767724.2025.2577694 |journal=Globalisation, Societies and Education |language=en |pages=1–16 |doi=10.1080/14767724.2025.2577694 |issn=1476-7724}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |last=Pratt |first=Nicola |date=2025-11-25 |title=Scholasticide in Gaza: Settler Colonial Elimination, Genocide, and the Crisis of Academic Responsibility |url=https://www.e-ir.info/2025/11/25/scholasticide-in-gaza-settler-colonial-elimination-genocide-and-the-crisis-of-academic-responsibility/ |access-date=2026-01-23 |website=E-International Relations |language=en-US}}</ref> The IAGS in its 2025 resolution declaring  that Israel’s policies and actions in Gaza had met the legal definition of genocide, used the fact that  "Israel has destroyed schools, universities, libraries, museums, and archives, all of them essential to the continued existence of Palestinian collective well-being and identity;" in support of its resolution.<ref name="IAGSResolution" />

United Nations  [[United Nations special rapporteur|Special Rapporteurs]] and experts suggested that there was "an intentional effort to comprehensively destroy the Palestinian education system, an action known as ‘[[scholasticide]]” , The experts said that 'The attacks "present a systematic pattern of violence aimed at dismantling the very foundation of Palestinian society”.<ref name="scholasticide" />

South Africa, in its filing with the ICJ charging Israel with the crime of genocide, cited the destruction of 4 universities and the killing of leading Palestinian academics Professor [[Sufian Tayeh]], the President of the Islamic University; Dr [[Ahmed Hamdi Abo Absa]], Dean of the Software Engineering Department at the University of Palestine;  Professor [[Muhammad Eid Shabir]], Professor of Immunology and Virology, and former President of the Islamic University of Gaza, and Professor [[Refaat Alareer]], poet and Professor of Comparative Literature and Creative Writing at the Islamic University of Gaza.<ref name="ICJ-2023-12-29" />

Researchers at Birzeit university called the killing of educationalists to be  "deliberate and systematic". They stated that "94 professors were targeted and killed by Israeli occupation".<ref>{{Cite web |last=Rabaia |first=Ibrahim S.I |last2=Habash |first2=Lourdes |date=2024-04-18 |title=The Hidden War on Higher Education: Unmasking the 'Educide' in Gaza |url=https://pomeps.org/the-hidden-war-on-higher-education-unmasking-the-educide-in-gaza |access-date=2026-01-23 |website=Project on Middle East Political Science |pages=8-13 |language=en-US}}</ref>

==== Journalists ====
Press freedom organisations and human rights groups have characterised the systematic killing of Palestinian journalists as a component of the genocide in Gaza.<ref>{{Cite web |date=2025-09-08 |title=PCHR Launches Report on "Assassination of Truth: Killing of Journalists amid Genocide in Gaza" |url=https://pchrgaza.org/pchr-launches-report-on-assassination-of-truth-killing-of-journalists-amid-genocide-in-gaza/ |access-date=2026-01-23 |website=Palestinian Centre for Human Rights |language=en}}</ref> [[International Federation of Journalists|The International Federation of Journalists]] reported that 56 media professionals were killed in 2025 alone as part of the "genocidal war on Gaza".<ref>{{Cite web |date=2025-10-07 |title=Israel: Two years of killing journalists and controlling the narrative in Gaza |url=https://www.ifj.org/media-centre/news/detail/category/press-releases/article/israel-two-years-of-killing-journalists-and-controlling-the-narrative-in-gaza |access-date=2026-01-23 |website=IFJ |language=en}}</ref>

South Africa  cited the Palestinian journalists  being "killed at a rate significantly higher than has occurred in any conflict in the past 100 years" as part of its [[South Africa's genocide case against Israel|application accusing Israel]] of genocide.<ref name="ICJ-2023-12-29" />

The IDF has been accused of directly targeting journalists and media organisations despite clear marking and  protective measures. Al Jazeera reported that 278 journalists and 706 family members of Palestinian journalists have been killed during the "genocidal war" since October 2023. <ref>{{Cite web |last=Gjevori |first=Elis |date=2025-12-28 |title=Israel kills over 700 relatives of Palestinian journalists in Gaza: Report |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/12/28/israel-kills-over-700-relatives-of-palestinian-journalists-in-gaza-report |access-date=2026-01-20 |website=Al Jazeera |language=en}}</ref><ref name="Akila">{{Cite book |last=Akila |first=Hiba |title=Eliminating Witnessess on Genocide and Eithnic Cleansing Crimes in the Gaza Strip |publisher=Palestinian Center for Human Rights}}</ref> 

A [[Brown University|Brown university]] study found that Israel had killed more journalists in Gaza since October 2023 than "the U.S. Civil War, World Wars I and II, the Korean War, Vietnam War, the wars in Yugoslavia in the 1990s and 2000s, and the post-9/11 war in Afghanistan, combined". <ref>{{Cite book |last=Turse |first=Nick |url=https://costsofwar.watson.brown.edu/sites/default/files/papers/Turse_Costs-of-War_The-Reporting-Graveyard-4-2-25.pdf |title=News graveyards: How dangers to war reporters endanger the world. |publisher=Watson School for International and Public Affairs, Brown University |year=2025 |archive-url=https://archive.ph/feyZb |archive-date=20 Jan 2026}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |last=Batrawy |first=Aya |date=2025-09-01 |title=Media outlets demand Israel grant access to Gaza, halt attacks on journalists there |url=https://www.npr.org/2025/09/01/nx-s1-5521944/news-outlets-call-for-safety-of-journalists-covering-the-war-in-gaza |access-date=2026-01-20 |work=NPR |language=en}}</ref> 

The [[Committee to Protect Journalists|CPJ]] observed that "Israel is engaging in the deadliest and most deliberate effort to kill and silence journalists that CPJ has ever documented" and that there was a "pattern of journalists in Gaza reporting receiving threats, and subsequently, their family members being killed".<ref>{{Cite web |date=n.d. |title=Israel-Gaza War |url=https://cpj.org/issue/israel-gaza-war/ |access-date=2026-01-20 |website=Committee to Protect Journalists |language=en-US}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |last=McGreal |first=Chris |date=2023-12-21 |title=Israeli military accused of targeting journalists and their families in Gaza |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2023/dec/21/israel-idf-accused-targeting-journalists-gaza |access-date=2026-01-20 |work=The Guardian |language=en-GB |issn=0261-3077}}</ref>

The [[Reporters sans frontieres|RSF]] accused the IDF, in a case filed with the [[International Criminal Court|ICC]], of the targeted killing of 7 journalists in Gaza, in between the dates of 22 October to 15 December 2023. The 7 journalists were Asem Al-Barsh, Bilal Jadallah , Montaser Al-Sawaf,  Rushdi Al Siraj, Hassouna Salim,  Sari Mansour and Al Jazeera’s Abudaqa.  Targeting journalists is a war crime under Article 8 of the Rome Statute. <ref>{{Cite web |date=2023-12-22 |title=RSF files second war crimes complaint with ICC over Gaza journalists killed |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/12/22/rsf-files-second-war-crimes-complaint-with-icc-over-gaza-journalists-killed |access-date=2026-01-20 |website=Al Jazeera |language=en}}</ref>

The [[Palestinian Centre for Human Rights|PCHR]] alleges that this killing is to intimidate and deter journalists from coverage of current events.<ref name="Akila" />

==Academic and legal discourse==

There is a growing consensus among genocide and Holocaust scholars, international legal experts, human rights organisations, and governments that Israel's actions in Gaza constitute genocide. Israel and its supporters deny the accusation.<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
| {{harvnb|Mohyeldin|Hamdan|2024}}
| {{harvnb|Komnenic|2023}}
| {{harvnb|Sultany|2024|p=4}}
| {{harvnb|Swart|2025|p=689}}
}}</ref><ref name="Bouranova">{{harvnb|Bouranova|2024}}: "The opposition is political, as there is consensus amongst the international human rights legal community, many other legal and political experts, including many Holocaust scholars, that Israel is committing genocide in Gaza."</ref><ref name="MESB 2025"/>

=== Relationship to the Nakba, the broader Palestinian genocide accusation, and Israeli ideology ===
Some scholars say the Gaza genocide is merely the latest stage of a [[Palestinian genocide accusation|"slow-motion genocide" of Palestinians]] that began with the [[Nakba]] and the [[1948 Palestinian expulsion and flight|expulsion of hundreds of thousands of Palestinians]] upon Israel's founding in 1948.{{sfn|Shaw|2025b|p=2}}{{sfn|LeVine|2025|p=2}}<ref>{{Cite web |date=18 May 2025 |title=Four Facts about Israel's Genocide |url=https://www.lemkininstitute.com/statements-new-page/four-facts-about-israel%E2%80%99s-genocide |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250621102212/https://www.lemkininstitute.com/statements-new-page/four-facts-about-israel%E2%80%99s-genocide |archive-date=21 June 2025 |access-date=23 September 2025 |website=[[Lemkin Institute for Genocide Prevention]] |language=en |quote=Israel's genocide against Palestinians involves the planned and entirely intentional murder and forced displacement of all Palestinians from their ancestral homes across historical Palestine using all available means. It has been going on since Israel's founding, but sped up significantly first after Netanyahu assumed power in 2022 and again after October 7, 2023}}</ref>

According to [[B'Tselem]] and others, the Gaza genocide is occurring in the context of over 75 years of [[Zionism as settler colonialism|Zionist settler colonial]] violence and [[Jewish supremacy]] targeting Palestinians.{{sfn|B'Tselem|2025|p=5}}<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
| {{harvnb|O'Brien|2025}}
| {{harvnb|Nijim|2024|p=}}{{page needed|date=October 2025}}
| {{harvnb|Repo|2024|pp=}}{{page needed|date=October 2025}}
| {{harvnb|Sorek|2025|pp=}}{{page needed|date=October 2025}}
| {{harvnb|Lederman|2024|pp=1–2, 5}}
}}</ref> Multiple genocide scholars argue that [[settler colonialism]] is an important motive for Israel's actions.<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
| {{harvnb|Segal|2023}}
| {{harvnb|Lederman|2024|pp=1–2, 5}}
| {{harvnb|Abdo|2024|p=1}}
| {{harvnb|Shaw|2024|p=1}}
| {{harvnb|Üngör|2024|pp=3–4, 5–6}}
| {{harvnb|Albanese|2024a|p=2}}
}}</ref> [[Raz Segal]] and B'Tselem also highlight the increasing influence of Jewish supremacy in Israeli politics,{{sfn|Segal|2025|p=182}}{{sfn|B'Tselem|2025|p=5}} while reports by [[Francesca Albanese]] and [[Amos Goldberg]] highlight the project of [[Greater Israel]].{{sfn|Albanese|2024a|p=4}}{{sfn|Albanese|2024b|p=20–22}}{{sfn|Goldberg|2024|p=9}}

===Genocide and Holocaust studies===
In May 2025, ''[[NRC (newspaper)|NRC]]'' wrote that leading scholars in [[genocide studies]] are "surprisingly unanimous" that Israel is committing genocide.{{sfn|van Laarhoven|Peek|Walters|2025}} Some scholars of [[Holocaust studies]], such as [[Norman J. W. Goda]] and [[Jeffrey Herf]], have said that Israel is not committing genocide.<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
| {{harvnb|Goda|Herf|2025}}
| {{harvnb|Cohen|2024}}
| {{harvnb|Segal|2024|pp=62–66}}
| {{harvnb|Klein|2025|pp=1–7}}
}}</ref> Others, such as Israeli professors [[Raz Segal]] and {{ill|Shira Klein|he|שירה קליין}}, have argued that Israel's actions should be analysed as a case of genocide,{{sfn|van Laarhoven|Peek|Walters|2025}}{{sfn|Klein|2025|pp=1–7}}{{sfn|Segal|2024|pp=62–66}} citing, among other things, attacks on infrastructure, food, and water as genocidal.<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
| {{harvnb|Semerdjian|2024a|p=3}}
| {{harvnb|Samudzi|2024|pp=6–7}}
| {{harvnb|Stacey|2023}}
}}</ref> [[Omer Bartov]], professor of Holocaust and genocide studies at [[Brown University]] and an [[Israel Defense Forces]] veteran, has said: "intent has been publicly expressed by numerous officials and leaders. But intent can also be derived from a pattern of operations on the ground, and this pattern became clear by May 2024".<ref>{{Cite news |last=Bartov |first=Omer |author-link=Omer Bartov |date=15 July 2025 |title=Opinion {{!}} I'm a Genocide Scholar. I Know It When I See It. |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2025/07/15/opinion/israel-gaza-holocaust-genocide-palestinians.html |access-date=8 November 2025 |work=[[The New York Times]] |language=en-US |archive-url=https://archive.today/20250715050553/https://www.nytimes.com/2025/07/15/opinion/israel-gaza-holocaust-genocide-palestinians.html |archive-date=15 July 2025}}</ref> [[Amos Goldberg]] and [[Daniel Blatman]], historians of the Holocaust and genocide studies at the [[Hebrew University of Jerusalem]], noted that "most acts of genocide are perceived by their perpetrators as acts of self-defense against their victims" and the Gaza war "falls into this category."<ref>{{Cite news |date=30 January 2025 |title=There's no Auschwitz in Gaza. But it's still genocide |url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2025-01-30/ty-article-magazine/.highlight/theres-no-auschwitz-in-gaza-but-its-still-genocide/00000194-b8af-dee1-a5dc-fcff384b0000 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251001003740/https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2025-01-30/ty-article-magazine/.highlight/theres-no-auschwitz-in-gaza-but-its-still-genocide/00000194-b8af-dee1-a5dc-fcff384b0000 |archive-date=1 October 2025 |access-date=8 November 2025 |work=[[Haaretz]] |language=en}}</ref>

On 31 August 2025, the [[International Association of Genocide Scholars]] (IAGS), the world's biggest academic association of genocide scholars, passed a resolution saying that Israel has committed genocide in Gaza.<ref name="IAGSReuters" /><ref name="IAGSResolution" /><ref>{{Cite news |last=Tondo |first=Lorenzo |date=1 September 2025 |title=Israel committing genocide in Gaza, world's top scholars on the crime say |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2025/sep/01/israel-committing-genocide-in-gaza-worlds-top-scholars-on-the-say |access-date=1 September 2025 |work=[[The Guardian]] |language=en-GB |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250902000620/https://www.theguardian.com/world/2025/sep/01/israel-committing-genocide-in-gaza-worlds-top-scholars-on-the-say |archive-date=2 September 2025}}</ref>

===Legal and human rights experts===
{{Overly detailed|section|details=from the overview detailing grouped positions, the section has quadrupled in size, seeking to include quotes from every person who has commented|date=December 2025}}
In December 2023, former International Criminal Court chief prosecutor [[Luis Moreno Ocampo]] told ''[[Al Jazeera]]'' that the siege of Gaza was a form of genocide due to Israel's imposing conditions that would lead to the deaths of Palestinians.<ref>{{#invoke:Cite|news|url=https://www.aljazeera.com/program/upfront/2023/12/1/former-icc-chief-prosecutor-israels-siege-of-gaza-is-a-genocide |title=Former ICC chief prosecutor: Israel's siege of Gaza is a 'genocide' |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |date=1 December 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240710195403/https://www.aljazeera.com/program/upfront/2023/12/1/former-icc-chief-prosecutor-israels-siege-of-gaza-is-a-genocide |archive-date=10 July 2024}}</ref> In December, in correspondence published in ''The Lancet'', multiple specialists in international medicine and humanitarian aid reiterated warnings of the risk of genocide, while detailing how Israel's blocking of humanitarian support and aid were leading to unnecessary deaths, and how the death rate would continue to worsen. They called on signatories to the Genocide Convention to enforce a ceasefire on Israel.{{sfn|Faddoul|Shannon|Asghar|Boukari|2024|pp=25–26}} Nimer Sultany argues that, by mid-2024, a growing consensus among legal scholars suggested that Israel was committing genocide in Gaza.{{sfn|Sultany|2024|p=4}} Multiple public declarations from journals and academic organisations have warned of a potential genocide and declared opposition to an ongoing genocide.<ref name="twailr"/><ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted||{{harvnb|Segal|Daniele|2024|pp=5–6}}|{{harvnb|Narea|Samuel|2023}}|{{harvnb|Johnson|2023}}|{{harvnb|Segal|2023}}|{{#invoke:Cite|web|date=11 March 2024 |title=MESA Board Joint Statement with CAF regarding the ongoing genocidal violence against the Palestinian people and their cultural heritage in Gaza |url=https://mesana.org/advocacy/letters-from-the-board/2024/03/11/mesa-board-joint-statement-with-caf-regarding-the-ongoing-genocidal-violence-against-the-palestinian-people-and-their-cultural-heritage-in-gaza |publisher=[[Middle East Studies Association]] |access-date=14 March 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240314081322/https://mesana.org/advocacy/letters-from-the-board/2024/03/11/mesa-board-joint-statement-with-caf-regarding-the-ongoing-genocidal-violence-against-the-palestinian-people-and-their-cultural-heritage-in-gaza |archive-date=14 March 2024}}}}</ref>{{sfn|International State Crime Initiative|2023}}

In January 2024, a number of prominent Israelis, represented by the human-rights lawyer [[Michael Sfard]], sent Israel's attorney general and state prosecutor an open letter detailing examples of "the discourse of annihilation, expulsion and revenge".<ref name="Graham-Harrison & Kierszenbaum 2024">{{#invoke:Cite|news|last1=Graham-Harrison |first1=Emma |last2=Kierszenbaum |first2=Quique |date=3 January 2024 |title=Israeli public figures accuse judiciary of ignoring incitement to genocide in Gaza |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2024/jan/03/israeli-public-figures-accuse-judiciary-of-ignoring-incitement-to-genocide-in-gaza |access-date=6 January 2024 |work=[[The Guardian]] |language=en-GB |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240128043046/https://www.guardian.com/world/2024/jan/03/israeli-public-figures-accuse-judiciary-of-ignoring-incitement-to-genocide-in-gaza |archive-date=28 January 2024}}</ref> The signatories said the Israeli judiciary was ignoring incitement to genocide in Gaza.<ref name="Graham-Harrison & Kierszenbaum 2024" /> In January 2024, the American political scientist and international relations scholar [[John Mearsheimer]] wrote that, while he had believed during the first two months of the war that Israel was "guilty of serious war crimes", once the [[2023 Gaza war ceasefire]] ended, it "became clear" to him "that Israeli leaders were in fact seeking to physically destroy a substantial portion of Gaza's Palestinian population".<ref>{{#invoke:Cite|web|last=Mearsheimer |first=John J. |author-link=John Mearsheimer |date=4 January 2024 |title=Genocide in Gaza |url=https://mearsheimer.substack.com/p/genocide-in-gaza |access-date=3 April 2025 |website=John's Substack |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250726142901/https://mearsheimer.substack.com/p/genocide-in-gaza |archive-date=26 July 2025}}</ref> [[William Schabas]], an expert in [[international criminal law]],{{sfn|Currie|2011}} said that South Africa's case was the strongest of all recent genocide cases at the [[International Court of Justice]], citing the destruction of Gazan infrastructure and statements by Israeli politicians that Gazans are "human animals" and that Israel would deny them electricity, water, and medical care.<ref>{{#invoke:Cite|news|date=28 June 2024 |access-date=15 July 2024 |language=en |title=International laws against genocide exist: so why don't they work? |url=https://www.cbc.ca/radio/ideas/genocide-convention-william-schabas-1.7249721 |work=[[CBC/Radio-Canada|CBC]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240714231001/https://www.cbc.ca/radio/ideas/genocide-convention-william-schabas-1.7249721 |archive-date=14 July 2024}}</ref><ref>{{#invoke:Cite|news|last=Marin |first=Stephanie |date=4 October 2024 |title=Le déchirement autour du mot «génocide» |language=fr |trans-title=The rift around the word "genocide" |url=https://www.ledevoir.com/monde/moyen-orient/821121/y-il-genocide-gaza |work=[[Le Devoir]] |archive-url=https://archive.today/20250312184658/https://www.ledevoir.com/monde/moyen-orient/821121/y-il-genocide-gaza |archive-date=12 March 2025}}</ref><ref>{{#invoke:Cite|news|last=Sansour |first=Leila |date=10 January 2024 |access-date=15 July 2024 |language=en |work=[[ITV (TV network)|ITV]] |title=South Africa accuses Israel of genocide: Everything we know about the landmark court case |url=https://www.itv.com/news/2024-01-10/south-africa-accuses-israel-of-genocide-everything-we-know-about-the-case |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240110190756/https://www.itv.com/news/2024-01-10/south-africa-accuses-israel-of-genocide-everything-we-know-about-the-case |archive-date=10 January 2024}}</ref>

On 26 January 2024, the ICJ issued a preliminary ruling finding that the rights asserted in [[South Africa's genocide case against Israel|South Africa's filing]] were "plausible", and an order requiring that Israel take all measures in its power to prevent acts of genocide, prevent and punish incitement to genocide, and allow basic humanitarian services into Gaza.<ref name="ICJruling"/><ref name="Donoghue">{{harvnb|Donoghue|2024|loc=5:10}} ("The court decided that the Palestinians had a plausible right to be protected from genocide, and that South Africa had the right to present that claim in the court."); [[#ICJ-order-2024-01-26|Order, ''S. Afr.'', No. 192 (ICJ 26 January 2024)]], ¶ 54 ("In the Court's view, the facts and circumstances mentioned above are sufficient to conclude that at least some of the rights claimed by South Africa and for which it is seeking protection are plausible. This is the case with respect to the right of the Palestinians in Gaza to be protected from acts of genocide and related prohibited acts identified in Article III, and the right of South Africa to seek Israel's compliance with the latter's obligations under the Convention.").</ref> Judge ad hoc [[Aharon Barak]] dissented from the majority's view that genocide-related rights were "plausible", writing that South Africa had not demonstrated genocidal intent on Israel's part.<ref>{{cite web |title=Application of the Convention on the Prevention and Punishment of the Crime of Genocide in the Gaza Strip (South Africa v. Israel), Separate Opinion of Judge ad hoc Barak |date=26 January 2024 |url=https://www.icj-cij.org/case/192 |publisher=International Court of Justice |access-date=1 December 2025}}</ref>

On 15 May 2024, a report by the [[University Network for Human Rights]], [[Boston University School of Law]], [[Cornell Law School]], [[University of Pretoria]], and the [[Yale Law School]] found that "Israel has committed genocidal acts".<ref name="Bouranova"/><ref>{{Cite web |date=15 May 2024 |title=Genocide in Gaza: Analysis of International Law and its Application to Israel's Military Actions since October 7, 2023 |url=https://www.humanrightsnetwork.org/publications/genocide-in-gaza |access-date=30 September 2025 |website=University Network for Human Rights |language=en-US |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251001005253/https://www.humanrightsnetwork.org/publications/genocide-in-gaza |archive-date=1 October 2025}}</ref> In a May 2024 interview, Human Rights Watch co-founder [[Aryeh Neier]] detailed how Israel's blocking of aid and the subsequent starvation of Gaza's population is indicative of genocide.{{sfn|Zakaria|2024}}

On 1 June 2024, professor of international law {{ill|Daniel-Erasmus Khan|de|Daniel-Erasmus Khan}} said there was no clear evidence of a special intent among Israeli leadership.<ref>{{cite news |last=Henrich |first=Jan |date=1 June 2024 |title=Krieg in Gaza: Was Gerichte zum Völkermord-Vorwurf sagen |trans-title=What courts say about the genocide accusation |url=https://www.zdf.de/nachrichten/politik/ausland/israel-vorwurf-voelkermord-palaestinenser-gericht-gazastreifen-100.html |access-date=21 February 2025 |work=[[heute]] |publisher=[[ZDF]] |language=de |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250125155540/https://www.zdf.de/nachrichten/politik/ausland/israel-vorwurf-voelkermord-palaestinenser-gericht-gazastreifen-100.html |archive-date=25 January 2025}}</ref> A June 2024 report by the [[University Network for Human Rights]] and [[Boston University School of Law]] found that "Israel has committed genocidal acts".<ref name="Bouranova"/> In an August 2024 op-ed, [[Eli Rosenbaum]], a lawyer and former director of the [[Office of Special Investigations (United States Department of Justice)|United States Department of Justice's Office of Special Investigations]], wrote that Israel's actions in Gaza were not genocidal since it was aiming to "prevent genocide" by Hamas.<ref>{{cite news |last=Rosenbaum |first=Eli M. |author-link=Eli Rosenbaum |date=11 August 2024 |title=The big lie of genocide & Gaza: Seven experts on Nazi genocide expose the canard of Israeli 'crimes' |url=https://www.nydailynews.com/2024/08/11/the-big-lie-of-genocide-gaza-seven-experts-on-nazi-genocide-expose-the-canard-of-israeli-crimes/ |access-date=10 September 2024 |work=[[New York Daily News]] |language=en-US |archive-url=https://archive.today/20240812191410/https://www.nydailynews.com/2024/08/11/the-big-lie-of-genocide-gaza-seven-experts-on-nazi-genocide-expose-the-canard-of-israeli-crimes/ |archive-date=12 August 2024}}</ref>

In October 2024, Professor [[Conor Gearty]] called Israel genocidal, pointing to the continued attacks on schools and hospitals and the lack of internal investigations by Israeli authorities into potential crimes.<ref>{{#invoke:Cite|web|last=Gearty |first=Conor |author-link=Conor Gearty |date=26 October 2024 |title=Homeland Insecurity. Launch LSE 24 October 2024 |url=https://conorgearty.co.uk/2024/10/homeland-insecurity-launch-lse-24-october-2024/ |website=Conor Gearty |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250324111202/https://conorgearty.co.uk/2024/10/homeland-insecurity-launch-lse-24-october-2024/ |archive-date=24 March 2025}}</ref> Some scholars, particularly those associated with [[Third World approaches to international law]], have argued that the international community's failure to treat Israel's actions in Gaza as genocide and respond accordingly has harmed the principles of the [[international order]] and international law itself, and exposed the deficiencies of international governance.<ref name="Baars 2024">{{#invoke:Cite|web|last=Baars |first=Grietje |date=19 February 2024 |title=The uses of Marxist theory of law during a genocide |url=https://criticallegalthinking.com/2024/02/19/the-uses-of-marxist-theory-of-law-during-a-genocide/ |access-date=8 May 2025 |website=Critical Legal Thinking |language=en-US |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250508014644/https://criticallegalthinking.com/2024/02/19/the-uses-of-marxist-theory-of-law-during-a-genocide/ |archive-date=8 May 2025}}</ref><ref name="Barreto 2024">{{#invoke:Cite|web|last=Barreto |first=José Manuel |date=8 October 2024 |title=Rethinking International Law After Gaza Symposium: The Palestinian Genocide and the Colonial Core of International Law |url=https://opiniojuris.org/2024/10/08/rethinking-international-law-after-gaza-symposium-the-palestinian-genocide-and-the-colonial-core-of-international-law/ |access-date=8 May 2025 |website=[[Opinio Juris (blog)|Juris]] |language=en-US |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250508014645/https://opiniojuris.org/2024/10/08/rethinking-international-law-after-gaza-symposium-the-palestinian-genocide-and-the-colonial-core-of-international-law/ |archive-date=8 May 2025}}</ref>{{sfn|Englert|Bhattacharyya|2024|p=}}{{pn|date=August 2025}} José Manuel Barreto{{who2|date=January 2026}} argues that "the Palestinian genocide has unveiled the deep colonial structure of the international legal order" and identifies events in Gaza with the history of genocides in the colonised world, which he says the [[Westphalian system]] has historically failed to prevent.<ref name="Barreto 2024" />

In December 2024, Amnesty International published a report accusing Israel of committing genocide.<ref>{{cite news|last=Magdy |first=Sam |date=5 December 2024 |url=https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-hamas-war-rights-amnesty-genocide-19aa8fb76f7271942e73d5d7a42434e0 |title=Amnesty International says Israel is committing genocide in Gaza. Israel rejects the allegations |work=[[Associated Press]] |access-date=17 December 2024 |archive-date=17 December 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20241217174023/https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-hamas-war-rights-amnesty-genocide-19aa8fb76f7271942e73d5d7a42434e0 |url-status=live}}</ref><ref>{{cite magazine |last=Lanard |first=Noah |date=5 December 2024 |url=https://www.motherjones.com/politics/2024/12/israel-genocide-gaza-amnesty-international-report/ |title=Amnesty International: Israel is guilty of genocide in Gaza |magazine=[[Mother Jones (magazine)|Mother Jones]] |access-date=17 December 2024 |archive-date=10 December 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20241210022113/https://www.motherjones.com/politics/2024/12/israel-genocide-gaza-amnesty-international-report/ |url-status=live}}</ref><ref>{{cite web |last=Haque |first=Adil Ahmad |author-link=Adil Ahmad Haque |date=16 December 2024 |url=https://www.justsecurity.org/105629/amnesty-international-gaza-genocide-report/ |title=The Amnesty International Report on Genocide in Gaza |website=Just Security |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20241220103911/https://www.justsecurity.org/105629/amnesty-international-gaza-genocide-report/ |archive-date=20 December 2024}}</ref> After the Amnesty report, Human Rights Watch also said Israel had committed "genocidal acts" and that Israeli officials statements may indicate genocidal intent.<ref>{{cite news |last=Geller |first=Adam |date=19 December 2024 |url=https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-hamas-gaza-genocide-human-rights-watch-0cae5c250415975ebbfcfdab6808abc4 |title=Human Rights Watch says Israel's restriction of water supply in Gaza amounts to acts of genocide |work=[[Associated Press]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20241220100513/https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-hamas-gaza-genocide-human-rights-watch-0cae5c250415975ebbfcfdab6808abc4 |archive-date=20 December 2024}}</ref>

In April 2025, the barrister [[Michael Mansfield]] said there was "no question" that genocide was occurring.<ref>{{#invoke:Cite|news|last=Safdar |first=Anealla |date=16 April 2025 |title=Top UK barrister: Israel is carrying out 'destruction of humanity' in Gaza |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/4/16/top-uk-barrister-israel-is-carrying-out-destruction-of-humanity-in-gaza |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250419150140/https://www.aljazeera.com/amp/news/2025/4/16/top-uk-barrister-israel-is-carrying-out-destruction-of-humanity-in-gaza |archive-date=19 April 2025}}</ref> In May 2025, Luigi Daniele, a lecturer at [[Nottingham Law School]], noted a link between the IDF's justification for its conduct in Gaza and the [[Rapid Support Forces]] rationale in the [[Sudanese civil war (2023–present)|Sudanese civil war]], saying it "reveals the emergence of a template to commit mass extermination and even genocide".{{sfn|Nashed|2025}} In May 2024 the scholar Nimer Sultany supported [[Forensic Architecture]]'s assessment that Israel had weaponised international humanitarian law into "humanitarian violence".{{sfn|Sultany|2024|pp=10–11}} This was supported in July by Professor [[Neve Gordon]] and the anthropologist [[Nicola Perugini]], who argued that Israel used "the law itself as a tool legitimizing genocide".{{sfn|Perugini|Gordon|2024}}

In June 2025, Ambos and scholar {{ill|Stefanie Bock|de|Stefanie Bock (Rechtswissenschaftlerin)}} wrote that it has become more difficult to deny genocidal intent.<ref>{{#invoke:Cite|journal|last1=Ambos |first1=Kai |author1-link=Kai Ambos |last2=Bock |first2=Stefanie |author2-link=:de:Stefanie Bock (Rechtswissenschaftlerin) |date=4 June 2025 |title=Genocide in Gaza? |url=https://verfassungsblog.de/genocide-in-gaza/ |access-date=9 July 2025 |journal=[[Verfassungsblog]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250624141521/https://verfassungsblog.de/genocide-in-gaza/ |archive-date=24 June 2025 |url-status=live}}</ref>

In July 2025, 1,300 professionals and academics in public health, health care, and the social sciences signed a letter acknowledging the Gaza genocide.{{sfn|De Vogli|Montomoli|Abu-Sittah|Pappé|2025|p=1}} According to professor Ernesto Verdeja, even by "the most inflexible interpretation of genocide, Gaza qualifies as genocidal".{{sfn|Verdeja|2025|p=8}} In July 2025, {{lang|fr|[[Le Monde]]}} reported that legal experts remained divided on the question, with some agreeing that Israel was committing genocide and others viewing the charge as unsubstantiated.<ref name="Ayad 2025">{{cite news |last=Ayad |first=Christophe |date=27 July 2025 |title=Is there a genocide in Gaza? Why legal experts are split |work=[[Le Monde]] |url=https://www.lemonde.fr/en/opinion/article/2025/07/27/is-there-a-genocide-in-gaza-why-legal-experts-are-split_6743780_23.html |access-date=1 December 2025 |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250727161927/https://www.lemonde.fr/en/opinion/article/2025/07/27/is-there-a-genocide-in-gaza-why-legal-experts-are-split_6743780_23.html |archive-date=27 July 2025}}</ref> Bartov wrote that the silence of many scholars of the Holocaust and Holocaust commemoration institutions and their disbelief that Israel could commit war crimes, crimes against humanity, ethnic cleansing, or genocide threatens [[Universalism|universalist]] interpretations of Holocaust studies and Holocaust commemoration and may lead to a decline in the relevance of Holocaust education.<ref>{{#invoke:Cite|news|date=17 July 2025 |title="I'm a Genocide Scholar. I Know It When I See It": Prof. Omer Bartov on the Growing Consensus on Gaza |url=https://www.democracynow.org/2025/7/17/omer_bartov |access-date=18 July 2025 |work=[[Democracy Now!]] |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250725080837/https://www.democracynow.org/2025/7/17/omer_bartov |archive-date=25 July 2025}}</ref><ref>{{#invoke:Cite|news|last=Bartov |first=Omer |author-link=Omer Bartov |date=15 July 2025 |title=Opinion {{!}} I'm a Genocide Scholar. I Know It When I See It. |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2025/07/15/opinion/israel-gaza-holocaust-genocide-palestinians.html |access-date=18 July 2025 |work=[[The New York Times]] |language=en-US |archive-url=https://archive.today/20250731052733/https://www.nytimes.com/2025/07/15/opinion/israel-gaza-holocaust-genocide-palestinians.html |archive-date=31 July 2025}}</ref> Journalist Colin Jones interviewed lawyers affiliated with the US military and concluded that they see Gaza as a test case for what military conduct might be acceptable in a hypothetical war between the US and a peer power such as China.<ref name="Jones 2025">{{#invoke:Cite|magazine|last=Jones |first=Colin |date=25 April 2025 |title=What's Legally Allowed in War |url=https://www.newyorker.com/news/the-lede/whats-legally-allowed-in-war |access-date=26 July 2025 |magazine=[[The New Yorker]] |language=en-US |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250715150411/https://www.newyorker.com/news/the-lede/whats-legally-allowed-in-war |archive-date=15 July 2025}}</ref> 

In August 2025, according to Mia Swart, a growing consensus was emerging "in international legal circles that Israel is committing genocide".{{sfn|Swart|2025|p=3}} [[Craig Mokhiber]], a retired UN human rights lawyer, wrote, "Never, in the modern era, have we seen such a clear-cut, article-by-article violation of the United Nations Genocide Convention, so broad a consensus in the identification of the crime".<ref name="Mokhiber">{{cite journal |last1=Mokhiber |first1=Craig |date=March 2025 |title=Law on trial: Gaza and the future of the international legal order |journal=Dialectical Anthropology |volume=49 |issue=1 |pages=121–144 |doi=10.1007/s10624-025-09764-0}}</ref>

===Other scholars===
In March 2024, the [[Middle East Studies Association]] condemned the "accelerating scale of genocidal violence being inflicted on the Palestinian population of Gaza", saying that Israel's conduct constituted [[cultural genocide]].<ref>{{cite news |last1=Motamedi |first1=Maziar |last2=Siddiqui |first2=Usaid |date=11 March 2024 |title=Middle East Studies Association denounces Israel's 'cultural genocide' in Gaza |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/3/11/israels-war-on-gaza-live-ramadan-begins-with-no-end-to-israels-siege?update=2766040 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=14 March 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240312000648/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/3/11/israels-war-on-gaza-live-ramadan-begins-with-no-end-to-israels-siege?update=2766040 |archive-date=12 March 2024}}</ref> Surveys of 758 Middle East scholars by the [[Brookings Institution]] indicated a growing consensus that Israel's military campaign in Gaza was genocide.<ref>{{Cite web |last1=Lynch |first1=Marc |last2=Telhami |first2=Shibley |date=20 June 2024 |url=https://www.brookings.edu/articles/gloom-about-the-day-after-the-gaza-war-pervasive-among-mideast-scholars/ |title=Gloom about the 'day after' the Gaza war pervasive among Mideast scholars |publisher=[[Brookings Institution|Brookings]] |access-date=29 June 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240626215734/https://www.brookings.edu/articles/gloom-about-the-day-after-the-gaza-war-pervasive-among-mideast-scholars/ |archive-date=26 June 2024}}</ref><ref>{{cite web |author=<!--Not stated--> |date=21 June 2024 |title=2021 Middle East Scholar Barometer #7 (May 23 – June 6, 2024) |url=https://criticalissues.umd.edu/middle-east-scholar-barometer |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240626215735/https://criticalissues.umd.edu/middle-east-scholar-barometer|archive-date=26 June 2024 |access-date=29 June 2024 |work=Critical Issues Poll |publisher=[[University of Maryland]]}}</ref><ref name="MESB 2025">{{cite web |title=Middle East Scholar Barometer #8 (January 31–February 19, 2025) |url=https://criticalissues.umd.edu/sites/criticalissues.umd.edu/files/Questionnaire_MESB2025.pdf |website=University of Maryland Critical Issues Poll |publisher=University of Maryland and George Washington University Project on Middle East Political Science |date=February 2025 |access-date=5 September 2025 |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251006025947/https://criticalissues.umd.edu/sites/criticalissues.umd.edu/files/Questionnaire_MESB2025.pdf |archive-date=6 October 2025 |url-status=dead }}</ref>

In 2025, [[John Spencer (military officer)|John Spencer]], chair of urban warfare studies at the [[Modern War Institute]] at the [[United States Military Academy]], argued that Israel had not demonstrated genocidal intent, based on what he called "evidence of what Israel is doing to preserve infrastructure, civilian life, to provide services".<ref>{{cite news |last=Inskeep |first=Steve |date=29 July 2025 |title=War scholar discusses why he does not think there is a genocide in Gaza |work=[[NPR]] |url=https://www.npr.org/2025/07/29/nx-s1-5478643/war-scholar-discusses-why-he-does-not-think-there-is-a-genocide-in-gaza |access-date=18 November 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251112100804/https://www.npr.org/2025/07/29/nx-s1-5478643/war-scholar-discusses-why-he-does-not-think-there-is-a-genocide-in-gaza |archive-date=12 November 2025}}</ref>

[[Robert Satloff]] of the [[Washington Institute for Near East Policy]] criticized the IAGS genocide resolution for its sourcing and for lacking independent research, noting that it passed with the support of "only one-fifth{{nbsp}}... of the organization’s membership", though he wrote that his "critique of the IAGS resolution should not be misread as endorsement of Israeli strategy and tactics in Gaza or indifference to the terrible human toll in this conflict".<ref>{{cite web |last1=Satloff |first1=Robert |title=A Charade in Academic Garb |url=https://www.washingtoninstitute.org/policy-analysis/charade-academic-garb |website=[[Washington Institute for Near East Policy]] |access-date=23 December 2025 |date=2 September 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250912004555/https://www.washingtoninstitute.org/policy-analysis/charade-academic-garb |archive-date=12 September 2025}}</ref>

== Legal proceedings ==
=== International Court of Justice application ===
{{main|South Africa's genocide case against Israel}}

[[File:International stances on South Africa v. Israel lawsuit.svg|thumb|Stances of states on [[South Africa's genocide case against Israel|''South Africa v. Israel'']]:{{legend|#3f612d|South Africa}} {{legend|#6da84d|Countries that have supported South Africa's case}} {{legend|#3d62a4|Countries that have opposed South Africa's case}} {{legend|#213659|Israel}}]]
In December 2023, [[South Africa]] instituted proceedings at the [[International Court of Justice]] pursuant to the [[Genocide Convention]], accusing Israel of committing genocide, war crimes, and crimes against humanity against Palestinians in Gaza.<ref name="Chao-Fong et al. 2023">{{cite news |last1=Chao-Fong |first1=Léonie |last2=Belam |first2=Martin |last3=Ahmad |first3=Reged |date=29 December 2023 |title=Israel-Gaza war live: Israel hits back at South Africa after it launches genocide case at UN's top court |language=en |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/live/2023/dec/29/israel-gaza-war-live-updates-hamas-egypt-delegation-ceasefire-cairo |access-date=29 December 2023 |work=[[The Guardian]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240115013657/https://www.theguardian.com/world/live/2023/dec/29/israel-gaza-war-live-updates-hamas-egypt-delegation-ceasefire-cairo |archive-date=15 January 2024}}</ref><ref name="ICJ-2023-12-29">{{cite web |url=https://www.icj-cij.org/sites/default/files/case-related/192/192-20231228-app-01-00-en.pdf |title=Application Instituting Proceedings, Application of Convention on Prevention and Punishment of Crime of Genocide (S. Afr. v. Isr.), No. 192 |website=[[International Court of Justice|ICJ]] |date=29 December 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240105144115/https://www.icj-cij.org/index.php/node/203394 |archive-date=5 January 2024}}</ref><ref name="AP 2023">{{cite news |date=29 December 2023 |title=South Africa launches case at top UN court accusing Israel of genocide in Gaza |url=https://apnews.com/article/south-africa-israel-un-court-palestinians-genocide-ffe672c4eb3e14a30128542eaa537b21 |access-date=3 January 2024 |work=[[Associated Press]] |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240122062939/https://apnews.com/article/south-africa-israel-un-court-palestinians-genocide-ffe672c4eb3e14a30128542eaa537b21 |archive-date=22 January 2024}}</ref> South African president [[Cyril Ramaphosa]] [[Israeli apartheid|compared Israel's actions]] to [[apartheid]].<ref>{{cite news |last=Carl |first=Traci |date=29 December 2023 |title=South Africa accuses Israel of genocide in a U.N. court. |language=en-US |work=[[The New York Times]] |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2023/12/29/world/middleeast/south-africa-israel-genocide.html |access-date=30 December 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240117041902/https://www.nytimes.com/2023/12/29/world/middleeast/south-africa-israel-genocide.html |archive-date=17 January 2024}}</ref> Several [[South Africa v. Israel (Genocide Convention)#Other international responses|international organisations and other nations]] supported South Africa's suit.<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
| {{harvnb|Roelf|Sterling|2023}}
| {{harvnb|Rifai|2024}}
| {{harvnb|Conley|2024}}
| {{harvnb|Jimoh|2024}}
| {{Cite news |title=South Africa's ICJ Case Against Israel Backed by Over 1,000 Organizations |work= [[Palestine Chronicle]] |date=10 January 2024 |url=https://www.palestinechronicle.com/south-africas-icj-case-against-israel-backed-by-over-1000-organizations/ |access-date=13 January 2024 |archive-date=12 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240112210235/https://www.palestinechronicle.com/south-africas-icj-case-against-israel-backed-by-over-1000-organizations/ |url-status=live}}
| {{harvnb|Shamim|2024}}
}}</ref><ref name="Progressive International 2024">{{cite web |title=We Support South Africa's Genocide Convention Case Against Israel |publisher=[[Progressive International]] |date=8 January 2024 |url=https://progressive.international/wire/2024-01-08-we-support-south-africas-genocide-convention-case-against-israel/en/ |access-date=8 January 2024 |archive-date=8 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240108224921/https://progressive.international/wire/2024-01-08-we-support-south-africas-genocide-convention-case-against-israel/en/ |url-status=live}}</ref>

In its application, South Africa argued that Israel's actions "are genocidal in character because they are intended to bring about the destruction of a substantial part of the Palestinian national, racial and ethnical group".<ref name="ICJ-2023-12-29"/>{{sfn|Corder|2024}} South Africa requested that the ICJ issue an [[interim order]] requiring Israel to "immediately suspend its military operations in and against Gaza".<ref name="ICJ-2023-12-29"/>{{sfn|Corder|2024}}

On 26 January 2024, the ICJ issued a preliminary ruling finding that the rights asserted in South Africa's filing were "plausible" and issued an order requiring that Israel take all measures in its power to prevent acts of genocide, prevent and punish incitement to genocide, and allow basic humanitarian services into Gaza.<ref name="ICJruling"/><ref name="Donoghue"/> Later that year, South Africa asked the ICJ to order additional measures against Israel,<ref>{{cite news |date=6 March 2024 |title=South Africa asks World Court for more measures against Israel |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/south-africa-asks-world-court-more-measures-against-israel-2024-03-06/ |work=[[Reuters]] |archive-url=https://archive.today/20240306223624/https://www.reuters.com/world/south-africa-asks-world-court-more-measures-against-israel-2024-03-06/ |archive-date=6 March 2024}}</ref> and in May, the court issued what some experts considered to be an ambiguous order but which was widely understood as requiring Israel to immediately halt its [[Rafah offensive|offensive in Rafah]].<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
| {{harvnb|Taub|2024}}
| {{harvnb|Wintour|2024}}: "a directive widely seen to have instructed Israel to completely stop its military offensive"
| {{harvnb|Clayton|2024a}}: "It was widely viewed as an unambiguous statement: The top United Nations court ordered Israel to immediately halt its military assault on Rafah—a dramatic intervention that left the nation and its chief ally, the U.S., increasingly isolated on the world stage."
| {{harvnb|Haque|2024a}}
}}</ref> Israel rejected this interpretation and continued its offensive.{{sfn|Casciani|2024b}}

The Israeli government spokesman [[Eylon Levy]] rejected the allegations "with disgust"<ref name="AP 2023"/> and accused South Africa of cooperating with Hamas,<ref name="Chao-Fong et al. 2023"/> calling South Africa's claims "[[blood libel]]".<ref>{{Cite news |date=29 December 2023 |title=South Africa launches case at The Hague accusing Israel of genocide in Gaza |url=https://www.heraldscotland.com/news/national/24018477.south-africa-launches-case-hague-accusing-israel-genocide-gaza/ |access-date=29 December 2023 |work=[[The Herald (Glasgow)|The Herald]] |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240118081223/https://www.heraldscotland.com/news/national/24018477.south-africa-launches-case-hague-accusing-israel-genocide-gaza/ |archive-date=18 January 2024}}</ref> On 2 January 2024, Israel decided to appear before the ICJ in response to South Africa's case, despite a history of ignoring international tribunals.{{sfn|Corder|2024}} On 13 January, Netanyahu said, "No one will stop us. Not The Hague, not the [[Axis of Resistance|Axis of Evil]], no one."<ref>{{cite news |last1=Al-Mughrabi |first1=Nidal |date=13 January 2024 |title=Israel pushes ahead with Gaza offensive approaching 100 days of war |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/israel-presses-with-gaza-offensive-approaching-100-days-war-2024-01-13/ |work=[[Reuters]] |access-date=14 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240127095016/https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/israel-presses-with-gaza-offensive-approaching-100-days-war-2024-01-13/ |archive-date=27 January 2024}}</ref> Israeli officials accused the court of antisemitic bias.<ref name="McKernan 2024">{{cite news |last=McKernan |first=Bethan |date=26 January 2024 |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2024/jan/26/israeli-officials-accuse-international-court-of-justice-of-antisemitic-bias |title=Israeli officials accuse international court of justice of antisemitic bias |work=[[The Guardian]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240227184626/https://www.theguardian.com/world/2024/jan/26/israeli-officials-accuse-international-court-of-justice-of-antisemitic-bias |archive-date=27 February 2024}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |date=26 January 2024 |title='Not only false, it's outrageous': Netanyahu rejects Gaza genocide charges |url=https://www.nbcnews.com/video/netanyahu-rejects-outrageous-icj-charges-of-gaza-genocide-203021381942 |work=[[NBC News]] |access-date=28 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240130123637/https://www.nbcnews.com/video/netanyahu-rejects-outrageous-icj-charges-of-gaza-genocide-203021381942 |archive-date=30 January 2024}}</ref> Israel asserted that that it had taken all possible measures to safeguard civilians during its military campaign in Gaza.<ref>{{cite news |last=Quell |first=Molly |title=Israel insists it is doing all it can to protect civilians in Gaza and denies genocide charges |work=[[Associated Press]] |date=7 May 2024 |url=https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-gaza-rafah-un-world-court-2f739ad4f64ff3a8186a423ad8f350e8 |access-date=19 October 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251004163645/https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-gaza-rafah-un-world-court-2f739ad4f64ff3a8186a423ad8f350e8 |archive-date=4 October 2025}}</ref>{{sfn|McDoom|2024|pp=5–6}} Some [[Left-wing politics in Israel|left-wing Israeli politicians]], including [[Ofer Cassif]], supported South Africa's case.<ref>{{cite news |title=MK Ofer Cassif joins lawsuit against Israel in the ICJ |url=https://www.jpost.com/breaking-news/article-781194 |access-date=8 January 2024 |work=[[The Jerusalem Post]] |date=7 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240108060131/https://www.jpost.com/breaking-news/article-781194 |archive-date=8 January 2024}}</ref>

International Court of Justice Vice President [[Julia Sebutinde]] was one of the 17 judges ruling on provisional measures in [[South Africa's genocide case against Israel]]. She voted against all the provisional measures, and was the only [[Judges of the International Court of Justice#Permanent judges|permanent judge]] to vote against any of the measures.<ref>{{cite news |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/8/27/why-icj-judge-sebutinde-faces-calls-to-quit-from-israel-genocide-case |title=Why ICJ Judge Sebutinde faces calls to quit from Israel genocide case |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |date=27 August 2025 |access-date=28 December 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251228000416/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/8/27/why-icj-judge-sebutinde-faces-calls-to-quit-from-israel-genocide-case |archive-date=28 December 2025}}</ref><ref name=jta-20240126>{{cite news |url=https://www.jta.org/2024/01/26/politics/international-court-of-justice-rules-that-some-allegations-of-israel-committing-genocide-are-plausible |title=International Court of Justice rules that some allegations of Israel committing genocide are 'plausible' |last=Kampeas |first=Ron |website=[[Jewish Telegraphic Agency]] |date=26 January 2024 |access-date=18 November 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251229003507/https://www.jta.org/2024/01/26/politics/international-court-of-justice-rules-that-some-allegations-of-israel-committing-genocide-are-plausible |archive-date=29 December 2025}}</ref> In her dissenting opinion, Sebutinde wrote, "multiple concrete actions were taken by Israel to facilitate the provision of humanitarian aid for the civilian population of Gaza."<ref>{{cite web |title=Dissenting opinion of Vice-President Sebutinde |website=[[International Court of Justice]] |date=24 May 2024 |url=https://www.icj-cij.org/node/204092 |access-date=18 November 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251229004443/https://www.icj-cij.org/node/204092 |archive-date=29 December 2025}}</ref> She was [[Julia Sebutinde#Plagiarism_controversy|accused of plagiarizing]] large parts of her dissenting opinion from pro-Israel sources,<ref>{{Cite news|title=ICJ president accused of plagiarism in dissenting opinion on Israeli occupation|url=https://www.middleeasteye.net/news/icj-president-accused-plagiarism-dissenting-opinion-israeli-occupation|work=Middle East Eye|date=27 January 2025}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=2025-01-28 |title=ICJ President Julia Sebutinde accused of 'plagiarism' in opposing opinion on Israeli occupation |url=https://today.lorientlejour.com/article/1445412/icj-president-julia-sebutinde-accused-of-plagiarism-in-opposing-opinion-on-israeli-occupation.html |access-date=2025-02-05 |website=L'Orient Today |language=en}}</ref> as well as plagiarism from [[Wikipedia]] and the [[BBC]]. According to political scientist [[Norman Finkelstein]], "at least 32 percent of Sebutinde’s dissent was plagiarised", including from writings from [[Douglas Feith]].<ref>{{cite news |date=3 February 2025 |title=ICJ president 'plagiarised 32 percent of pro-Israel dissenting opinion' |url=https://www.middleeasteye.net/news/fresh-allegations-emerge-plagiarism-icj-president-israel-opinion |work=Middle East Eye}}</ref>

=== International Criminal Court ===
{{main|International Criminal Court investigation in Palestine|International Criminal Court arrest warrants for Israeli leaders}}

In May 2024, Khan applied for arrest warrants against Israeli Prime Minister Netanyahu and Minister of Defence Yoav Gallant, saying he had reasonable grounds to believe they bore criminal responsibility for war crimes and crimes against humanity committed in Gaza.<ref>{{cite press release |url=https://www.icc-cpi.int/news/statement-icc-prosecutor-karim-aa-khan-kc-applications-arrest-warrants-situation-state |title=Statement of ICC Prosecutor Karim A.A. Khan KC: Applications for arrest warrants in the situation in the State of Palestine |publisher=[[International Criminal Court]] |date=20 May 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240620045322/https://www.icc-cpi.int/news/statement-icc-prosecutor-karim-aa-khan-kc-applications-arrest-warrants-situation-state |archive-date=20 June 2024}}</ref> The list of crimes did not include genocide, which is legally distinct from [[Extermination (crime)|extermination]].<ref>{{cite web |last=Luban |first=David |date=22 May 2024 |title=What the ICC Prosecutor Charged – and Didn't Charge – in Gaza Warrants |url=https://www.justsecurity.org/95985/icc-gaza-warrant-charges/ |access-date=19 August 2024 |website=[[justsecurity.org|Just Security]] |language=en-US |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240703062415/https://www.justsecurity.org/95985/icc-gaza-warrant-charges/ |archive-date=3 July 2024}}</ref> The warrants were issued in November 2024.<ref name="El Abdallah 2024"/>

As part of a December 2024 report accusing Israel of genocide, Amnesty International called on the ICC "to urgently consider the commission of the crime of genocide by Israeli officials since 7 October 2023 in the ongoing investigation into the situation in the State of Palestine".<ref name="AmnestyGenocideConclusion">{{cite web |url=https://www.amnesty.org/en/latest/news/2024/12/amnesty-international-concludes-israel-is-committing-genocide-against-palestinians-in-gaza/ |title=Amnesty International concludes Israel is committing genocide against Palestinians in Gaza |date=5 December 2024 |website=[[Amnesty International]] |archive-date=19 January 2025}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |last=Ferrer |first=Isabel |date=5 December 2024 |archive-date=20 January 2025}}</ref> Also in December 2024, the Israeli law professor Omer Shatz filed a complaint with the ICC naming eight Israeli political and media figures he believed were responsible for incitement to genocide.<ref>{{cite news |last=Nechin |first=Etan |date=24 January 2025 |url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2025-01-24/ty-article-magazine/.premium/the-israeli-lawyer-filing-a-landmark-genocide-case-against-israel-at-the-icc/00000194-59bf-d76e-a7dd-7bff42610000 |archive-date=24 January 2025}}</ref> On 1 October 2025, a complaint was filed with the ICC accusing Italian Prime Minister [[Giorgia Meloni]] and other officials of genocide for their support of Israel.<ref>{{cite news |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/10/8/italys-meloni-says-icc-complaint-accuses-her-of-gaza-genocide-complicity |title=Italy's Meloni says ICC complaint accuses her of Gaza genocide complicity |newspaper=[[Al Jazeera]] |date=8 October 2025 |first=Lyndal |last=Rowlands |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251230044214/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/10/8/italys-meloni-says-icc-complaint-accuses-her-of-gaza-genocide-complicity |archive-date=30 December 2025}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |url=https://www.lemonde.fr/en/international/article/2025/10/07/meloni-says-accused-of-complicity-in-genocide-at-world-court_6746197_4.html |title=Meloni says ICC complaint accuses her of complicity in Gaza genocide |newspaper=[[Le Monde]] |date=8 October 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251230044415/https://www.lemonde.fr/en/international/article/2025/10/07/meloni-says-accused-of-complicity-in-genocide-at-world-court_6746197_4.html |archive-date=30 December 2025}}</ref> The US and Israel have politically pressured and imposed sanctions on the ICC due to its positions during the war.<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted||{{harvnb|Iraqi|2024}}|{{harvnb|Davies|McKernan|Abraham|Rapoport|2024}}|{{harvnb|Team Zeteo|Hasan|2024}}|{{cite web |date=7 February 2025 |title=US: Trump Authorizes
