=== Other proceedings ===
{{Main|Defense for Children International – Palestine v. Biden|Nicaragua v. Germany}}

In November 2023, the [[Center for Constitutional Rights]] sued US President [[Joe Biden]], Secretary of State [[Antony Blinken]], and Secretary of Defence [[Lloyd Austin]],<ref name="Mansoor 2023">{{cite magazine |last=Mansoor |first=Sanya |date=21 November 2023 |title=Pro-Palestinian Americans Are Pushing Biden to Pivot |url=https://time.com/6337911/biden-israel-policy-palestine-pressure/ |access-date=8 January 2024 |magazine=[[Time (magazine)|Time]] |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240102191717/https://time.com/6337911/biden-israel-policy-palestine-pressure/ |archive-date=2 January 2024}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last=Haigh |first=Elizabeth |date=15 November 2023 |title=Humanitarian groups sue Biden and administration officials for involvement in Israel-Hamas war |url=https://www.jurist.org/news/2023/11/humanitarian-groups-sue-biden-and-administration-officials-for-involvement-in-israel-hamas-war/ |access-date=8 January 2024 |work=[[Jurist (website)|Jurist]] |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240117233607/https://www.jurist.org/news/2023/11/humanitarian-groups-sue-biden-and-administration-officials-for-involvement-in-israel-hamas-war/ |archive-date=17 January 2024}}</ref>{{sfn|Segal|Daniele|2024|p=6}} alleging that Israel's "mass killings", targeting of civilian infrastructure, and forced expulsions amount to genocide,<ref name="McGreal 2023"/><ref name="Mansoor 2023"/> and that the US was capable of deterring Israel from committing these acts due to the countries' close relationship.<ref name="McGreal 2023"/> A [[United States federal judge|federal judge]] dismissed the case in January 2024, ruling that the [[US Constitution]] prevented his court from determining foreign policy, but writing that "as the ICJ has found, it is plausible that Israel's conduct amounts to genocide".<ref>{{Cite news |last=Hubler |first=Shawn |date=31 January 2024 |title=A federal judge dismisses a suit to block U.S. support of Israel{{snd}}but urges Biden to re-examine his approach |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2024/01/31/world/middleeast/joe-biden-israel-support.html |url-access=subscription |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240201153444/https://www.nytimes.com/2024/01/31/world/middleeast/joe-biden-israel-support.html%20 |archive-date=1 February 2024 |access-date=1 February 2024 |work=[[The New York Times]]}}</ref> The judge also commented that he would have preferred to have issued the injunction and urged Biden to rethink US policy.<ref>{{cite news |last=Borger |first=Julian |author-link=Julian Borger |date=1 February 2024 |title=Israel's campaign in Gaza 'plausibly' amounts to genocide, US court finds |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2024/feb/01/genocide-gaza-israel-california-court |access-date=2 February 2024 |work=[[The Guardian]] |language=en-GB |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240202041336/https://www.theguardian.com/world/2024/feb/01/genocide-gaza-israel-california-court |archive-date=2 February 2024}}</ref><ref name="Hanson 2023">{{cite news |last=Hanson |first=Natalie |date=13 November 2023 |title=Palestinians file lawsuit accusing Biden administration of violating Genocide Convention |url=https://www.courthousenews.com/palestinians-file-lawsuit-accusing-biden-administration-of-violating-genocide-convention/ |work=[[Courthouse News Service]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231213203151/https://www.courthousenews.com/palestinians-file-lawsuit-accusing-biden-administration-of-violating-genocide-convention/ |archive-date=13 December 2023}}</ref><ref name="Mansoor 2023" />

In February 2024, lawyers representing Palestinians in Germany filed a criminal complaint against politicians including Chancellor [[Olaf Scholz]], Foreign Minister [[Annalena Baerbock]], Economic Minister [[Robert Habeck]], and Finance Minister [[Christian Lindner]] for "aiding and abetting" genocide in Gaza.<ref name="Schaer 2024">{{cite news |last=Schaer |first=Cathrin |date=23 February 2024 |title=German lawyers sue Scholz, alleging complicity in Gaza 'genocide' |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2024/2/23/german-lawyers-sue-politicians-including-scholz-over-complicity-in-gaza |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240224051949/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2024/2/23/german-lawyers-sue-politicians-including-scholz-over-complicity-in-gaza |archive-date=24 February 2024}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |date=23 February 2024 |title=Gaza victims sue German government for 'aiding genocide against Palestinians' |url=https://www.middleeastmonitor.com/20240223-gaza-victims-sue-german-government-for-aiding-genocide-against-palestinians/ |work=[[Middle East Monitor]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240224115453/https://www.middleeastmonitor.com/20240223-gaza-victims-sue-german-government-for-aiding-genocide-against-palestinians/ |archive-date=24 February 2024}}</ref> The [[Public Prosecutor General (Germany)|Public Prosecutor General]] dismissed the complaint due to lack of [[reasonable suspicion]].<ref name="lto-2025-09-20">{{Cite web |last=Kolter |first=Max |date=20 September 2025 |title=Waffenexporte: Merz, Scholz und Co. wegen Beihilfe strafbar? |trans-title=Weapons exports: Are Merz, Scholz and Co. liable to prosecution for aiding and abetting? |url=https://www.lto.de/recht/hintergruende/h/waffen-waffenlieferungen-scholz-merz-strafantrag-beihilfe-gaza-israel-export |access-date=10 November 2025 |website={{ill|Legal Tribune Online|de}} |language=de |quote=In der Vergangenheit reagierte man in Karlsruhe auf derlei PR-Aktionen gelassen. Bereits Anfang 2024 hatte es eine Strafanzeige gegen Mitglieder der Ampel-Regierung wegen der Unterstützung Israels u.a. durch Waffenlieferungen gegeben. Man entschied sich gegen Ermittlungen – kein Anfangsverdacht. Dass sich an dieser Haltung etwas ändert, kann man sich kaum vorstellen. |trans-quote=In the past, officials in Karlsruhe reacted calmly to such [[public relations|PR]] activities. There had already been a criminal complaint in early 2024 against members of the [[Scholz cabinet|traffic light coalition]] because of support of Israel through weapons deliveries, among other reasons. The officials decided against investigations – no [[reasonable suspicion]]. It's hard to imagine that this stance is going to change. |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251218235050/https://www.lto.de/recht/hintergruende/h/waffen-waffenlieferungen-scholz-merz-strafantrag-beihilfe-gaza-israel-export |archive-date=18 December 2025}}</ref> The lawyers filed a similar complaint against current and former German government members in September 2025.<ref name="lto-2025-09-20"/><ref>{{Cite web |last= |date=19 September 2025 |title=The Time for Accountability is Now: Criminal Complaint against German Government Officials for Aiding and Abetting Israel's Genocide in Gaza |url=https://elsc.support/the-time-for-accountability-is-now-criminal-complaint-against-german-government-officials-for-aiding-and-abetting-israels-genocide-in-gaza/ |access-date=10 November 2025 |website=European Legal Support Center |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251108054432/https://elsc.support/the-time-for-accountability-is-now-criminal-complaint-against-german-government-officials-for-aiding-and-abetting-israels-genocide-in-gaza/ |archive-date=8 November 2025}}</ref>

In March 2024, the Nicaraguan government initiated proceedings against Germany at the ICJ under the Genocide Convention concerning Germany's support for Israel in the Gaza war.<ref name="mee-2024-1-1">{{cite news |date=1 March 2024 |title=Nicaragua files application to World Court, accusing Germany of complicity in Gaza genocide |url=https://www.middleeasteye.net/live-blog/live-blog-update/nicaragua-files-application-world-court-accusing-germany-complicity-gaza |work=[[Middle East Eye]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240302035942/https://www.middleeasteye.net/live-blog/live-blog-update/nicaragua-files-application-world-court-accusing-germany-complicity-gaza |archive-date=2 March 2024}}</ref>{{sfn|van den Berg|2024}} It sought [[provisional measures of protection]], including resumption of suspended German funding of the [[UNRWA]] and cessation of military supplies to Israel.{{sfn|van den Berg|2024}}

In March 2024, Birchgrove Legal referred Australian Prime Minister [[Anthony Albanese]], Foreign Minister [[Penny Wong]], Opposition Leader [[Peter Dutton]], and others to the ICC as accessories to genocide, war crimes, and crimes against humanity, citing the defunding of UNRWA, the provision of military aid, and "unequivocal political support" for Israel's actions during the Gaza war.<ref>{{Cite news |last=Wedesweiler |first=Madeleine |date=5 March 2024 |title=Anthony Albanese dismisses ICC war crimes allegations: Experts weigh in on the claims |url=https://www.sbs.com.au/news/article/anthony-albanese-dismisses-icc-war-crimes-allegations-experts-weigh-in-on-the-claims/xu4kueiql |access-date=5 March 2024 |work=[[SBS News]] |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240305094219/https://www.sbs.com.au/news/article/anthony-albanese-dismisses-icc-war-crimes-allegations-experts-weigh-in-on-the-claims/xu4kueiql |archive-date=5 March 2024}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |last=Rothwell |first=Donald |date=5 March 2024 |title=Why have Anthony Albanese and other politicians been referred to the ICC over the Gaza war? |url=http://theconversation.com/why-have-anthony-albanese-and-other-politicians-been-referred-to-the-icc-over-the-gaza-war-225079 |access-date=5 March 2024 |website=[[The Conversation (website)|The Conversation]] |language=en-US |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240305092042/https://theconversation.com/why-have-anthony-albanese-and-other-politicians-been-referred-to-the-icc-over-the-gaza-war-225079 |archive-date=5 March 2024}}</ref>{{Importance inline|date=November 2025}}

In November 2025, the Chief Public Prosecutor's Office in [[Turkey]] issued arrest warrants for 37 Israeli suspects on charges of genocide and crimes against humanity. Officials named in the Turkish indictment included Netanyahu, security minister [[Itamar Ben-Gvir]], defence minister [[Israel Katz]] (who had replaced Gallant), and IDF chief of staff [[Eyal Zamir]].<ref>{{cite news |url=https://edition.cnn.com/2025/11/07/middleeast/turkey-issues-genocide-arrest-warrant-against-netanyahu-intl-latam |title=Turkey issues 'genocide' arrest warrants against Netanyahu and other Israeli officials |newspaper=CNN |date=7 November 2025 |first1=Hira |last1=Humayun |first2=Betül |last2=Tuncer |first3=Tamar |last3=Michaelis}}</ref>

== Responsibility of third states and other entities ==
{{See also|Complicity in genocide|Responsibility to protect}}

All UN states that are signatories to the Genocide Convention are obliged "to employ all means reasonably available to them, so as to prevent genocide so far as possible" and must not provide "means to enable or facilitate the commission of the crime".<ref>{{cite web |last=Bastaki |first=Jinan |date=5 February 2024 |url=http://opiniojuris.org/2024/02/05/the-icjs-provisional-orders-measures-and-the-responsibility-of-third-states/ |title=The ICJ's Provisional Orders Measures and the Responsibility of Third States |website=Opinio Juris |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20241123080634/https://opiniojuris.org/2024/02/05/the-icjs-provisional-orders-measures-and-the-responsibility-of-third-states/ |archive-date=23 November 2024}}</ref> Multiple scholars argue that the inaction of the international community to confirmed atrocities in Gaza expose the irrelevance and weakness of the [[Responsibility to protect|Responsibility to Protect (R2P) doctrine]].<ref>{{harvnb|Moses|2024|pp=211–215}}: "The absence of a clear, sustained, and powerful invocation of the Responsibility to Protect (R2P) in response to Israel's vicious assault on Gaza reveals the fundamental weaknesses of the doctrine{{nbsp}}... We are now over three months into a military assault that many experts have labelled as a genocide (Government of South Africa Citation 2023) and the R2P has played no significant role in debates over how to respond."</ref>{{sfn|Sirleaf|2024|p=182}}{{sfn|Verdeja|2025|p=16–18}} Many Western countries, especially the United States, Germany, and the United Kingdom, have supported Israel by offering diplomatic, military, and intelligence support.{{sfn|Shaw|2025a|pp=416–422}} 

Multiple sources — including journalists, scholars, and the [[Independent International Commission of Inquiry on the Occupied Palestinian Territory|UN officials]]<ref>{{cite news |last1=Chang |first1=Alisa |last2=Mehta |first2=Jonaki |last3=Jarenwattananon |first3=Patrick |date=16 September 2025 |title=Israel is committing genocide in Gaza, a UN inquiry finds |url=https://www.npr.org/2025/09/16/nx-s1-5543246/israel-genocide-gaza-united-nations |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250917234926/https://www.npr.org/2025/09/16/nx-s1-5543246/israel-genocide-gaza-united-nations |archive-date=17 September 2025 |access-date=19 September 2025 |work=[[NPR]]}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last=Walker |first=Michael |date=5 February 2024 |title=Former UNWRA Spokesperson Says UK & US Complicit in Gaza Genocide |url=https://novaramedia.com/2024/02/05/former-unwra-spokesperson-says-uk-us-complicit-in-gaza-genocide/ |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240206184734/https://novaramedia.com/2024/02/05/former-unwra-spokesperson-says-uk-us-complicit-in-gaza-genocide/ |archive-date=6 February 2024 |work=[[Novara Media]]}}</ref> — state that the actions of Western countries make them complicit in genocide.<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
| {{harvnb|Beaklini|2023}}
| {{harvnb|Porras|2023}}
| {{harvnb|Scahill|Grim|2024}}
| {{harvnb|Levitz|2023}}
| {{harvnb|Ayyash|2023}}
}}</ref><ref name="Lakhani & Niranjan 2024">{{cite news |last1=Lakhani |first1=Nina |last2=Niranjan |first2=Ajit |date=20 August 2024 |title=Countries fueling Israel's Gaza war may be complicit in war crimes, experts warn |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/article/2024/aug/20/israel-war-gaza-fuel-war-crimes-warning |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240824052111/https://www.theguardian.com/world/article/2024/aug/20/israel-war-gaza-fuel-war-crimes-warning |archive-date=24 August 2024 |work=[[The Guardian]]}}</ref> Abdelwahab El-Affendi, academic in politics, describes the situation as hypocritical: "yesterday’s proponents of the 'responsibility to protect' doctrine are today’s biggest supporters of Israel’s genocidal assault on Gaza."<ref>{{Cite journal |last=Teitt |first=Sarah |date=2025-06-05 |title=Israel, Gaza, and the Unrealised Promise of the Responsibility to Protect |url=https://brill.com/view/journals/gr2p/aop/article-10.1163-1875984X-20250014/article-10.1163-1875984X-20250014.xml |journal=Global Responsibility to Protect |pages=1–7 |doi=10.1163/1875984X-20250014 |issn=1875-9858}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |last=El-Affendi |first=Abdelwahab |date=2023-10-31 |title=Where is the 'responsibility to protect' in Gaza? |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/opinions/2023/10/31/where-is-the-responsibility-to-protect-in-gaza |access-date=2026-01-20 |website=Al Jazeera |language=en}}</ref>

The [[Independent International Commission of Inquiry on the Occupied Palestinian Territory|Independent International Commission of Inquiry on Palestine]] said, "States may be complicit in failing to prevent genocide if they do not act in compliance" with the [[South Africa's genocide case against Israel|International Court of Justice's]] orders or if they directly aid or assist in "the commission of genocide".<ref>{{cite magazine |last1=Larson |first1=Nina |date=18 October 2024 |title=States Helping Israel's Occupation May Be 'Complicit': UN Experts |url=https://www.barrons.com/news/states-helping-israel-s-occupation-may-be-complicit-un-experts-570f4bfd |magazine=[[Barron's]] |access-date=21 October 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20241108155907/https://www.barrons.com/news/states-helping-israel-s-occupation-may-be-complicit-un-experts-570f4bfd |archive-date=8 November 2024}}</ref>  A [[Special Committee to Investigate Israeli Practices Affecting the Human Rights of the Palestinian People|UN Special Committee]] wrote, "Failing to act now{{nbsp}}... will tear apart the very foundation of the international rule of law we have collectively built to protect peace, security, and the well-being of all. Our inaction today is setting a perilous precedent for tomorrow."<ref name="UNCommitteeHeadGenocide" />

=== United States ===
{{see also|United States support for Israel in the Gaza war|3=Defense for Children International – Palestine v. Biden}}
[[File:U_S_Air_Force_Airmen_supply_Israel_with_missile_defense_(8086168).jpg|thumb|[[USAF]] airmen prepare for departure in a [[C-17 Globemaster III]] to [[United States support for Israel in the Gaza war|supply Israel]] with munitions, Oct. 15, 2023, at [[Ramstein Air Base]], Germany.]]
The United States has been a key provider of diplomatic and material support before and during the Gaza war.<ref>{{harvnb|Joyce|Martel|Pahuja|2025|p=1}}: "The US has bombed Iranian nuclear sites and continues to support the Israeli genocide in Gaza by supplying of weapons and providing diplomatic cover (as does the UK and Germany)"</ref>{{sfn|Wezeman|Djokic|George|Hussain|2024|pp=11–12}} It pays for around 15% of Israel's military budget and is its largest supplier of arms; it provided more than {{ntsp|22760000000||$}} to the war effort in its first year.{{sfn|Bachman|Ruiz|2025|p=5}} According to the [[Quincy Institute]], the destruction of Gaza is "in large part, the result of unconditional U.S. assistance and diplomatic cover".<ref>{{cite news |title=Mind the Gap: U.S. Preferences and Israel's War Conduct |url=https://quincyinst.org/research/mind-the-gap-u-s-preferences-and-israels-war-conduct/#h-introduction |access-date=28 September 2025 |work=[[Quincy Institute for Responsible Statecraft]] |date=22 November 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250811144111/https://quincyinst.org/research/mind-the-gap-u-s-preferences-and-israels-war-conduct/#h-introduction |archive-date=11 August 2025}}</ref>

Both the Biden and Trump administrations have denied genocide in Gaza;<ref name=newlines>{{cite magazine |last1=Zunes |first1=Stephen |title=By Rejecting Evidence of Genocide in Gaza, the US Is Following a Familiar Pattern |url=https://newlinesmag.com/essays/by-rejecting-evidence-of-genocide-in-gaza-the-us-is-following-a-familiar-pattern/ |access-date=28 September 2025 |magazine=[[New Lines Magazine]] |date=14 February 2025 |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250902182329/https://newlinesmag.com/essays/by-rejecting-evidence-of-genocide-in-gaza-the-us-is-following-a-familiar-pattern/ |archive-date=2 September 2025}}</ref> Biden's support of Israel earned him the nickname "Genocide Joe".<ref>{{cite news |last=Baker |first=Peter |title=A Bystander to '60s Protests, Biden Now Becomes a Target |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2024/04/30/us/politics/biden-columbia-protests-israel-antisemitism.html |access-date=19 October 2025 |work=[[The New York Times]] |date=30 April 2024 |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250930181505/https://www.nytimes.com/2024/04/30/us/politics/biden-columbia-protests-israel-antisemitism.html |archive-date=30 September 2025}}</ref> In February 2025, Trump [[Donald Trump's February 2025 Gaza Strip proposal|proposed an American takeover of Gaza]] and displacing the people living there, though he no longer supports this.<ref name=newlines/> According to an August opinion poll, half of US voters believe Israel is committing genocide in Gaza and 60% oppose further military assistance.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Power |first1=John |title=Half of US voters believe Israel committing genocide in Gaza, poll says |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/8/28/half-of-us-voters-believe-israel-committing-genocide-in-gaza-poll-says |access-date=28 September 2025 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |date=28 August 2025 |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251007192844/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/8/28/half-of-us-voters-believe-israel-committing-genocide-in-gaza-poll-says |archive-date=7 October 2025}}</ref> Six members of the [[United States Congress|US Congress]] have recognised the genocide: [[Alexandria Ocasio-Cortez]], [[Rashida Tlaib]], [[Summer Lee]], [[Marjorie Taylor Greene]], [[Becca Balint]] and [[Bernie Sanders]].<ref name="Sanders092025">{{cite news |title=Bernie Sanders becomes first US senator to say Israel committing genocide in Gaza |url=https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/2025/sep/17/bernie-sanders-israel-gaza-genocide |work=[[The Guardian]] |date=17 September 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251008103612/https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/2025/sep/17/bernie-sanders-israel-gaza-genocide |archive-date=8 October 2025}}</ref>

=== United Kingdom ===
{{See also|United Kingdom and the Gaza war|Israel–United Kingdom relations}}
[[File:Reminding Keir Starmer that he's could be complicit in genocide (53334628181).jpg|thumb|Protester holding a sign claiming the [[Labour Party (UK)|UK Labour Party]] leader [[Keir Starmer]] (image blurred due to copyright) supports genocide]]
The British government does not give weapons to Israel directly but rather [[UK arms export|issues licences for British companies to sell them]].<ref>{{cite news |last1=Holden |first1=Michael |last2=James |first2=William |date=3 September 2024 |title=UK suspends 30 of its 350 arms export licences to Israel |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/uk/uk-says-it-is-suspending-30-its-350-arms-export-licences-israel-2024-09-02/ |work=[[Reuters]] |archive-url=https://archive.today/20240904173718/https://www.reuters.com/world/uk/uk-says-it-is-suspending-30-its-350-arms-export-licences-israel-2024-09-02/ |archive-date=4 September 2024}}</ref> On 12 December 2023 [[Human Rights Watch]] said that selling weapons to Israel could make the UK complicit in war crimes. UK law says licences cannot be granted when there is a clear risk the items might be used to commit or facilitate a serious violation of international humanitarian law.<ref>{{cite web |last=Ahmed |first=Yasmine |date=12 December 2023 |title=Selling Weapons to Israel Could Make UK Complicit in War Crimes |url=https://www.hrw.org/news/2023/12/12/selling-weapons-israel-could-make-uk-complicit-war-crimes |publisher=[[Human Rights Watch]] |access-date=11 April 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231218005339/https://www.hrw.org/news/2023/12/12/selling-weapons-israel-could-make-uk-complicit-war-crimes |archive-date=18 December 2023}}</ref> [[James Denselow]] of [[Save the Children UK]] said, "By failing to push for a permanent end to the fighting or speak out against the weaponisation of aid, [[Rishi Sunak]] and [[Sunak ministry|his government]] are complicit in the horror that is unfolding."<ref>{{cite web |date=8 December 2023 |title=STATEMENT: 'We are failing the Children of Gaza' |url=https://www.savethechildren.org.uk/news/media-centre/press-releases/conditions-to-provide-humanitarian-assistance-to-children-in-gaz |website=[[Save the Children]] |access-date=11 April 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231215080729/https://www.savethechildren.org.uk/news/media-centre/press-releases/conditions-to-provide-humanitarian-assistance-to-children-in-gaz |archive-date=15 December 2023}}</ref> In December 2023, Scottish First Minister [[Humza Yousaf]] condemned the UK's abstention from a draft UN resolution calling for a ceasefire in Gaza, saying this would lead to the deaths of more children.<ref>{{cite news |date=10 December 2023 |title=Humza Yousaf says UK 'complicit' in killing Gaza children |url=https://www.newarab.com/news/humza-yousaf-says-uk-complicit-killing-gaza-children |work=[[The New Arab]] |access-date=11 April 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231215080728/https://www.newarab.com/news/humza-yousaf-says-uk-complicit-killing-gaza-children |archive-date=15 December 2023}}</ref>

In April 2024, [[Guy Goodwin-Gill]], a professor of international law at Oxford University, said: "There is a serious risk of genocide, as the International Court of Justice has found. If the UK, with that knowledge in mind, carries on exporting arms to Israel, there is a risk that those arms will be used in the conduct of aggressive activities and in the conduct of genocide."<ref>{{cite news |last1=Adler |first1=Nils |last2=Najjar |first2=Farah |date=4 April 2024 |title='The risk must be taken into account now' |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/4/4/israels-war-on-gaza-live-israel-accused-of-ai-assisted-genocide-in-gaza?update=2817755 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=16 April 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240416141416/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/4/4/israels-war-on-gaza-live-israel-accused-of-ai-assisted-genocide-in-gaza?update=2817755 |archive-date=16 April 2024}}</ref> The same month, hundreds of lawyers and legal academics published a legal opinion warning that the government risked complicity in genocide by continuing to arm Israel.{{sfn|Lawless|2024}}<ref>{{cite news |last=Brown |first=Faye |date=4 April 2024 |url=https://news.sky.com/story/uk-is-breaching-international-law-by-continuing-to-arm-israel-sunak-warned-13107474 |title=UK is breaching international law by continuing to arm Israel, Sunak warned |newspaper=[[Sky News]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240416214420/https://news.sky.com/story/amp/uk-is-breaching-international-law-by-continuing-to-arm-israel-sunak-warned-13107474 |archive-date=16 April 2024}}</ref>

On 2{{nbsp}}September 2024, Foreign Secretary [[David Lammy]] announced he was suspending approximately 30 arms export licences to Israel after a government review concluded there was a high risk these exports were being used for severe violations of international humanitarian law.<ref>{{cite news |last=Cecil |first=Nicholas |date=2 September 2024 |url=https://www.standard.co.uk/news/politics/uk-arms-exports-israel-gaza-hamas-david-lammy-b1179628.html |newspaper=[[Evening Standard]] |title=UK suspends 30 arms export licences to Israel over Gaza war including for fighter aircraft and drone spares |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240909043215/https://www.standard.co.uk/news/politics/uk-arms-exports-israel-gaza-hamas-david-lammy-b1179628.html |archive-date=9 September 2024}}</ref> At the time of the suspension, Israel had around 350 arms export licences in the UK.<ref>{{cite news |last=Fisher |first=Lucy |date=2 September 2024 |url=https://www.ft.com/content/bac169fb-4d28-4729-85e8-a13a197b0368 |title=UK to halt exports of some arms to Israel citing possible law breaches |newspaper=[[Financial Times]] |archive-url=https://archive.today/20240903075212/https://www.ft.com/content/bac169fb-4d28-4729-85e8-a13a197b0368 |archive-date=3 September 2024}}</ref>

On 3{{nbsp}}September 2025, the [[Scottish Government]] announced a ban on funding to "arms companies whose products or services are provided to countries where there is plausible evidence of genocide being committed", including Israel.<ref>{{cite news |last=Pollock |first=Laura |date=3 September 2025 |title=Scottish Government announces range of measures against Israel |url=https://www.thenational.scot/news/25438714.scottish-government-announces-range-measures-israel/ |access-date=5 September 2025 |work=[[The National (Scotland)|The National]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251204102140/https://www.thenational.scot/news/25438714.scottish-government-announces-range-measures-israel/ |archive-date=4 December 2025}}</ref> The [[Scottish Parliament]] also voted for a boycott of Israel and any companies providing it military support.<ref>{{cite news |last=Brawn |first=Steph |date=3 September 2025 |title=Scottish Parliament votes for immediate boycott of Israel |url=https://www.thenational.scot/news/25439517.msps-vote-full-boycott-israel/ |access-date=5 September 2025 |work=[[The National (Scotland)|The National]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20260103122232/https://www.thenational.scot/news/25439517.msps-vote-full-boycott-israel/ |archive-date=3 January 2026}}</ref>

==== Lawsuit over export licences ====
The human rights groups [[Al-Haq]] and Global Legal Action Network took legal action against the British government in December 2023, saying that the government risked violating the Genocide Convention by granting export licences for the sale of military equipment to Israel.<ref>{{cite news |last=Abdul |first=Geneva |date=6 December 2023 |title=UK government faces legal challenge over arms exports to Israel |work=[[The Guardian]] |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2023/dec/06/uk-government-faces-legal-challenge-over-arms-exports-to-israel |access-date=11 April 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231213060015/https://www.theguardian.com/world/2023/dec/06/uk-government-faces-legal-challenge-over-arms-exports-to-israel |archive-date=13 December 2023}}</ref>

In May 2025, a hearing began at the [[High Court of Justice]] to determine whether the UK had violated arms export control laws by continuing to supply Israel with components for [[F-35]] fighter jets even after other licences were suspended. At the hearing, government lawyers argued that UK-made parts enter a global spares pool rather than being shipped directly to Israel, where it is "generally not possible to determine who the end user would be" and that suspending them "would have a critical impact on international peace and security, including NATO's defence and deterrence".<ref>{{cite news |last=Wintour |first=Patrick |author-link=Patrick Wintour |date=12 May 2025 |title=UK's F-35 exports more important than stopping genocide, lawyers to argue |url=https://www.theguardian.com/uk-news/2025/may/12/uks-f-35-exports-more-important-than-stopping-genocide-lawyers-to-argue |newspaper=[[The Guardian]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250517022020/https://www.theguardian.com/uk-news/2025/may/12/uks-f-35-exports-more-important-than-stopping-genocide-lawyers-to-argue |archive-date=17 May 2025}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |date=12 May 2025 |title=UK to argue F-35 exports outweighs Gaza genocide risk in landmark case |url=https://www.newarab.com/news/uk-will-argue-f-35-exports-outweighs-gaza-genocide-risk |newspaper=[[The New Arab]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250513144120/https://www.newarab.com/news/uk-will-argue-f-35-export-outweighs-gaza-genocide-risk |archive-date=13 May 2025}}</ref>

On 30 June 2025, the court dismissed the claim, holding the "F-35 carve out" lawful; it added that some aspects of the challenge were "not for a domestic court to decide" and that the carve-out's "true nature" was that the UK would "not cease to participate in the F-35 Programme", even though some UK components would ultimately reach Israel.<ref>{{Cite web |date=30 June 2025 |title=Al-Haq -v- Secretary of State for Business and Trade |url=https://www.judiciary.uk/judgments/al-haq-v-secretary-of-state-for-business-and-trade-2/ |access-date=8 November 2025 |website=Courts and Tribunals Judiciary |language=en-UK |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251114101626/https://www.judiciary.uk/judgments/al-haq-v-secretary-of-state-for-business-and-trade-2/ |archive-date=14 November 2025}}</ref>

=== Germany ===
{{see also|German support for Israel in the Gaza war}}
In October 2023, political analyst Lena Obermaier argued that Germany is complicit in Israel's war crimes against Gaza.<ref name="Obermaier 2023">{{cite magazine |last=Obermaier |first=Lena |date=23 October 2023 |title=Germany Is Complicit in Israel's War Crimes in Gaza |url=https://jacobin.com/2023/10/germany-israel-war-crimes-gaza-palestine-international-law |magazine=[[Jacobin (magazine)|Jacobin]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240301181227/https://jacobin.com/2023/10/germany-israel-war-crimes-gaza-palestine-international-law |archive-date=1 March 2024}}</ref> She detailed how most of Germany's most prominent news outlets have "been silent on Israeli genocidal policies". She also highlighted police suppression of pro-Palestine protests<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
| {{cite news |date=16 October 2023 |title=Berlin police break up banned pro-Palestinian rally |url=https://www.dw.com/en/berlin-police-break-up-banned-pro-palestinian-rally/a-67104373 |work=[[Deutsche Welle]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240221073758/https://www.dw.com/en/berlin-police-break-up-banned-pro-palestinian-rally/a-67104373 |archive-date=21 February 2024}}
| {{harvnb|Jamal|2023}}
| {{harvnb|Sharma|2023}}
| {{harvnb|Marsh|2023}}
| {{harvnb|Schaer|2023}}
| {{harvnb|Boffey|2023}}
| {{cite news |date=30 December 2023 |title=Police in Berlin ban pro-Palestinian New Year rally |url=https://www.dw.com/en/police-in-berlin-ban-pro-palestinian-new-year-rally/a-67858991 |work=[[Deutsche Welle]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240222200733/https://www.dw.com/en/police-in-berlin-ban-pro-palestinian-new-year-rally/a-67858991 |archive-date=22 February 2024}}
}}</ref> as evidence of state complicity.<ref name="Obermaier 2023"/> According to [[Anti-antisemitism in Germany#Creation of antisemitism commissioners|Germany's Federal Commissioner for the Fight against Antisemitism]], accusing Israel of genocide is antisemitic.<ref>{{cite magazine |last=Kuras |first=Peter |date=18 July 2023 |title=The Strange Logic of Germany's Antisemitism Bureaucrats |url=https://jewishcurrents.org/the-strange-logic-of-germanys-antisemitism-bureaucrats |access-date=28 November 2024 |magazine=[[Jewish Currents]] |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20241217184503/https://jewishcurrents.org/the-strange-logic-of-germanys-antisemitism-bureaucrats |archive-date=17 December 2024}}</ref> Publicly accusing Israel of genocide can lead to arrest in Germany, even when the accusers are Jewish or Israeli.<ref>{{cite magazine |last=Varoufakis |first=Yanis |author-link=Yanis Varoufakis |date=17 April 2024 |title=Why I was banned from Germany |url=https://www.newstatesman.com/diary/2024/04/cancelled-germany-yanis-varoufakis-israel-palestine |access-date=28 November 2024 |magazine=[[New Statesman]] |language=en-US |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20241219043511/https://www.newstatesman.com/diary/2024/04/cancelled-germany-yanis-varoufakis-israel-palestine |archive-date=19 December 2024}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |date=14 October 2024 |title=Gaza und das Grundgesetz |trans-title=Gaza and the Basic Law |url=https://www.fr.de/kultur/gesellschaft/gaza-und-das-grundgesetz-93373670.html |access-date=28 November 2024 |work=[[Frankfurter Rundschau]] |language=de |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20241203090254/https://www.fr.de/kultur/gesellschaft/gaza-und-das-grundgesetz-93373670.html |archive-date=3 December 2024}}</ref> In February 2024 a criminal complaint was filed in German courts accusing various senior politicians of complicity in genocide.<ref name="Schaer 2024"/> In March, [[Nicaragua v. Germany|Nicaragua sued Germany for complicity at the ICJ]].<ref name="mee-2024-1-1"/>

=== European Union ===
{{see also|Israel–European Union relations#Gaza war}}
The European Union was accused of potential complicity after it did not suspend the [[European Union Association Agreement|EU-Israel Association Agreement]]. Secretary General of Amnesty International [[Agnès Callamard]] said the EU was giving Israel a "green light" to continue its genocide and was at "risk of complicity in Israel's actions".<ref>{{cite |url=https://www.nrc.nl/nieuws/2025/07/15/morele-faillissement-van-onze-buitenlandpolitiek-organisaties-woedend-over-uitblijven-eu-sancties-tegen-israel-a4900375 |archive-date=16 July 2025 |work=[[NRC (newspaper)|NRC]] |language=nl}}</ref>  In March 2024, [[Oxfam]] released a statement detailing its intention, alongside several other non-governmental |archive-date=12 March 2024 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]]}}</ref>

=== Egypt ===
{{see also|Egypt and the Gaza war|Egypt–Israel relations}}
Egypt has been accused of complicity in genocide for its enforcement of the blockade on Gaza and refusal to open the [[Rafah Border Crossing]].<ref name="Mahmoud 2024">{{cite magazine |last=Mahmoud |first=Omar |date=20 June 2024 |title=Why Egypt Is Complicit in the Genocide in Gaza |url=https://jacobin.com/2024/06/egypt-palestine-gaza-genocide-al-sisi |access-date=21 June 2025 |magazine=[[Jacobin (magazine)|Jacobin]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250619122052/https://jacobin.com/2024/06/egypt-palestine-gaza-genocide-al-sisi |archive-date=19 June 2025}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last=Sabry |first=Mohannad |date=26 January 2024 |title=After ICJ rule, will Egypt end its complicity with Israel starving Gaza? |url=https://www.middleeasteye.net/opinion/icj-rule-egypt-end-complicity-israel-starving-gaza-will |access-date=21 June 2025 |work=[[Middle East Eye]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250621085824/https://www.middleeasteye.net/opinion/icj-rule-egypt-end-complicity-israel-starving-gaza-will |archive-date=21 June 2025}}</ref> In April 2025, [[Cage (organisation)|Cage]] and five other African advocacy organisations filed a complaint with the [[African Commission on Human and Peoples' Rights]].{{sfn|Cage|2025}} Egypt is not permitted to turn people away at its borders if doing so would expose them to life-threatening conditions or collective punishment, as this would violate its obligations under the [[International Covenant on Civil and Political Rights]] and the [[Convention Against Torture]].<ref>{{cite journal |last=Hathaway |first=James C. |date=25 October 2023 |title=Trapped in Gaza |url=https://verfassungsblog.de/trapped-in-gaza/ |journal=[[Verfassungsblog]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250704134620/https://verfassungsblog.de/trapped-in-gaza/ |archive-date=4 July 2025}}</ref><ref>{{cite magazine |last=Edwards |first=Alice Jill |date=30 April 2024 |title=Egypt Is Obliged to Let Gaza Refugees In |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250621212522/https://foreignpolicy.com/2024/04/30/gaza-refugees-egypt-border-palestine/ |archive-date=21 June 2025}}</ref> Egypt was also accused of complicity with Israel for its crackdown on the [[Global March to Gaza]].<ref>{{cite news |date=12 June 2025 |title=Egypt slammed for its treatment of foreign nationals doing Global March for Gaza |url=https://www.middleeasteye.net/trending/egypt-slammed-treatment-foreign-nationals-joining-global-march-gaza |access-date=23 June 2025 |work=[[Middle East Eye]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250621011406/https://www.middleeasteye.net/trending/egypt-slammed-treatment-foreign-nationals-joining-global-march-gaza |archive-date=21 June 2025}}</ref>

Egypt has said that its closure of the Rafah crossing is done in opposition to Israeli plans to displace Palestinians.<ref name="Mahmoud 2024"/> Egypt rejected an Israeli proposal for Gaza to be [[Occupation of the Gaza Strip by the United Arab Republic|returned to Egypt]] for up to 15 years<ref>{{cite web |last1=El-Menawy |first1=Abdellatif |title=Why Egypt Refuses To Administer Gaza – OpEd |url=https://www.eurasiareview.com/17032025-why-egypt-refuses-to-administer-gaza-oped/ |website=Eurasia Review |date=17 March 2025 |access-date=19 March 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250515171810/https://www.eurasiareview.com/17032025-why-egypt-refuses-to-administer-gaza-oped/ |archive-date=15 May 2025 |url-status=live}}</ref> and formally supported South Africa's genocide case against Israel.<ref>{{Cite news|date=12 May 2024 |title=Egypt to support South Africa's genocide case against Israel at ICJ |url=https://www.france24.com/en/middle-east/20240512-🔴-live-israel-steps-up-strikes-in-gaza-after-issuing-new-rafah-evacuation-order |work=[[France 24]] |access-date=27 January 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250127151805/https://www.france24.com/en/middle-east/20240512-%F0%9F%94%B4-live-israel-steps-up-strikes-in-gaza-after-issuing-new-rafah-evacuation-order |archive-date=27 January 2025}}</ref>

=== Italy ===
{{see also|Israel–Italy relations}}

On 7 October 2025, Prime Minister [[Giorgia Meloni]] said in an interview with ''[[RAI|RAI – Radiotelevisione italiana]]'' that a pro-Palestinian advocacy group had reported her, Defence Minister [[Guido Crosetto]], Foreign Minister [[Antonio Tajani]], and [[Leonardo (company)|Leonardo]] director [[Roberto Cingolani]] to the International Criminal Court for alleged complicity in the genocide.<ref>{{cite news |last=Amante |first=Angelo |date=8 October 2025 |title= Italy's Meloni says she has been denounced to ICC for complicity in genocide |url=https://www.reuters.com/business/aerospace-defense/italy-pm-meloni-says-been-denounced-icc-complicity-genocide-2025-10-07/ |access-date=8 October 2025 |work=[[Reuters]] |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251008014513/https://www.reuters.com/business/aerospace-defense/italy-pm-meloni-says-been-denounced-icc-complicity-genocide-2025-10-07/ |archive-date=8 October 2025}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title=Meloni says accused of 'complicity in genocide' at world court |url=https://today.lorientlejour.com/article/1480226/meloni-says-accused-of-complicity-in-genocide-at-world-court.html |work=[[L'Orient–Le Jour|L'Orient Today]] |date=8 October 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251008130430/https://today.lorientlejour.com/article/1480226/meloni-says-accused-of-complicity-in-genocide-at-world-court.html |archive-date=8 October 2025 |access-date=8 October 2025}}</ref> The complaint, which was signed by 50 people, including law professors, lawyers, and several public figures, was filed on 1 October. It accused Meloni's government of complicity for supplying arms to Israel and urged the ICC to evaluate whether a formal investigation into the allegation could be initiated.<ref>{{cite news |date=8 October 2025 |title= Giorgia Meloni says she has been accused of complicity in Gaza genocide at ICC court |url=https://www.newarab.com/news/meloni-says-accused-complicity-gaza-genocide-icc-court|access-date=8 October 2025 |work=[[The New Arab]] |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251008015303/https://www.newarab.com/news/meloni-accused-complicity-gaza-genocide-icc-court |archive-date=8 October 2025}}</ref> As of May 2025, Italy was the third-largest supplier of weaponry to Israel, representing around 1% of Israel's weaponry imports.<ref>{{Cite web |date=26 May 2025 |title=Italy's Quiet Role in Arming Israel Amid Conflict |url=https://unipd-centrodirittiumani.it/en/news/italys-quiet-role-in-arming-israel-amid-conflict |access-date=15 October 2025 |website=Centro di Ateneo per i Diritti Umani |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251008173836/https://unipd-centrodirittiumani.it/en/news/italys-quiet-role-in-arming-israel-amid-conflict |archive-date=8 October 2025}}</ref>{{sfn|Wezeman|Djokic|George|Hussain|2024}} Despite the Italian government's claims that weaponry supplement to Israel had been interrupted, [[Leonardo (company)|Leonardo]], one of Italy's biggest arms companies, confirmed that the Italian government and Italian companies still export arms to Israel.<ref>{{Cite news |last=Facchini |first=Duccio |date=1 October 2025 |title=Leonardo ammette l'export di armi in Israele e fa cadere la maschera del governo |url=https://altreconomia.it/leonardo-ammette-lexport-di-armi-in-israele-e-fa-cadere-la-maschera-del-governo/ |access-date=5 November 2025 |work={{ill|Altreconomia|it}} |language=it}}</ref> Francesca Albanese directly called Italy an accomplice in the Gaza genocide.<ref>{{Cite news |last=Pivitera |first=Greta |date=31 October 2025 |title=Francesca Albanese, nuova bufera. In un report accusa l'Italia all'Onu: «Complice di genocidio» |trans-title=Francesca Albanese, new controversy. In a report, she accuses Italy to the UN: "Complicit in genocide." |url=https://www.corriere.it/esteri/25_ottobre_30/francesca-albanese-genocidio-bufera-4948dc1d-2d3f-4ccd-a5e2-7e74be19dxlk.shtml |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251117003831/https://www.corriere.it/esteri/25_ottobre_30/francesca-albanese-genocidio-bufera-4948dc1d-2d3f-4ccd-a5e2-7e74be19dxlk.shtml |access-date=5 November 2025 |archive-date=17 November 2025 |work=[[Corriere della Sera]] |language=it}}</ref>

=== Private sector and media ===
{{See also|List of companies involved in the Gaza war}}
Multiple corporations have been accused of profiting from the Gaza genocide.<ref>{{cite magazine |last=Ackerman |first=Spencer |author-link=Spencer Ackerman |date=9 July 2024 |title=These Corporations Are the True "Winners" of the War on Gaza |magazine=[[The Nation]] |url=https://www.thenation.com/article/economy/gaza-war-profiteers-corporations/ |access-date=16 May 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250422070627/https://www.thenation.com/article/economy/gaza-war-profiteers-corporations/ |archive-date=22 April 2025}}</ref>{{sfn|Albanese|2025|pp=1–2}} Executives from [[Lockheed Martin]], [[General Dynamics]], and [[RTX Corporation]] have described the war in Gaza as a source of increased profits.<ref>{{cite news |last=Goodkind |first=Nicole |date=18 October 2023 |title=What the Israel-Hamas war means for defense stocks |url=https://www.cnn.com/2023/10/18/investing/premarket-stocks-trading/index.html |access-date=14 May 2025 |work=[[CNN]] |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250319234048/https://www.cnn.com/2023/10/18/investing/premarket-stocks-trading/index.html |archive-date=19 March 2025}}</ref><ref>{{cite magazine |last=French |first=Nick |title=The Obscene US Profiteering From Israeli War and Occupation |url=https://jacobin.com/2024/03/gaza-profits-bds-weapons-corporations/ |magazine=[[Jacobin (magazine)|Jacobin]] |access-date=18 May 2025 |date=16 March 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250723130413/https://jacobin.com/2024/03/gaza-profits-bds-weapons-corporations |archive-date=23 July 2025}}</ref>

On 20{{nbsp}}June 2024, UN experts warned that continued arms transfers to Israel could amount to violations of international law and risk state and corporate complicity in potential genocide. They called for an immediate halt to all weapons transfers to Israel, including by such major arms manufacturers as [[BAE Systems]], [[Boeing]], Lockheed Martin, and [[Caterpillar Inc.|Caterpillar]]. They also warned institutions investing in these companies, such as [[Bank of America]], [[BlackRock]], [[Citigroup]], and [[Wells Fargo]].{{sfn|OHCHR|2024c}}

In June 2025, a UN expert's report named [[Alphabet (company)|Alphabet]], [[Amazon (company)|Amazon]], [[Microsoft]], and [[IBM]] as "central to Israel's surveillance apparatus and the ongoing Gaza destruction", and [[Palantir Technologies|Palantir]] as a source of AI tools for the Israeli military.<ref name=UN-corporate-report>{{cite news |last1=Farge |first1=Emma |date=1 July 2025 |title='Lucrative' business deals help sustain Israel's Gaza campaign, UN expert says |url=https://www.reuters.com/business/aerospace-defense/lucrative-business-deals-help-sustain-israels-gaza-campaign-un-expert-says-2025-07-01/ |access-date=1 July 2025 |work=[[Reuters]] |language=en |archive-url=https://archive.today/20250701174630/https://www.reuters.com/business/aerospace-defense/lucrative-business-deals-help-sustain-israels-gaza-campaign-un-expert-says-2025-07-01/ |archive-date=1 July 2025}}</ref> The report also named [[Allianz]], [[Barclays]], BlackRock, and [[BNP Paribas]] for [[underwriting]] and purchasing Israeli government bonds, which the UN said are the main source of financing for Israel's military expenditures.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Yan |first1=Sophia |date=1 July 2025 |title=British companies named and shamed by UN for profiting from Israeli 'genocide' |url=https://www.telegraph.co.uk/world-news/2025/07/01/british-companies-profiting-israeli-genocide-un-gaza-shamed/ |access-date=1 July 2025 |work=[[The Daily Telegraph]] |archive-url=https://archive.today/20250701173739/https://www.telegraph.co.uk/world-news/2025/07/01/british-companies-profiting-israeli-genocide-un-gaza-shamed/ |archive-date=1 July 2025}}</ref> Scholars, journalists, media analysts and human rights advocates have accused various media outlets of [[Complicity in genocide|complicity]] through [[media imperialism]].<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
| {{harvnb|Moallem|2023|pp=542–543}}
| {{harvnb|Qutami|2023|p=532}}
| {{harvnb|Khouri|2023}}
| {{Cite news |date=29 June 2025 |title=Western media enabling Gaza genocide and rewriting history, say experts |url=https://www.middleeasteye.net/news/experts-say-western-media-enabling-gaza-genocide-and-rewriting-history |access-date=1 July 2025 |work=[[Middle East Eye]] |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250724122831/https://www.middleeasteye.net/news/experts-say-western-media-enabling-gaza-genocide-and-rewriting-history |archive-date=24 July 2025}}
}}</ref>

== Political discourse ==

2025}}</ref>

The [[Organisation of Islamic Cooperation]] (OIC), the [[Arab League]], and the [[African Union]] have collectively endorsed the characterisation of Israel's actions as genocide and called for accountability and measures such as ending arms transfers.<ref>{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
| {{cite news |date=5 May 2024 |title=Islamic Cooperation Denounces Gaza 'Genocide', Urges Sanctions Against Israel |url=https://www.barrons.com/news/islamic-cooperation-denounces-gaza-genocide-urges-sanctions-against-israel-c8c7ac87 |magazine=[[Barron's]] |agency=[[Agence France-Presse]] |access-date=10 May 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240510024352/https://www.barrons.com/news/islamic-cooperation-denounces-gaza-genocide-urges-sanctions-against-israel-c8c7ac87 |archive-date=10 May 2024}}
| {{cite news |title=Arab, Islamic countries condemn Netanyahu's 'Greater Israel' remark |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/8/16/arab-islamic-countries-condemn-netanyahus-greater-israel-remark |access-date=17 August 2025 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |date=16 August 2025 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250821081232/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/8/16/arab-islamic-countries-condemn-netanyahus-greater-israel-remark |archive-date=21 August 2025}}
| {{harvnb|Maina|2025}}
| {{Cite web |date=28 February 2024 |title=The African Union Delivered its Oral Statement Before the International Court of Justice for the Palestine Advisory Opinion Proceedings |url=https://au.int/en/pressreleases/20240228/african-union-delivered-its-oral-statement-international-court-justice |url-status=live |access-date=10 September 2025 |website=[[African Union]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251007135410/https://au.int/en/pressreleases/20240228/african-union-delivered-its-oral-statement-international-court-justice |archive-date=7 October 2025}}
}}</ref> In January 2025, the [[Hague Group]] convened in [[Bogotá]] with the aim to uphold international rulings on Gaza, end arms shipments to Israel and build a pathway to broader recognition of Palestinian statehood.<ref>{{Cite news |last=Wintour |first=Patrick |author-link=Patrick Wintour |date=31 January 2025 |title=South Africa and Malaysia to launch campaign to protect international justice |url=https://www.theguardian.com/law/2025/jan/31/south-africa-and-malaysia-to-launch-campaign-to-protect-justice |access-date=4 November 2025 |work=[[The Guardian]] |language=en-GB |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251114194030/https://www.theguardian.com/law/2025/jan/31/south-africa-and-malaysia-to-launch-campaign-to-protect-justice |archive-date=14 November 2025}}</ref>

=== Non-governmental organisations and intergovernmental organisations ===
{{main|List of humanitarian and human rights groups accusing Israel of genocide in Gaza}}

Numerous non-governmental organisations and intergovernmental organisations have accused Israel of genocide. Among the first to warn of a risk of genocide, in mid-October 2023, were [[Genocide Watch]] and the [[Lemkin Institute for Genocide Prevention]].<ref>{{cite web |date=13 October 2023 |title=Active Genocide Alert – Israel-Palestine: There is No Justification for Genocide |url=https://www.genocidewatch.com/single-post/genocide-emergency-alert-israel-and-gaza |url-status=live |publisher=[[Genocide |date=17 October 2023 |title=Genocide Emergency Alert: Israel and Gaza Genocide Prevention]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231227220339/https://www.lemkininstitute.com/active-genocide-alert-1/active-genocide-alert---israel-palestine%3A-there-is-no-justification-for-genocide |archive-date=27 December 2023}}</ref> Several Palestinian human rights groups, including [[Defence for Children International]] (DCI),<ref>{{Cite news |last1=Mohamed |first1=Edna |last2=Stepansky |first2=Joseph |last3=Najjar |first3=Farah |date=1 November 2023 |title=Rights group accuses US of complicity in children's deaths in Gaza |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231102022100/http://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2023/11/1/israel-hamas-war-live-anger-grows-over-israeli-attack-on-gaza-refugee-camp?update=2455675 |archive-date=2 November 2023}}</ref> [[Al-Haq]], [[Al Mezan Center for Human Rights|Al Mezan]], and the [[Palestinian Centre for Human Rights]], have filed lawsuits alleging a genocide.<ref name="sccoip">{{#invoke:list|bulleted|
| {{Cite news |date=21 October 2023 |title=Scholars, civil society call on ICC Prosecutor to issue arrest warrants, investigate Israeli crimes in Gaza |publisher=[[Wafa]] |url=https://english.wafa.ps/Pages/Details/138509 |access-date=24 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231026192122/https://english.wafa.ps/Pages/Details/138509 |archive-date=26 October 2023}}

}}</ref> Some Israeli human rights organisations, such as [[B'Tselem]]{{sfn|B'Tselem|2025|pp=4, 86}} and [[Physicians for Human Rights–Israel]], released reports calling Israel's campaign in Gaza a 2024}}</ref> {{lang|fr|[[Médecins Sans Frontières]]}} (MSF) has also found that Israel is committing genocide.<ref>{{harvnb|Médecins Sans Frontières|2024c|p=5}}: "Our firsthand observations of the displacement, and impossible conditions of life for Palestinians under siege and bombardment—are undeniable."</ref><ref>{{cite web |date=30 December 2024 January 2025}}</ref>{{sfn|Médecins Sans Frontières|2025}} The American activist group [[Jewish Voice for Peace]] has stated that Israel is committing genocide.<ref>{{cite web |date=11 October 2023 Times of Israel]] |language=en-US |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251114163212/https://jewishchronicle.timesofisrael.com/jewish-voice-for-peace-retools-to-focus-on-swaying-elections/ In September 2025, the [[UN Human Rights Council]]'s [[Independent International Commission of Inquiry on the Occupied Palestinian Territory|Independent International Commission of Inquiry]] issued a report concluding that Israel is committing genocide against Palestinians in Gaza. The Commission found reasonable grounds to determine that Israeli authorities and security forces have committed, and continue to commit, four of the five genocidal acts defined under the 1948 Genocide Convention: killing members of the group; causing serious bodily or mental harm; deliberately inflicting conditions of life calculated to bring about the group's physical destruction in whole or in part; and imposing measures intended to prevent births.<ref name="UNCommissionGenocide" /><ref>{{Cite news |last=Henley |first=Jon |date=16 September 2025 |title=Israel has committed genocide in Gaza, says UN commission of inquiry |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2025/sep/16/israel-committed-genocide-in-gaza-says-un-inquiry |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250922105448/https://www.theguardian.com/world/2025/sep/16/israel-committed-genocide-in-gaza-says-un-inquiry |archive-date=22 September 2025 |access-date=16 September 2025 |work=[[The Guardian]]}}</ref>

== Cultural discourse ==
{{Main|Cultural discourse about the Gaza genocide}}

Israel's genocide against the Palestinian people in Gaza has been a contentious topic in cultural discourse. Celebrities, athletes, public intellectuals, activists, cultural institutions and ordinary people have weighed in on the events in Gaza, as well as on the cultural and societal implications of viewing those events through the framework of genocide.<ref>{{cite news |last=Barat |first=Frank |title=Gaza's genocide has forced many celebrities out of silence |url=https://www.newarab.com/opinion/gazas-genocide-has-forced-many-celebrities-out-silence |url-status=live |work=[[The New Arab]] |date=14 July 2025 |access-date=11 August 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250811040850/https://www.newarab.com/opinion/gazas-genocide-has-forced-many-celebrities-out-silence |archive-date=11 August 2025}}</ref>

=== Public opinion in Israel and abroad ===
Multiple surveys have found broad support among Jewish Israelis for the government's policies toward Gaza.<ref name="HaaretzTransferPoll">{{Cite news |date=28 May 2025 |title=Yes to transfer: 82% of Jewish Israelis back expelling Gazans |url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2025-05-28/ty-article-magazine/.premium/yes-to-transfer-82-of-jewish-israelis-back-expelling-gazans/00000197-12a4-df22-a9d7-9ef6af930000 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251011183022/https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2025-05-28/ty-article-magazine/.premium/yes-to-transfer-82-of-jewish-israelis-back-expelling-gazans/00000197-12a4-df22-a9d7-9ef6af930000 |archive-date=11 October 2025 |access-date=8 November 2025 |work=[[Haaretz]] |language=en}}</ref><ref name="HaaretzFaminePoll">{{Cite news |last=Dayan |first=Linda |date=5 August 2025 |title=Large majority of Israeli Jews untroubled by reports of famine in Gaza, poll finds |url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2025-08-05/ty-article/.premium/large-majority-of-israeli-jews-untroubled-by-reports-of-famine-in-gaza-poll-finds/00000198-7ab3-d0ce-a5de-fbb374f30000 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250826060312/https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2025-08-05/ty-article/.premium/large-majority-of-israeli-jews-untroubled-by-reports-of-famine-in-gaza-poll-finds/00000198-7ab3-d0ce-a5de-fbb374f30000 |archive-date=26 August 2025 |access-date=8 November 2025 |work=[[Haaretz]] |language=en}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |date=26 January 2024 |title=Jewish, Arab Israelis disagree on IDF use of force in Gaza |url=https://www.jpost.com/israel-news/article-783849 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250722162135/https://www.jpost.com/israel-news/article-783849 |archive-date=22 July 2025 |access-date=8 November 2025 |work=[[The Jerusalem Post]] |language=en}}</ref> An August 2025 Accord Center poll found that 76% of Jewish Israelis agreed with the statement "there are no innocent people in Gaza".<ref>{{Cite web |date=25 August 2025 |title=Poll: 62% of Israelis say "there are no innocent people in Gaza" |url=https://www.i24news.tv/en/news/israel-at-war/artc-poll-62-of-israelis-say-there-are-no-innocent-people-in-gaza |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20251006150146/https://www.i24news.tv/en/news/israel-at-war/artc-poll-62-of-israelis-say-there-are-no-innocent-people-in-gaza |archive-date=6 October 2025 |access-date=8 November 2025 |website=i24NEWS |language=en}}</ref> A May 2025 survey found that 82% supported expelling Gazans, while 56% favoured also expelling Palestinians from Israel.<ref name="HaaretzTransferPoll" /> Another August 2025 poll found that 79% of Jewish Israelis were untroubled by reports of famine in Gaza.<ref name="HaaretzFaminePoll" /> According to the [[Lemkin Institute for Genocide Prevention]], "the vast majority of Israelis agree with...[Israel's] plan and clearly will support anything to see it realized – from [[Israeli apartheid|apartheid]] to extermination."<ref>{{Cite web |date=18 May 2025 |title=Four Facts about Israel's Genocide |url=https://www.lemkininstitute.com/statements-new-page/four-facts-about-israel%E2%80%99s-genocide |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250711072013/https://www.lemkininstitute.com/statements-new-page/four-facts-about-israel%E2%80%99s-genocide |archive-date=11 July 2025 |access-date=23 September 2025 |website=[[Lemkin Institute for Genocide Prevention]] |language=en}}</ref>

A September 2025 AP-NORC poll found that the number of Americans who believe that Israel's military actions in Gaza have "gone too far" was increasing.<ref>{{Cite web |date=2025-09-18 |title=More Americans feel Israel has 'gone too far' in Gaza, AP-NORC poll shows |url=https://www.pbs.org/newshour/politics/more-americans-feel-israel-has-gone-too-far-in-gaza-ap-norc-poll-shows |access-date=2025-11-22 |website=PBS News |language=en-us}}</ref>

==Impact==
[[File:Palestine Rally End The Siege, Stop the War on Gaza (53264903858).jpg|thumb|Millions of people around the world protested Israel's actions, many of them explicitly calling for the recognition and cessation of genocide.{{sfn|Shaw|2025b|p=10}}]]
British sociologist [[Martin Shaw (sociologist)|Martin Shaw]] has called the Gaza genocide "the genocide that changed the world" because of mass mobilisation against genocide. He also highlights some political victories by Israel, but "at huge cost to [[Legitimacy of Israel|its global legitimacy]] and that of the West".{{sfn|Shaw|2025b|p=|pp=4, 14}} Israeli journalist and author [[Gideon Levy]] wrote an article in ''Haaretz'' insisting that the people of Gaza will never forget the massacres, bombardments, destruction, and trauma.<ref>{{cite news |last=Levy |first=Gideon |date=5 October 2025 |title=Do Cry Over Spilt Blood: Generations Will Go by Before Gaza Forgets the Genocide |url=https://www.haaretz.com/opinion/2025-10-05/ty-article-opinion/.premium/do-cry-over-spilt-blood-generations-will-go-by-before-gaza-forgets-the-genocide/00000199-afd4-d5a6-afff-efdff5560000 |access-date=5 October 2025 |work=[[Haaretz]] |language=en |archive-url=https://archive.today/20251005003148/https://www.haaretz.com/opinion/2025-10-05/ty-article-opinion/.premium/do-cry-over-spilt-blood-generations-will-go-by-before-gaza-forgets-the-genocide/00000199-afd4-d5a6-afff-efdff5560000 |archive-date=5 October 2025}}</ref>

Some scholars, particularly those associated with [[Third World approaches to international law]], have argued that the international community's failure to treat Israel's actions in Gaza as a genocide and respond accordingly has harmed the principles of the [[international order]] and international law and exposed the deficiencies of international governance.<ref name="Baars 2024"/><ref name="Barreto 2024"/>{{sfn|Englert|Bhattacharyya|2024|p=}}{{page needed|date=September 2025}} José Manuel Barreto argues that "the Palestinian genocide has unveiled the deep colonial structure of the international legal order", placing the Gaza genocide in a long list of colonial genocides the international system has tolerated.<ref name="Barreto 2024"/> Historian [[Mark LeVine]] argues that Israel's actions have destroyed respect for international law and weakened the taboo against large-scale violence in response to perceived threats.{{sfn|LeVine|2025|p=5}} Dutch lawyer and professor of international law {{ill|André Nollkaemper|nl|André Nollkaemper}} has said that the United States' rejection of international law is a unique feature of the Gaza war.<ref>{{cite news |last=Walters |first=Derk |title=Is het internationaal recht nog relevant na 'Gaza'? 'We gaan een donker decennium tegemoet' |url=https://www.nrc.nl/nieuws/2025/10/06/is-het-internationaal-recht-nog-relevant-na-gaza-we-gaan-een-donker-decennium-tegemoet-a4908607 |work=[[NRC (newspaper)|NRC]] |date=6 October 2025 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20251006221648/https://www.nrc.nl/nieuws/2025/10/06/is-het-internationaal-recht-nog-relevant-na-gaza-we-gaan-een-donker-decennium-tegemoet-a4908607 |archive-date=6 October 2025 |url-status=live |language=nl |trans-title=Is international law still relevant after Gaza? "We are entering a dark decade."}}</ref> The journalist Colin Jones interviewed lawyers affiliated with the US military and concluded that they see Gaza as a test case for what military conduct might be acceptable in a hypothetical war between the US and a peer power such as China.<ref name="Jones 2025"/>
